Ko min tɔ bɛ kɔfɛ, Dirisa Togola - Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ, Sogɛli Kokala Mayiga, n’a ka Kumalaseli minisiri ka bilasirali ye. Mɛtiri Haruna Tureh taara, ntɛnɛndon zuwɛnkalo tile 28 san 2021, Kunnafonidilaw ka soba la, yaasa ka kunnafonidilaw mɔgɔw kunbɛn.
Nin badenyataama la kunnafonidilaw ka soba la, laɲini ye ka kunnafonidilaw kunnafoni cɛmancɛfanga gɔfɛrɛnaman ka baarabolodali fɔlɔlɔw kan, minnu ye dugukolo lakana, politiki ani fangabulonkow yɛlɛmaniw ye, ani hadamadenyako waati madali.
Minisiri ɲɛmɔgɔ y’a kɛ sababu ye ka Jamana Labɛn kura tɔgɔla ɛmɔgɔw jɛya kunnafonidiminɛnw ye.
Ani fana kalataw ɲɛnabɔli cakɛda kelen sigili, min bɛ na segin ka na,
O tun kɛra kunnafonidilaw ka soba perezidan, Banjugu Dante, ɲɛna.
U ka weleli kɔrɔfɔ kɔnɔ, kunnafonidilaw ka soba perezidan, Dante ye gɔfɛrɛnaman hakililatigɛ ni Mali kunnafonidilaw ka bilasirali ye, kasɔrɔ ma sɔrɔ a ma sɔrɔ.
A kɛtɔla ka nin taama nafamafɛ, a ye Mali waleyali ɲɛmɔgɔ minɛ, bisimila, gɛlɛyaw kan, minnu bɛ kunnafonidilaw ka don ɲanamaya la.
Labɛn kura tɛ se ka kɛ kasɔrɔ kunnafonidilaw ka labɛn kura tɛ.
a y’o fɔ.
Ale ka fɔ la, gɛlɛyaw min bɛ Mali kunnafonidisɛbɛnw cɛma, o ye sariya kura ɲangili ye cyberjugubakɛlɛya kan, kunnafonidilaw ka jalatigɛli lajɔliw, kunnafonidilaw ka dɛmɛli kun jɔnjɔn, kabini san saba, lakanako doni minnu tɛ se ka kɛ a yɔrɔ lamagata cakɛdaw kan, minnu yɔrɔ bɛ yɔrɔ la ani kunnafonidilaw ka soba lakurayali ɲini.

Aliyu Badara Jara Giyomu Soro kiri kɔnna ni kasobonba ye Konowari kiri fɛ
Konowari Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ lakodɔnnen k’a jalaki ni ɲinini ye ka Jamana lakanani lataa ɲɛ.
A ka awokati Fusita Banba Lamini, a ka porotokɔli Sulu ɲɛmɔgɔ, depite kɔrɔ Bɛni Suki, bɛ san 20 bɔ u kan.
Min ye Alɛni Lɔbɔnjɔn ye, sɔrɔ Simon ani Risibɛri Soro ani Falicɛbu Sekongo.
u kiri bɔra ni kalo 17 kaso ye k’a sababu kɛ forobakiritigɛli ye.
Kiriko y’a latigɛ fana Giyomu Soro ka politikijɛkulu, Zeneraliw ani fasojamaɲɔgɔndɛmɛw ( ZEPEYƐSI ) cili.
a tɛmɛna kalan kɛ rfi.fr kan. Kumalaselisɛbɛn dɔ kɔnɔ, min bɔra nin wulaɲɔgɔn na, Kolatilenjɛkulu Kɛli Ansar ani Faraɲɔgɔnkanw ye ɲɔgɔnye mɛn sɔrɔ ni nisɔndiya ye dɔgɔkun nin dɔgɔkun Gundamu, ni kɛra fɛn jɔnjɔnw dɔ ye, Tawode marabolo maracɛbɔli koɲɛnabɔli sariyasɛbɛn.
O cogo la, kumalaselisɛbɛn y’o fara a kan, bi, Dawudɛni marabolo ye sɔrɔ belebele ye, min ka kan ka dusu don ani min jamaw ka kan ka bilasira ani k’u kologɛlɛya.
« A ka kan ka kɛ misali ye ani misali ye, min tɔ bɛ kɛ yɔrɔ tɔw la, minnu cɛbɔli tora fɛn ɲuman ye, ka bɛn jamaw ka ŋaniyaw ma.
Sigida mɔgɔ minnu y’a kɛ jamajɛkulu ye, olu ka ca, y’u kɛlɛ kɛ fan bɛɛ fɛ, walasa ka nin marabolo kɛ tiɲɛ ye, min bɛ tɛmɛ politiki mɔgɔw ani faraɲɔgɔnkanw kan », Kolatilenjɛkulu y’o dantigɛ.
Yaan’a k’a fara a kan ko nin dusu don ni cɛsiri, min ka kan ka fara ɲɔgɔn kan fan wɛrɛ fɛ, janko Lakɔnba marabolo, min ɲininkalen don foro bɛɛ kɔnɔ ani min makɔnɔnen bɛ Faguibini taabolo jamaw fɛ ani mɔgɔ caman wɛrɛw.
« A y’a kuncɛ ten cogo min na an ka ciw b’a fɛ cogo min na, an bɛ bɛn hakilinaw bɛɛ bila ɲɔgɔn na ani ka wele bila a latigɛbagaw ni ɲɔgɔn minnu sen bɛ a la ka taa bɛn sira la sigidajama mɔgɔw bɛɛ ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, minnu bɛ mɔgɔw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ bɛnɲini sigili la, n’a m’a to mɔgɔ si bila ɲɔgɔn na »,
Berehima JALO - A koɲɛ fɔlɔ, min lakodɔnna Moti Kirisigiba fɛ, ntɛnɛndon zuwɛnkalo tile 21 san 2021, tun bɛ forobakiritigɛla bila Umaru Gadaga (baga Dɛdugu, Bankasi sɛrikili la) la, min jalakilen bɛ Nuhumu Sidibe ka saya la.
A sɔrɔlen k’a nɔ bɛ kow la, minnu kiri bɔra a la, Umaru Gadiga kiri bɔra a la ni kaso ye.
kow!
A bɛ ye sɛbɛnw kɔnɔ kow nataw bɔ.
Feburuyekalo tile 18, san 2019, Bedugu, Fakalana togodalakomini na, Jene sɛrikili la, sɔgɔmada, Umaru Gadiga taara dugunin dugukolo marago la, k’a to nɔfɛnw fan dɔ la.
Taama kɔnɔ, a ye npogotigi Nuhumu Sidibe, min si bɛ san 13 la, sɔrɔ a ka kalanso kɔnɔ.
Kumafalenw kɔfɛ, minnu tun cɛla u ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, Umaru Gadiga bɛ mankutu caman mara Nuhumu Sidibe la a farikolo yɔrɔ caman fɛ, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la bolow, senw ani kafɛ.
Nuhumu y’a ka joli la a yɔrɔ la.
Umaru tara a balimakɛw fɛ, a fa ka yamaruya kɔrɔ duguninɲɛmɔgɔ ye.
Sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛlɛli kɔfɛ, min lakodɔnna Jene Zandaramaw ka Zandaramaw ka bolofara fɛ, Umaru Gadiga nɔminɛna k’a fɔ u ka faga.
Jalaki bɔra a jalakilen na, a ma gɛlɛya sɔrɔ a jalakilen kow la.
A y’a ɲɛfɔ k’a ye cɛmisɛn Nuhumu Sidibe sɔrɔ u ka kalanso la feburuyekalo tile 18, min, i n’a fɔ a ka laada la, y’a yɛrɛ bila ka ɲagali kɛ a la kasɔrɔ kun tun tɛ se ka kɛ a la.
Wa k’a laban a ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, a y’i gɛrɛ Nuhumu Sidibe la ka mugu ci a la siɲɛ caman ni mankutu min tun bɛ a bolo.
O sɛbɛnni tun bɛ bɔli kɛ yaasa Umaru Gadiga ka jɔyɔrɔtigiya lakɔlɔsi cɛmisɛn Nuhumu Sidibe ka saya la.
Umar nɔgɔrɔla k’a fɔ u ka faga.
Nka, mɔgɔw walima mɔgɔw tun dɛsɛlen don.
O cogo de la, kow tiɲɛna ka kɛ binkanni ye, ka ɲɛsin ɲangilisariya sariyasen 199 ani 201 ma.
K’a da o kan, jalakiw, minnu bɛ bɔli kɛ ka sin Umaru Gadiga ma, bɔli kɛra sababu ye ka se ka Diɲugu, Fakalana togodalakomini komini, Jene sɛrikili la, san 2019 feburukalo tile 18, k’a yɛrɛ di Nuhumu Sidibe ma, kow la, minnu ɲɛsigilen don ani k’u ɲangi ɲangilisariya sariyasenw 199, alisɛbɛn 1 ani 201 fɛ.
Jalaki bɛ jalaki n’a ye kow la, minnu kiri bɔra a la. Kunnafoni bakurubajatew siratigɛ la, jalaki bɛ min kɔnɔnasɛbɛn n° 2 sanfɛ kofɔlen tɛ jalaki si fɔ.
Kunnafoni sɔrɔlenw a ka mɔgɔbaw kanu bɛ a fɛ.
Nka dɔgɔtɔrɔ faamuyalen, min kɛra k’a ka hakilina faamuyali kɛ, a ka san 2019 desanburukalo tile 11 laselisɛbɛn kɔnɔ, ko fisika walima hakilina tiɲɛni si t’a la, min bɛ bɔ a ka ɲangali jɔyɔrɔtigiya la.
Nin kunw na, kiritigɛlaw ye murutili nɔfɛ kow tiɲɛtigiya ani k’a dantigɛ ko labɛnnen ka bɔli kɛ k’a ɲɛsin mɔgɔ jalakilen Umaru Gadiga ma, k’a ɲɛsin kow tiɲɛtigiya ma.
Kiritigɛla y’a jira k’a fɔ k’a bila jalaki la Moti kirisigiba ɲɛkɔrɔ.
Bɔlɔn kɔnɔ, ntɛnɛn zuwɛnkalo tile 21 san 2021, Umaru Gadiga, min ma cɛsiri sɔrɔ, jɔra a kow la, minnu tun kiri bɔra a la, n’a ye baara gɛlɛya o la a ka awoka, Mɛtiri Simɔni Legu, ye.
A maramafɛntigi kɛlen a la, ale tun ma sugandili wɛrɛ sɔrɔ mɔgɔ wɛrɛ de ye k’a ɲini Kiribulonba fɛ.
Bawo, a ka kuma fɔlenw na, Umaru Gadiga t’a hakili dafabaliya la.
« Ne ka mɔgɔlafasata bɛ sɔrɔ, a t’a hakili dafabaliyaw fa.
A hakili dafalen tɛ.
A kɛlen kɔ a kow la, minnu kiri bɔra a la, n bɛ barikada ani fɛn minnu b’a lafisaya », a y’o dantigɛ.
Nka forobakiritigɛla ye kɔlɔsiliw tiɲɛn, k’a sɛmɛntiya ko jalakilen b’a ka se bɛɛ la ani ko a ka waleya ɲɛbilala.
A y’a fɔ ni kow labɛnni kura tɛ dɔwɛrɛ ye.
Mɛtiri Legu ka laɲiniw ma lamɛn kiriso fɛ, min y’a jira k’a fɔ ko Umaru Gadaga jalaki bɛ a la ni k’a ɲangi ni kaso ye.
Siyaka Dunbiya - Ciden kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen Seware - Sebaga saba, ntolatan caman na, celu wolonwila donnen, jaabi si tɛ sɔrɔ.
Ni nin bakurubajate ye, siga t’a la, Litali tun ye nin Euro 2020 ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw cɛɲi dɔ ye.
Fo ka se hakɛ la, jama caman tun bɛ Jamana mɔgɔ minnu bɛ se ka taa yɔrɔ jan na ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw kɔnɔ.

Gɛlɛya kɔnɔ ( 2 – 1 ).
Sɛgɛsɛli kun ye.
Sɛgɛsɛgɛlikɛla Zenerali ( BEWEZE ) ka nin sɛgɛsɛgɛli bɛ tali kɛ baaraw ɲɛnabɔli la, minnu kɛra Sibi togoda yɛrɛmarakafo fɛ, waati kɔnɔ, k’a ta zanwiye tile 1 san 2017 la ka taa desanburukalo tile 31 san 2019.
A laɲini ye ka hakililatigɛ ko Sibi yɛrɛmarakofo ( SEYƐRIYƐSI ) bɛ ka mara ni sɔrɔko, nafasɔrɔ ni kɛcogo ɲuman saratiw ye ani ka bɛn sariyaw ani baarabɛnkanw ma, minnu bɛ senna.
Sɛgɛsɛgɛli baaraw kɛra sababu ye kɔnɔkow kɔlɔsili, marakɛcogo, nafoloko ani jatebɔli marakɛcogo, so ani dugukolo marakɛcogo, fasodenya marakɛcogo, baarakɛjama marakɛcogo, faamuyako marakɛcogo an’a jama ka sebagaya kokɛtaw.
Fan dɔ fɛ, BEVEZE ka ci ye bolonkɔnijaasere kɔlɔsili jɔnjɔnw ye, bilasiraliw don minnu na k’a to se ka lafisaya ani fan wɛrɛ fɛ, ka hakili da nafoloko kɛcogoya juguw kan, ka bɔ majɛliw la minnu bɛ kɛ sariyaw ni baarabɛnkanw labɛnw na.
BEVEZE ka laɲiniw, walasa ka mara kɛcogoya juguw latilen.
Sibi togoda yɛrɛmarakafo komini ka kolatigɛjɛkulu ka kan :
ka baarakɛjɛkulu sigilenw lataamacogo hakililatigɛ.
Sibi togoda yɛrɛmarakafo « mɛri » ka kan ka :
forobana ka marako seginni la, ka bɛn sariyaw ma, minnu bɛ senna.
ka Komini ka sebagaya jateminɛ kɛ, waati bɛɛ,
ka baarakɛnafolo jɛlenya taabolo labato,
ka wari sɔrɔlenw mara sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛ ka bɛn baarasariya ma, min bɛ senna.
ka Sibi dugu an’a laminiw dugubakɔnɔni ɛmɔgɔba Sɛbɛn bila sen kan.
Ka so jɔlenw ani jɔlenw fara ɲɔgɔn kan minnu ka kan ka bɔ yɔrɔmarakafo la ani ka fɛɛrɛw kɛ u donni kama yɔrɔmarakafo la.
K ‘a hakili to fasodensɛbɛnw gafew datuguli n’u lajɔli la san bɛɛ desanburukalo tile 31 don.
ka forobabaarakɛla jatebɔ ani ka taaɲɛ kɛ, ka bɛn baarasariya ma, min bɛ senna.
Ka hakililatigɛ ko yɔrɔw-yɔrɔw baaraw kɛyɔrɔ ka bɛn baarasariya ma min bɛ senna.
ka jɛkuluw sigi, ka kɛɲɛ ni sɛbɛnw ye minnu bɛ senna, taabolow ani baaradenw sɔrɔli tuma na.
Kati kubeda « kumandanba » ka kan :
ka dantigɛliw gafew ani fasodenya gafew kɛlɛli ye.
Filɛlikɛla ka kan :
ka Sibi togoda yɛrɛmarakafo an’a ka taabolo bɛɛ lakodɔn ka kɛɲɛ ni taabolo jɔyɔrɔw ye.
ka wari sɔrɔlenw mara sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛ ka bɛn baarasariya ma, min bɛ senna.
Nafoloko kɔlɔsilikɛla ka kan :
ka Komini ka nafoloko cogoya bakurubaw laselisɛbɛnw kɛ.
Sibi yɛrɛmarakafo Wariladonnenw Musakatigi ka kan :
ka kɔlɔsili kɛ ɲɔgɔn kan min wajibiyalen don baarasariya fɛ, min bɛ senna.
Sibi yɛrɛmarakafo Wariladonnenw Musakatigi ka kan :
ka kɔlɔsili kɛ ɲɔgɔn kan min wajibiyalen don baarasariya fɛ, min bɛ senna.
Nafolo kɛcogoya juguw.
Nafolo kɛcogoya juguw hakɛ bakuruba, min bɛ nin duguma na, bɛ ta i jɔ sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 27 130 (miliyon mugan ni naani ani naani ani naani ani naani ani naani ani naani ani naani ani naani ani naani ani naani ani naani ani naani ani naani ani naani ani naani ani naani ani naani ani naani ) ma.
WALEYAW LATƐMƐNI AN’U KOFƐLI KIRITIGƐBULONBA JATEBƐGƐLIKƐBULONBA MA SƐGƐSƐGƐSƐGƐLIKƐLABA FƐ ANI JAMANA LAFASASARIYATIGI MIN BƐ BAMAKO DISITIRIKI KOMINI III WARIKOKIRISO LA, Sɔrɔ ani Nafoloko DONI BƐ MIN BƐ MIN K’A BƐN.
Musakaw kɛcogoya juguw yamaruyalenw ma, ka se se sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 1 022 830 (miliyon kelen ani ba kɛmɛ segin ni bi saba) ma.
wari sɔrɔlenw kɛcogoya juguw la, ka se se sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 24 400 (miliyon mugan ni naani ani ba kɛmɛ ni naani ani kɛmɛ naani ani kɛmɛ naani ani kɛmɛ naani ) ma.
wari hakɛ minnu ma ɲɛfɔ, ka se bakuruba la sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 1 159 900 ( miliyon kelen ani ba kɛmɛ ni bi duuru ni kɔnɔntɔn ni kɛmɛ kɔnɔntɔn ) ma.
Sibi yɛrɛmarakafo marako sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛlen bɛ baaraɲɔgɔnya kɔnɔ, Sɛgɛsɛgɛlikɛla Zenerali Cakɛda Cakɛda ani Erɔpu kelenyatɔn cidenkulu Mali la cɛ.
A b’a ɲini k’a hakililatigɛ ko dugubakɔnɔkow ani dugubakɔnɔkow, bakuruba la ani Sibi ta, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, b’u ka jɔyɔrɔw an’u ka jɔyɔrɔtigiyaw laboli la, desantaralizasyɔn bilali la sen kan ani k’o kɛ, ka bɛn baarasariya ma, min bɛ senna.
Kunnafoni caman kama.
NET_RAPP_CR_DE_pdf (bvg-mali.org). U filɛlikɛla ba tan caman tun don, latɔmɔnenw koɲuman ka fara ɲɔgɔn kan « Canannimɛni » fɛrɛba kan Siniwajamana na, alamisadon zuluye tile 1ɔlɔ.
U wɔyɔtɔla bandari bekebele tɛmɛni na, min donnen don helikɔpitɛri kelen fɛ, ani k’a masiri ni wɔlɔsɔ ni mantaraka ye, u tun nana Siniwaw ka Kominisi Tɔnba ka san kɛmɛ ɲɛnajɛ ɲɛnamɛya.
Wa, ni pankurujɛkulu dayɛlɛla tun bɛ i n’a fɔ taamasiyɛn tun tɛ se ka jɛya bilen.
Pariti min bɛ fanga la kabini 1949 fanga la, kasɔrɔ a ma deli kɛ abada, a bɛ fɛ ka to Siniwajamana ɲɛmɔgɔya la.
A ko ye sababu ye Siniwaw ka fanga kama k’a ka koɲɛw jira, kabini a sigili la k’a kɛ sariyasɔsɔ ye zuluyekalo la san 1921, Shanghai, Faransi cɛmancɛlafanga kɔnɔ.
Ni perezidan Sisi Jinpingi ka kɔrɔfɔ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye, mɔgɔ welelen bɛ min kɔnɔ.
Fanga belebele seginna ka kɛ, Siniwajamana tɛna yɛrɛ bɔ jamana tɔw fɛ, i n’a fɔ tilebinyanfan koloniyali waati la walima Japo wulikajɔ (1931 – 1945 ).
San caman kama, Siniwaw ka fanga, jamaw ɲɛnabɔli faamuyalen, ye alamisa belebele ye.
Bandari ka sonyali kɔfɛ, jateden 100 jira sankolo la, k’a kɛ helikopitɛri bi saba ɲɔgɔnna fɛ.
Kɛlɛkɛlɛkanw bɛ da u kan, o kɔfɛ akorobatiki mɔgɔw bɛ ɲɛjugu da Sino faaba sanfɛ.
A kɛtɔla k’a kɛ Mao ka fangaɲɔgɔn ye, Siniwajamana kelen-kelen tɔgɔlamɔgɔ sigilen bɛ nin yɛrɛ-yɛrɛ-yɛrɛ-yɛrɛ-yɛrɛ-yɛrɛ-yɛrɛ-yɛrɛ-yɛrɛ-yɛrɛ-yɛrɛ-yɛrɛ-yɛrɛ kan, yaasa k’a ka fanga sigi.
O bɛɛ kɛtɔla ka fanga sigibaga ka politikimɔgɔw sɔrɔdasi miliyon kɔnɔn mɔgɔ minnu sɔrɔlen do (Garadɔn Bɔnd ɲɛ fɛ, dɔnko-dɔnko-dɔnko-dɔnko) walima 1989 demokarasi kɔnɔna wulikajɔw kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen na nin jɔyɔrɔ kelen na Zanimɛni.
PeSeSe « sekeretɛri zenerali » y’a ka kɔrɔfɔ daminɛ ni kumakan ni giriman ye.
Tɔɲɔgɔnw, teri teriw?
A b’a ka kuma cɛsiri ni « kominisiw » ka ko kɛlenw ye, ka hakililatigɛ ko « marikisisimu » bɛ to jamana bereminɛkala ye, sɔrɔko yɛlɛma jɔnjɔnw n’u ta bɛɛ kabini san 40, sɔrɔ sugufiyɛ sɔrɔli kosɔn.
A kɔrɔfɔ kuntaala bɛ ka tɛmɛ ɲɔgɔn kan.
Mɔgɔ minnu wulila su kɔnɔ yaasa ka na ɲɛnajɛ kɛ ani ka tɛmɛ lakɔlɔsili yɔrɔ caman fɛ, a bɛ i n’a fɔ u y’i yɛrɛ bɔ a yɛrɛ la.
O bɛɛ n’a ta, perezidan b’a dɔn tuma min a b’a kan k’a kumakanw kɛ.
Waati bɛ ka wuli wa sɔgɔ bɛ ka na.
Mɔgɔw bɛ ɲɛfɛ, i n’a fɔ cɛ dɔwɛrɛ, ɲugu durɔn, min dira u ma.
Sun bɛ segin k’a kɔrɔfɔ laban na, k’a sɔrɔ Diɲɛmɔgɔw ka jɛnsɛn, yann’a kɛ bolonkɔni caman ani bolola caman bɔli ye ɲɛ.
U kɛtɔla k’a kanu bɛɛ ɲɔgɔn na, jama bɛ fara ɲɔgɔn na ni ka jama ka kanu Ode ka taa faso kanu la.
Cɛni san 25, min bɛ ban k’a tɔgɔ fɔ, k’a fɔ k’a nisɔndiyalen don ɲɛnajɛ fɛ, k’a da a kan a ka pariti tɔnden don kabini san kelen durɔn.
N jigi bɛ k’a fɔ ko n bangera an ka waati la.
A ko ten Faransi – Pɛrɛsi Cakɛda ma.
Duguba jama ka jiidili gɛlɛya, min ɲɔgɔn ma boloda, ye gɛlɛya sɔrɔ sirabakanboli siratigɛ la.
N’a ta bɛɛ, bugɔli 3 ye ba kɛnɛ kan, ka bɔ ba kɛrɛnɛ kan ni dugu cɛmancɛ ye, o ye barikada ye.
Hali ni Koɲɛw Cɛmancɛ de tɛ Bamakɔ la, dugu cɛmancɛ, sɛbɛnkankɛnɛ kan, bɛ mara caman bɔ.
Kɛrɛfɛjɔw jagoyalen don ka bɔ ba kɛrɛfɛjɔ la wa o ye tiɲɛni yɛrɛ de ye sɔgɔmada ka taa wula fɛ.
K’a daminɛ sɔgɔmada nɛgɛkanɲɛ 6 fanfɛ, Bamakɔ – Senu pankurujigidenkalankɛnɛ siratigɛ taaraw la.
Mɔgɔ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw ka mobili, cakɛda taamaw, sen saba, takisiw, motow..., b’u ka miiriya k’u ka tɛmɛsiraw sɔrɔ.
Tiɲɛ don, dusukasi bɛ kɛ ka ye.
Lamini Jere, Sotarama sofɛri ka fɔ la.
nin basigiw b’u yɔrɔ sɔrɔ polisi dɔw jogo juguw la, minnu, k’a sɔrɔ ka taabolo ɲɛnabɔ, bɛ ɲankataabagaw lagosi.
Fɔdasi jɔsen bolodalen don ni tɛmɛsira ye.
O bɛɛ n’a ta, o tɛmɛsira bɛ kɛ fana motobolilaw fɛ, o tɛ ɲɛnabɔcogo si to pewu.
Yiriwali dugu cɛmancɛ la ye kɛnɛkanko ye.
Alu Tarawore, lafasalikɛla, ka fɔ la, gɛlɛya kunw bɛ Bamakɔ sirabakanboli la, n’u bɛ ɲɛfɔ, dɔwɛrɛw cɛla, polisi dɔw jogo fɛ, sirakanboliw gɛlɛya, mototakisiw.
ɛmɔgɔw ka kan ka kokɛta dɔw ta walasa ka sirabakanboli lanɔgɔya.
A ko ten.
Kalabani – Kura – Dabanani ( dugu cɛmancɛ ) taabolo bɛ an kan ka tɛmɛ ɲɛ kelen kan.
Fulamini Aminata Goyita, nsonw feerekɛla Wɔnida sugu la.
Polisi lasidan, Jakaridi Jara, b’a jate ko: Polisiw ka maganw n’u ta bɛɛ, sirabakanboli sariyaw labato, taamabaga dɔw b’a ɲini k’a baara gɛlɛya u la.
O bɛ mɔgɔ juguya sɔrɔ sirabakan na tuma dɔw la.
Sirabakanna yɛlɛmana n’a ta bɛɛ, min ɲininen don ka sirabakanna lanɔgɔya Bamakɔ, gɛlɛyaw bɛ sɔrɔ u ka tilebinyanfan sigibagaw bolo tuguni u ka sɛgɛsɛgɛ ka sɛgɛsɛgɛ ka sɛgɛsɛgɛ ka sɛgɛsɛgɛ ka sɛgɛsɛgɛ ka sɛgɛsɛgɛ ka sɛgɛsɛgɛ la.
Dugukolo wɛrɛ mago bɛ ye min bɛ ye Bamakɔ, Nizɛri ba kɔnɔ.
Inza Tarawore (baraminɛkalanden) - Hamani angi ka kɔkɔrɔdonjɛkulu y’a soronadon ko, zuwɛnkalo tile 29, kunnafonilajɛ dɔ senfɛ, a ka ɲɛmɔgɔ nkalontigiya kosɔn, a koɲɛ na a bɛ fɔ min ma ko « diyagoya kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini Mali basikɛtiboli federason ye ».
A bɛ lagali bisigikumaw kofɔ Hamani angi juguya la, a kɛtɔla k’a ka kɔkɔrɔdon, min tɛ dɔn ka ban, Kayi ka denbaya ma.
Nin waati gɛlɛn kɔnɔ an bɛ ka minɛ, n’a y’a kɛ siratigɛ dɔ ye, an bɛ ɲɛcogoya min kɔnɔ bi, Mali basikɛti de ye.
Anw ye ŋanadanw ye fan bɛɛ la, ɲɛmɔgɔw ka dusu kɔnɔ, Hamani angi bɛ minnu cɛla.
Ka tɛmɛ a kan ka kɛ Mali basikɛtiboli federason perezidan ye, ka tɛmɛ a kan ka kɛ Farikoloɲɛnajɛw minisiri ye, a ka laɲiniw fɛ, nin Kayi jamana ye Mali darapo lase kosɛbɛ, fɔlɔ la Afiriki ( FIBA Afiriki ) la, o kɔfɛ diɲɛ basikɛti sanfɛjɔba, FIBA diɲɛ ta la.
A ka kan ka bilasira, ka kɔkɔrɔdon.
Yusufu Sidibe, Hamani angi ka kɔkɔrɔdon Jɛkulu mɔgɔ dɔ y’o fɔ.
A ka kuma fɔlenw na, ni Hamani angi bɛ gɛlɛya la, Kayi bɛɛ de bɛ gɛlɛya la, i ko Mali ani Afiriki bɛɛ kama.
K’a da a kan, a y’a jira k’a fɔ ko Mali de bɛ indexed bi, Mali de bolonkɔni bɛ min kɔnɔ wa Afiriki fana de b’a i ko ale ka tɔgɔ bɛ ɲɔgɔn fɛ nin bisigikumaw fɛ.
bisigikumaw, k’a da a kan an bɛ sɛgɛsɛgɛliw, minnu bɛ senna, mara ani kiri danfaralenw jaabiw makɔnɔni na.
ɛnamɛya bɛɛ ka kɛ nin bisigikumaw kan, tiɲɛnni kama.
Yusufu Sidibe y’o fɔ.
Sɛgɛsɛgɛli caman wɛrɛw kɔfɛ Mali basikɛtiboli federason perezidan kɔrɔ kan, lajɛba, Ba Kone, ye Malidenw wele k’o ko in ta bolo la walasa ka Hamani angi ka jalaki seereya.
Burama Kamara - O dusukunnako de ye baarakɛkulu mɔgɔw nisɔndiya sisan, Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kura, Sogɛli K. Mayiga ka taama kɔfɛ Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Bubu Sise, minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ dafɛ.
Mɔgɔw b’a sɔrɔ Sogɛli ka nin latigɛli la k’a bɔ Bubu la.
Mɔgɔw b’a jate ko Sogɛli yɛrɛ ye Bubu marakɛcogo jugu bila sen fɛ wa a yɛrɛ kɛlɛ k’a la fo ka fanga sɔrɔ.
A ma kɛ sababu ye ka nɛgɛ da a koɲɛ kan, u bolo, Sogɛli ma mago bubu ka koɲɛnabɔliw sɔrɔ abada.
Olu laban bɛ k’u miiri ko bololabaara durɔn de bɛ yen.
U dalen b’a la ko nin taama tun ka kɛ ka ɲɛsin Bubu ma, w’o tɛ foyi wɛrɛ fɛ.
Mɔgɔ tun bɛ se hali k’a dɔn a ɲɔgɔnkunbɛ ja kan ko Sogɛli y’i gɛlɛya k’i ye kɛ mɔgɔ nisɔndiyalen ni laɲuman ye, mɔgɔ dɔ y’o ɲɛfɔ.
Nka barokɛyɔrɔ la, u bɛɛ miiri k’a fɔ ko Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ ka kan ka nin sɛrikɛ minɛ yaasa ka taa baara la joona bawo, waati caman t’a bolo tugun.
Ibarahima Ɛdiayi - Fɛnw ko don, i n’a fɔ sogo, tulo, sɔrɔ, nɔnɔ, malo.
Kabini waati dɔ la, an ɲɛ bɛ magoɲɛfɛn fɔlɔw sɔngɔ yɛlɛnni kɛ ka caya Mali sugu kan.
O bɛ kɛ, gɔfɛrɛnaman ka maganw kɛli n’u ta bɛɛ, magoɲɛfɛn fɔlɔw basigili ani k’u damakɛɲɛ kɛ, yaasa Mali sannikɛlaw ka nin magoɲɛfɛn belebelew sɔrɔ sɔngɔ bɛ minnu na, ni k’u dɛmɛ kɛtɔla.
Nka, o n’a ta bɛɛ, jagokɛla dɔw, minnu y’u kan k’u ka sɔngɔw yɛlɛn, b’u yɛrɛ bila.
Ka sin nin ko cogoya ma, kumalasesɛbɛn dɔ kɔnɔ, min bɔra dɔgɔkun tɛmɛnen, gɔfɛrɛnaman, ka tɛmɛ DEZESEYƐSI fɛ, jɔlen don ka jama hakililatigɛ k’a bɛ baara kɛ kasɔrɔ a bɛ fanga sabati.
O cogo de la, magoɲɛfɛn belebele dɔw sɔngɔn yɛlɛmana, a ye kunnafoni di.
Kunnafoni cikan lasera cogo min, o sannayɛlɛma sɔngɔw labatoli, minnu bɛ se ka kɛ dugukolo fan bɛɛ fɛ, bɛ to wajibi ye bɛɛ kama.
Walasa k’o sɔngɔw kɛcogoya lakɔlɔsi, DEZESEYƐSI ka kumalasesɛbɛn bɛ sannikɛlaw kunnafoni ko a ka kɔlɔsilikɛuluw bɛ kɛnɛ kan, yaasa k’u lakana ka bɔ damatɛmɛliw la, minnu sirilen don jagoko ɲɛfɔliw la.
O gɔfɛrɛnaman ka magan, min bɛ ta ka taa sɔngɔw kannabila taabolo kan, min bɛ ta sariyasɛbɛnw fɛ, minnu bɛ jagoko ɲɛnabɔ Mali jamana kɔnɔ, bɛ ka ɲɛ, a y’o ɲɛfɔ.
Yaan’a ka sannikɛlaw wele ka sɔsɔli ko bɛɛ kɛli dantigɛ Minisiriɲɛ, Dunni ani  ɲɔgɔndan ɛmɔgɔyasoba cakɛdaw fɛ.
AMTure - Perezidan Emaniyɛli Makoron b’a bagabagali k’a bɛ bɔ Mali la n’a ka jamakuluw ye.
K’a sɔrɔ latigɛlisɛbɛn ka se ka waleya
O de fɔlen bɛ ntɛnɛndon tɛmɛnen kumafalen na Kolonɛli Asimi Goyita ni Faransi ciden kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw cɛ.
Makɔnɔyako ( walima makɔnɔyako walima makɔnɔyako ) ye politiki hakilililako ye, min bɛ kɛ ka politikimɔgɔ ani Faransi Jamana perezidan, Emaniyɛli Makɔrɔn, mankutuluw caman jateminɛ, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, minnu fɔra forobabaaraw senfɛ.
Mali Cɛmancɛlafanga perezidan, Kolonɛli Asimi Goyita, filɛ ka
Makɔnɔdaw.
O cogo la, mɛkalo tile 24 fangadafili kɔfɛ Mali la, Faransi perezidan Emaniyɛli Makoron tun ye a ka ŋaniya ta ka Barikani sɔrɔdasiw senbɔ jamana kɔnɔ.
Kumaɲɔgɔnya dɔ la Karidon kunnafonidisɛbɛn ( ZEDEYƐDEDE ) la, Faransi perezidan tun b’a sɛmɛntiya ko Faransi bɛna a jamakuluw senbɔ n’a y’a sɔrɔ Mali bɛ na « silamɛya ɲumanba » ta la, Jamana cunnen filanan kɔ jamana kɔnɔ kalo kɔnɔntɔn kɔnɔ.
Faransi, a tun y’o fɔ, ni mɔgɔ 5 100 ɲɔgɔnna ye Barikani kɔnɔ, bɛ Mali kɔkɔrɔdon, min bɛ ka ɲɛsin kɛra kaɲaka fan dɔ ma kabini san 2012 ni k’a ye jamana cunnen lakanako gɛlɛya kɔnɔ, yann’a ka taa jamana cɛmancɛ la.
Wa Makɔrɔn, i n’a fɔ EU, ka « jamana gɔfɛn min tɛ sɔn ka bɔ » kofɔ perezidan Ba Njadu ani Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ Mukutari Wani ka minɛni kɔfɛ.
Jɔlen tɛ?
An ka tɔgɔ!
K’a bɔ a la, ntɛnɛdon tɛmɛnen, i n’a fɔ Mali cɛ kologɛlɛn kura tigiɲɔgɔn fɔlɔ b’a sɛmɛntiya cogo min, Emanuyɛli Makoron ye cidenkulu dɔ bila ka taa Asimi Goyita la.

Anw ye kumafalenw kɛ cɛsiriko kan, minnu sirilen bɛ kɛlɛli la kɛlɛli la kɛlɛli la kɛlɛli la kɛlɛli la kɛlɛli la kɛlɛli la ani Sahɛli basigi.

Makɔrɔnɔn y’a masurunnakɔrɔw wele Asimi Goyita ma k’a fɔ ko ale fagala wa?
Misali la, walasa a ka hakilijigin kɛ fɔli dɔw la, i n’a fɔ nin.
« Mali perezidan Ba Ndaw kan, min tun cɛsirilen don kosɛbɛ fanga ni jihadikɛlaw cɛ, ne tun y’o fɔ.
« Silamɛyako ɲagali Mali la an ka sɔrɔdasiw an ka kɛnɛ kan wa?
Gɛlɛya abada!’ Nin ɲagali bɛ Mali la bi.
Nka n’o bɛ ɲɛ o siratigɛ la, n bɛna senbɔ ».
Faransi jamana kuntigi tun y’a sɛmɛntiya o tuma k’ale « ka kibaruya lase » Farafina Tilebinya ɲɛmɔgɔw ma ko ale « tɛna to jamana kɛrɛfɛ demokarasi sariyasɔsɔ ni cɛmancɛlafanga t’a la bilen ».
A bɛ hakilijigin kɛ k’a fɔ, kabini san saba, « Kɔfɛjɔkulu caman kɔnɔ, an tun ka kan k’an miiri min na bɔli la ».
Munna Makoron, min tun tɛ fɛ ka to jamana kɔnɔ min ka demokarasi sariyasɔsɔnya bɛ min kɔnɔ.
y’i gɛlɛya kosɛbɛ ka misira mɔgɔw tali kɛ yen minnu ka ca ni belebele ye, i n’a fɔ Faranki Pari ani Amirali Zan Filipu Rɔlɔni?
Pari bɛ siran min kan?
K’a bɔ walima a ka bagabagali k’a bɔ jamana na, a sirilen don min na, a tɔɔrɔlen bɛ min na.
An y’a jira k’a fɔ ko Parisi bɛ fɛ ka jate fo ka se tan yann’a ka walisiw dilan.
O nɔ na, Makɔrɔnɔn y’a jira k’a fɔ ko an bɛ ɲini ka na ni 8 ni 9 ye.
Kasɔrɔ Asimi Goyita bɛ to silamɛ ani madali la halibi.
o tɛ k’a ɲinɛ k’a miiri ko foyi si tɛ mago bɛ kɛnɛ kan, hali ni... a teri bɛɛ la ɲuman walima a jɛɲɔgɔnjugu!
Burɔni DE SEGBEDIZI - Ka degelikalanɲɛmɔgɔ dɔ labɛn, ɲɛnabɔli la ani waatiw yɛlɛmaniw kɛlɛli la, o de ye tile 10 baaradenya laɲini ye, min bɛ kɛ Segu.
Mɔgɔ bi saba ɲɔgɔnna bɛ minnu bɛ bɔ Segu kalan Akademi, Jamana Kalanyɔrɔ, Kalanyɔrɔkalan ani Dɔnko ɲinini baaradaba cɛmancɛlafanga cɛmancɛlafanga cɛmancɛlafanga cɛmancɛlafanga cɛmancɛlafanga cɛmancɛlafanga cɛmancɛlafanga cɛmancɛlafanga cɛmancɛlafanga cɛmancɛlafanga cɛmancɛlafanga la.
Sigida yiriwali laɲiniw ɲɛsɔrɔli galabu kɔnɔ, Mali Jamana gɔfɛrɛnaman ye Porodekɛ ka sɛgɛrɛ filanan ta, min labɛnna koɲuman, tilenniya ani sen bɛ min na, kalan ɲuman kama mɔgɔ bɛɛ kama.
Jamana kalan minisiriso ni IYƐNISKO ka dɛmɛ ye, ye kurikunɛbɛnw yɛlɛmali baaraboloda caman wuli, degelikaramɔgɔw dilanyɔrɔw ani baarakɛlaw degeli, min sirilen don kalanni na, ɲɛnabɔli ani waatiw yɛlɛmani kɛlɛli la.
Kuluw sugandili kɔfɛ, nin baarakɛyɔrɔ bɛ fɛ ka kɛ hukumu kɛrɛfɛla dilani kama, yaasa k’a faamuya ka ɲɛ ani k’a waleya ɲumanw la, yaasa ka lasigidenw kɛ mɔgɔw ye waati yɛlɛmani kɛlɛli la.
Nin tile 10 baaradanin bɛ bila Kalanso kologɛlɛya baarabolodali kɔnɔ, k’a kɛ Waati yɛlɛmaniw ɛgɛnni an’u kɛlɛli falenni ye.
Nin baarabolodali caman ka laɲini ye, bakuruba la, ka sigi lakɔli kɔnɔ, ka tɛmɛ kalanw bolodalen fɛ, lamini min na denmisɛn bɛɛna se ka kalan, yaasa ka jogoɲumanyaw ta, minnu bɛ ɲɛsin waati yɛlɛmani ma ani kɛlɛli ma, n’u kɛcogoya.
A ka kuma dayɛlɛli kɔrɔfɔ kɔnɔ, Jamana kalan minisiri Sekeretɛri zenerali tɔgɔlamɔgɔ ye wele kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la a mɔgɔ minnu sen bɛ a la k’u cɛsiri k’o baara sugandili kɛ ka ɲɛ.
nin kunnafoniɲɛmɔgɔ ka kan ka kɛ cogoya kosɛbɛ wa laɲiniw bɛ kɛ ka kɛlɛ daminɛ ni waati yɛlɛmaliw sirilenw kɛlɛli taabolo ye, ka tɛmɛ kalan na ani kalanw kɛliw fɛ.
A y’a kuncɛ ten.
Madamu Diko Umaru Diko min bɛ ɲɛsin IYƐNISKO la dɔnniyaw ni kɛnɛyako baarabolodaliw jɔli bɛ min bolo, y’a sinsin IYƐNISKO bilasirali kan Mali gɔfɛrɛnaman fɛ, a ka waati yɛlɛmani kɛlɛli baaraw la, min bɛ diɲɛ bɛɛ bagabagali kɛ.
Alɛbɛri Kalambiri - Koladilanjɛkulu Segu la, min labɛnna zuwɛnkalo tile 24 ka taa tile 27 la Denmisɛnw ani farikoloɲɛnajɛw layiriwali Tɔn (APJS) fɛ, a farikoloɲɛnajɛ lajɛba tako duuruna, min kɛra farikoloɲɛnajɛ nafaw kan.
yiriwali, hɛrɛ ani mɔgɔw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ bɛn.
ani k’a farikoloɲɛnajɛ federasonw ani farikoloɲɛnajɛ tɔnw danfaralenw fara ɲɔgɔn kan, a y’a ka lahidukanw bɛɛ labato.
A bilalen Jamana cɛmancɛlafanga ɲɛmɔgɔ, Kolonɛli Asimi Goyita, ka ɲɛmɔgɔya kɔnɔ, ani min bɛ denmisɛnw ani farikoloɲɛnajɛw minisiri bolo, fasodenyakalan ani fasodenya ɲuman jɔli bɛ min bolo, Mosa Agi Atahɛri, ka san 2021 zuwɛnkalo tile 24 ka taa tile 27 la, farikoloɲɛnajɛ lajɛrɛ tako 5nan na, jamana federason caman, farikoloɲɛnajɛ tɔnw fara ɲɔgɔn kan Bamakɔ.

Nin san, nin ɲɔgɔnyeba don ni baara caman ye, i n’a fɔ :
basikɛti ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw 3×3, Maracanya, galabu ntolatan kelen, kɛlɛdenw, farikoloɲɛnajɛw faraɲɔgɔnkanjɛkuluw ani farikoloɲɛnajɛ jɛkuluw fɛ, ntolatankɛnɛw taama, degelikalankuluw fɛ, kɛlɛdenw ka su, lafiya ntolatankɛnɛ Kulukɔrɔ marabolo kɔnɔ, ɲɔgɔye ni denmisenw ye minnu bolila ka bɔ amana.
A daminɛna farikoloɲɛnajɛw faraɲɔgɔnkanjɛkuluw ani farikoloɲɛnajɛw faraɲɔgɔnkanjɛkuluw fɛ, nin ɲɔgɔnyeba dayɛli ɲɛnajɛ, jumadon zuwɛnkalo tile 24 farikoloɲɛnajɛ masaso la, Salamatu Mayiga, ɲangira kɛra, k’a bɛn u kelen-kelen ma, komini 4nan mɛri ka kɔrɔfɔw fɛ ani diɲɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛ kan ɲɔgɔnkanjɛkulu ( FIYƐSI ) kolatilenna, Mmu Si Aminata Maku Tarawore.
Si ka fɔ la, farikoloɲɛnajɛ jɔda bɛ to senkan na, min kama mɔgɔ bɛ kalan don o don, laadala ani diinɛ fan bɛɛ fɛ.
Ko nin lajɛba laɲini ye ka hakilijakabɔ, hakilijakabɔ ani kumafalenw sigi nɔgɔyadaw kan, farikoloɲɛnajɛ bɛ minnu di Mali sɔrɔko ani hadamadenyako jiidili taabolo kɔnɔ.
A ka fɔ la, FIS ye kɔkanna ɲɔgɔye ye fariloloɲɛjɛ kunkan Mali la, min bɛ APJS kɛwalen fɛɛrɛw bolodalen na, minnu ka laɲini ye kalan ɲuman sɔrɔ, furakɛli ɲuman ani hɛrɛ bɛɛ ka kɛnɛ kan, yaasa ka fɛɛrɛ ɲumanw sigi Mali la walasa ka Diɲɛmɔgɔw ka yiriwali kuntaala jan na ( OEDE ) la.
FIS kolatilennamuso ka kɔrɔfɔ kɛlen kɔ kɔfɛ, jama ye hakɛ sɔrɔ kɛlɛdasiɲɛmɔgɔw ka kofɔliw la, minnu bilala a tɔgɔɲɔgɔn danfaralenw ka kɛɲɛ ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, i n’a fɔ IYƐMUYƐSI, IYƐNISƐFU, IYƐNISƐFU, adw.
Nin FIS tako duuruna tako bɔli jɔnjɔn dira Denmisɛnw ani Farikoloɲɛnajɛw minisiri fɛ, Fasodenyakalan ani fasodenya jɔli bɛ min bolo, Mosa AƐGI Atahɛri.
Jɔnni bɛn’a fɔ ko nin lajɛba ye hakilila ɲuman ye sisan cogoya kɔnɔ an ka jamana bɛ min na bawo a bɛ lafiya hakilina kofɔ ni farikoloɲɛnajɛ ye, ni ka ɲɛnabɔcogow ɲɛfɔli ye kɛbagaw ye, yaasa farikoloɲɛnajɛ ka kɛ lafiya moto yɛrɛ ye, min ɲininen don kosɛbɛ Mali denw bɛɛ fɛ.
O kosɔn, a ye foli kɛ a ka foro latigɛbagaw fɛ, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnneya la Si Aminata Kaku Tarawore.
Minisiri Agi Atahari ka fɔ la, nin tako bɛ na kɛnɛ kan ka caya farikoloɲɛnajɛ tɔn kɛbagaw ye, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la farikoloɲɛnajɛ federasonw ani tɔnw.
K’a da a kan, a bɛna dɛmɛ kɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛ ɲɛnamanw layiriwali la ani ka denmisɛnw ka danayako ni kokurakɛli da kɛnɛ kan farikoloɲɛnajɛ siratigɛw la.
ɔgɔndanw danfaralenw senfɛ, basikɛti ɲɔgɔndan 3 ni 3 la, minnu finaliw tanna Lafiyabugu Saba ntolatankɛnɛ kan, musow la, Bamakɔ musow ye tiɲɛ sɔrɔ komini 4nan tɔn kan, ni 13 ni 6 jaabi ye.
Cɛw ka fan na, Bamakɔ Ɛsitadi maliyɛn y’i cooko 8 – 7 ni Falade tɔn ye.
Gala ntolatan, min tun bɛ APJS mɔgɔw bila ɲɔgɔn na ni MINISIMA Cɛki cɛmancɛdenw ye, ye sɔrɔdasiw ka sebagaya filɛ APJS kan ( 5 – 2 ).
Aw k’a dɔn ko, nin jamanaw cɛ ɲɔgɔnyeba farikoloɲɛnajɛ kunkan tako duuruna ye farikoloɲɛnajɛ ɲɛmɔgɔ caman fara ɲɔgɔn kan jamana ani diɲɛ kɔnɔ, farikoloɲɛnajɛ kɔrɔw, pankulu mɔgɔ faamuyalenw, dɔwɛrɛw cɛla.
Salifu Kulibali fɛ - Kiri ɲumanw ka ciw cɛla, minnu kɛra kalo laban ninnu kɔnɔ, Konowari perezidan an’a ka fɔn kɔrɔ, dɔlakelen tora mankun kɔnɔ.
Mali Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ ani Afiriki Mɔgɔ kɔrɔ Afiriki.
Konowari perezidansigikalata laban senfɛ, ɔkutɔburukalo tile 31 san 2020, min ye Alasani Watara ( ADO ) seginna ka kɛ sarati sabanan kama, sɔsɔli kɛra a fɛn sabananw fɛ, Sumeyilu Bubɛyi Mayiga tun bɛ Sahɛlo-Sahari jamanaw ka Jɛkulu ( SEYƐNKI – SAD ) ka filɛli ci ɲɛmɔgɔya la.
Kalata kɔfɛ, Mali Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ bisimila Konowari perezidan fɛ Abijan.
An ka kunnafoniw ka fɔ la, cɛ fila ye fɔli kɛ, janko, ko ka jamana bɛnɲini ka kɛ ɲɛ, sisan ko ADO seginna ka kɛ, ani o tuma ka Loran Bagibo seginni to se, a tun bɛnna ka ŋɛnɛyaw sɛgɛsɛgɛ.
Pari – Berusɛliw - A kumafalen senfɛ, hakilina wolola, Sumuyulu Bubɛyi Mayiga ka fɔ la, min tun bɛna se ka kɛ nin kama.
ADO tun fɔlɔla ka Maki Sali ani Mahamadu Isufi ma, dɔwɛrɛw cɛla.
K’a sɔrɔ ko gɔfɛrɛnaman kuntigi kɔrɔ tɛ min na tuguni ni Bagibo ye ( a ni min tun ye Diɲɛ sosiyalisigidaw ka baarokɛyɔrɔ kelenw sen na ) kabini san tan hakɛ ɲɔgɔnna.
O de la, Giy Delibɛrɛli tɔgɔ y’a jira, min dulonnen don Hamɛdi Bakayoko fɛ, Konowari Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ min fatura marisikalo tile 10.

Mali ŋana kura bɛ na dɔn zuluyekalo tile 14, AYƐSI ka kari don 6nan n’a laban na.

T. KAMARA - A ka lakanabaliya sugu bɛɛ kɛlɛli baara kɔnɔ, Kayi arɔndiseman 2nan polisiso, min ɲɛmɔgɔya bɛ polisi Komisɛri pɛrɛnsipali, Musutafa Jakite, bolo, filɛ ka jɛɲɔgɔn bila Kuluni – Bankasisi sirabakanbagaw kan, n’a kɛtɔla ka tɛmɛ Dagidigi pankulu fɛ.
K’a bɔ polisikunnafonisunw na, mɛkalo tile 16 ka taa tile 17 san 2021, sɔgɔmada nɛgɛkanɲɛ 2 fanfɛla la, kunnafonilasela dɔ, min tɔgɔlen don, ye Kayi arɔndiseman 2nan polisiso wele ko sirabakankɛbagaw ka jamakulu dɔ bɛ Kuluni – Bankasisi sirabakankɛnɛ kan, ka tɛmɛ Dagidigi pankulufɛla fɛ.
Ani k’a fara a kan ko nin binkanikɛlaw tun ye minnu b’u bolofɛnw sɔrɔ kaban.
O nɔ goni na, Kayi arɔndiseman 2nan polisiso ka ɲininiw bolofara ka baarakɛkulu dɔ y’a ta yɔrɔ la yaasa k’a kow lakɔlɔsi ani ka mɔgɔ bisigilenw minɛ.
A yɔrɔ la, sɛgɛsɛgɛlikɛlaw y’a sɔrɔ tiɲɛ na ko mɔgɔ wɔɔrɔ tun minɛnen bɛ mɔgɔ fila la, ni bagabagali ye maramafɛn ɲɛbilalen dɔ fɛ (sɛgɛsɛgɛ dɔ faralen don nɛgɛ la, fɛnsɛgɛn dilanen don) ani motosɛgɛn saba, minnu garilen don sirakankɛnɛ kan.
Cɛman dɔ tun bɛ cɛmancɛ fɛ, o min kɔnɔdɔn kelen tun labɛnnen don nɛgɛkan dɔ la, w’a fan wɛrɛ tun tolen don binkannikɛlaw dɔ fɛ.
O tali, u tun b’a kɛ ka motobolilaw bin, yann’u ka bolominɛnw bɔ u bolo.
A ɲininkalenw ani a ɲininkalenw kuncɛla, a bɔra ko binkanikɛlaw fila bɛ jaabiw kɛ Bama Guta (san 18) ani Sumeyila M. Togo (san 24), bɛɛ jɔlɔsilaw ye, k’a bɛn u kelen-kelen ma.
U bilalen ka taa Polisiso la sɛgɛsɛgɛliw kologɛlɛyali kama, binkanikɛlaw fila nɔnɔnna a kow la, kasɔrɔ dɔ ma cɛsiri sɔrɔ, k’u jalaki.
O la, sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛlɛliw kɔfɛ, u bilala ka taa Kayi Arɔndiseman 2nan polisiso ka san 2021 mɛkalo tile 18 sariyasɛbɛn na.
U bilala yamaruyasɛbɛn kɔnɔ.
Sisan, u b’a sugandili kan k’u sigi arayiw faaba kasobon naani ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.

Alizemi kura tun ka kan.
Hadamadenya ni politiki sira sugu dɔ bɛ min na, yaasa ka bɔ nin murutili la.
Niameyika fanga cɛ kura, gɔfɛrɛnaman min bɛ bolo, kabini awirilikalo tile 02 san 2021, o min donna a la kabini a ka fanga ta, o y’a ka jɔnjɔnw ta.
Bazumu kɛcogo ni kɛcogo bɛ bila sen kan.
Ka kuma u ka Perezidan kura ka cɛsiri an’u ka nɔgɔya kan, Nizerikaw b’u cɛsiri ka maramafɛn jɔnjɔnw sɛbɛn.
Mɔgɔw b’o ani yan, a tɔgɔ ko Iftar ( denmisɛnw ka murutili Ramadan kɔnɔ ), minɛn Niameyi Jɔri Amani pankurujigi kɛnɛ kan, k’a sɔrɔ a tun ka kan ka taa perezidansigikalataama la, k’a segin ka ci kɛ kɔkan na, yaasa ka silamɛw bɛɛ lasɔrɔ ka na u ka sow la, kasɔrɔ sirabakanboli tɛ ban.
Miniti bi saba bɔli la,
Bɛɛlajɛlen na, nin basigi ni madali wale in bonya kosɛbɛ Nizerikaw fɛ.
U b’o parisi dugujukɔrɔfɛjɔyɔrɔ fana kofɔ, a n’a ka cidenkulu, min tun bɛ jamana kɔnɔ, a ka tile laban na Faransi jamana kɔnɔ wa a ka wideyo kɛra min ye bɔlɔlɔ ye bɔlɔlɔ sanfɛ.
Nin alamisadon zuluyekalo tile 1 san 2021, a ka taama ka na Jifa marabolo kɔnɔ ( fatulen an’a kɔrɔ Perezidan TANDYA Mamadu ) bɛ kɔnɔ.
Ani fana, Tɛsikɛri den ye dusukunjɛyɔrɔw jira ka sin nin mara jamaw ma.
U tun tɛ se k’u miiri, ko waati surunnin kɔnɔ jamana ɲɛmɔgɔya la, BAZUYƐMU Mohamɛdi durɔn de ka bonya kɛ yen.
Maramafɛntigiw. Perezidan Bazumu ka don fɔlɔ 100 taamasiyɛnna fana ni ɲɛtaaw ye, minnu man kan ka kɛ sira nataw la.

ladilikɛla ani minisiri jɔyɔrɔw faraɲɔgɔn kan,
ka ladilikɛyɔrɔ ɲɛmɔgɔ jɔyɔrɔw bɔ minisirisow la, minnu tun bɛ ka labɛn kɛ ni ladilikɛla ani sekeretɛri zenerali ye.
Perezidan ka weleli ani bɔli taabolo lakɔlɔsi a pankulu kɔnɔ, ani gɔfɛrɛnaman minisiriw kɛli wajibiyalenw senfɛ jamana taamaw ɲɛnajɛw kelen senfɛ.

jɛrɛjɛkulu baarakɛlaw minisiriw ka ladilikɛso la ( sendikatigiw, tɔnw, sɔrɔ baarakɛɲɔgɔnw kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw ani jagokɛlaw ).
Perezidan ka taamaw Cite kɔnɔ, kasɔrɔ perezidan ka garidiw ka maramafɛn kɛlen t’u bolo, wa u ka caya t’u bolo.

kannabila, min tora kunnafonidilaw ani jama hakilila fɔli ani kɔrɔfɔli la, perezidanfanga sariya ani a baarabolofara baarakɛlaw ka jogoɲumanya hukumu kɔnɔ.

Jamana sagotigiw bolofaraw basigili.
Jɛrɛjɛkulu basigili ani nizeriyako ɲininikɛri politikimɔgɔw bɛɛ sɔnni walasa ka gɔfɛrɛnaman kɛ ani k’a kologɛlɛya Jamana ka sɔrɔlenw kɔnɔ.
ka surun fasodenw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
nɛgɛsɛgɛli kalan ani degelikalan bolofara kan, walasa ka Nizɛri sigidajama hadamadenyako, sɔrɔko ani dɔnko dakun fara ɲɔgɔn kan.
Jamana ka baarakɛna labaarali hakilimaya ani hakilimaya labaarali.
kumaɲɔgɔnya ɲumanw ani danaya minnu hakililatigɛlen don ani k’u di nafolokow kɛbagaw ani kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw ani forobakow yiriwalinafolobɔlaw ma.
bɛn ani kelenya hadamadenya waati la sigidajama kɔnɔ, min sirilen don etiki kɔlɔsiliw madali ani dɔgɔdɔgɔw ani jama dɔgɔdɔw lakanani, minnu fanga ka dɔgɔn, ni Nizɛri sɔrɔko ani hadamadenyako cogoya fɛ.
O kun ninnu bɛɛ kama, Bazumu ka marakɛcogo bɛ fasojama ani Jamanaw teriw hakililatigɛ, ni hadamadenyako ni sɔrɔ yiriwali fɛn ɲumanw kɛli ye ani k’u cogoya ɲuman ye, Bazumu sera ka min labɛn ani k’a dusu don, ka tɛmɛ ɲɛ ani kologɛlɛyali politiki ta fan na.
Ka tɛmɛ tiɲɛtigiw kan Bi kunnafonidilaw waati.
Fasojama bɛ fɛ, a mana tigɛ a ɲɛ o ɲɛ kan, ka dɔ bɔ ɲɔgɔn na, minnu b’a kɔrɔbɔ.
Bazumu Mohamɛdi y’o dɔn koɲuman.
Cɛsiriko ye kokɛcogow ye : baara, ɲɔgɔnyeba, kalan, kɛnɛya, kɛlɛli kɛlɛli, iziniko la.
N’o t’a faamuya, o bɛ na kɛ gɛlɛya belebele ye.
Walasa k’a sɔrɔ a kɔnɔn, Perezidan ka kan ka Nizɛri fasoden-modɛli sugu kura sigi ani ka hadamadenya ɲɛko kɛcogoya « finman » bɔ, kabini waati dɔ la, fanga juguw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
O de ye Gɔfɛrɛnaman Bazumu hakilina an’a kɛcogoya bɛɛ ye.
A ka maramafɛn ani maramafɛn b’a la ka ɲɛ sɔrɔ.
Janko Nizɛri yɛlɛmani jɔnjɔn bɛ na tɛmɛ nin jama fɛ, min bɛ mɛn k’a dɔn ka ɲɛ ani k’a yɛrɛ bɛɛjɛn, tilenniya ani jɛɲɔgɔnya cogoya caman dɔn a kɔnɔ.
Isimayɛli AYIDARA fɛ ( Afiriki Editoriya ɛmɔgɔba ) O bɛ yen.
Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Bubu Sise ye Faraɲɔgɔnkan, perezidanfanga ani Bɛnkanfanga kama (IYƐRIDE) sugandi k’a ka walisiw jɔ.
IBEKA ka Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ ani laban, fo ka se Utikalo tile 18 san 2018 fanga ma, ye Jene bolofara sugandi, a dugunin bɔ, i n’a fɔ a jiginyɔrɔ. Nk’a yɛrɛ de la, bolofara sɔrɔkow sekeretɛri jɔyɔrɔ, min dira a ma, bɛ ye i n’a fɔ perezidansigikalataabolo bɔli jɔyɔrɔ dɔ fɛ, min dɔnnen tɛ dɔn.
Sewaya fɔlɔ de don kaban, IBEKA ka Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ tun bɛ se k’a sendonni jamanakuntigi fatura pariti la.
Mamadu Igɔri Jara ka nali kɛra sababu ye k’a kɛ bankiɲɛmɔgɔ ye cɛbɔ dabɔyalen ye, a degelikalanba tun bɛ min makɔnɔni na.
O waati la, IYƐRIDE, a ka ɲɛmɔgɔ fatura ka mɔgɔ juguya la, tun y’i gɛlɛya ka mɔgɔ jugu dɔ sɔrɔ min bɛ se k’a ka ɲɛmɔgɔya dɛsɛ dafa.
IBEKA Nafolokow Hotel kuntigi kɔrɔ, a tun y’a ɲɛsin Bubu Sise ma, min tun ye san 2018 perezidansigikalata la cɛbɔ kɔrɔn, k’a ɲɛsin a kuntigi kɔrɔ ma, tun ye bolonkɔniɲɔgɔnkɔrɔ degelikaramɔgɔw sɛgɛrɛ dɔgɔkun damadɔ Sumayila Sise ka fatuli kɔfɛ.
Tiɲɛ na, Bubu Sise donni koɲɛ tun bɛ kunw kɔnɔ kabini kalo caman, hali n’a y’a sɔrɔ dugukɔrɔmuso kuntigi kɔrɔ tun donna cogoya dɔ la walasa ka bɔ jɛkulu la, min tun b’a nɔ gɛlɛya walasa, a bɛ fɔ a ma, ka Jamana kubeda sifilɛli.
Pariti wolomara denmisɛn hakɛ dɔw tun b’a yɛrɛ yɛrɛ bɔ ƐMI SƐNKI ƐRƐFIPE kɔnɔ, yɔrɔ min na pariti ye k’a ka Mali fangaɲɛfɔlɔw, n’olu ye fangaɲɛfɔlɔ yɛrɛ-yɛrɛ ɲɛmɔgɔya yɛlɛma.
Hali n’a y’a sɔrɔ FSIDE ɲɛmɔgɔya bɛ kɔnɔna Sogɛli Kokala Mayiga fɛ, Ɛmusɛnki 5 ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu fɛɛrɛ jɛkulu kolatilenna, tun bɛ ye kɛ cogoya fɛ, i ko faraɲɔgɔnkankulu, min labɛnnen don IYƐRIDE fanfɛ, ka tɛmɛ o fɛ, pariti tun t’a kɔdon a faraɲɔgɔnkankulu la.
A bɛ ye kɛnɛ kan, Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Bubu Sise bɛ pariti kɔnɔ jɔyɔrɔ sigi ani min ka kan ka jate walasa ka fangaɲɔgɔnya cɛsiri, k’a da a kan kɔnɔko an’a kɔkanna kirikɛri kan, bawo, o n’a ta bɛɛ, Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ kɔkɔrɔ ka kɔkɔrɔdonnaw bɛ politikitɔn kelen mɔgɔw kan kosɛbɛ.
K’a bɔ Bubu Sise la, welew tun bɔra i ko falenna wɛrɛ, min bɛ da a kan, walima ka tɛmɛ a kan ka pariti hakililatigɛ perezidansigikalata nata marako caman na.
Jɛnni sɔsɔlen walima min makɔnɔnen don?
O bɛɛ la, garidi kɔrɔ tun y’a laɲini ka pariti kelen minɛn, a tun ye tɔgɔ wuli k’i hakililatigɛ ko perezidansigikalata nata don dɔw tun bɛ dayɛlɛ, n’a sarati ye tɔnni ye, min tiɲɛnen don degelikaramɔgɔ la, ni tɔndenyako ye, jɛlen tɛ min na.
A hakilila wulilen teliya la, IYƐRIDE kɛlen kɛra a kɛ mɔgɔ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye pariti misɛnninw ani politiki mɔgɔbaw, minnu sinamatɔnw bɛ ɲɔgɔn ma.
Nka, filɛlikɛla caman bɛ nafoloko yɛlɛma hakililatigɛ, min tɛ dɛsɛli kɛ mɔgɔ kura fɛ.
A ɲɛ walima a ɲɛ, Bubu Sise fana makɔnɔnen bɛ ka degelikaramɔgɔw bɛɛ walima u ka degelikaramɔgɔw fan dɔ ɲɛmɔgɔya, minnu nafolobɔ tun bɛ ka kɛ a perezidan fatura mɔgɔba kelen pewu.
Garidikɛ denmisɛn, min ye baara kɛ kosɛbɛ Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ ka nali na, siga t’a la o bɛ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn na ni Sumayila Sise tɔgɔɲɔgɔn kɔrɔw ye minnu y’a jira k’a fɔ ko fangaɲɔgɔnya yɛlɛma de b’u la degelikaramɔgɔw kɔnɔ.
O cogo kelen na, garidi min tun cɛsirilen don, o min tun y’i labɛn ka sigi Mamadu Igɔri Jara dafɛ, o bɛnni na k’a ye damatɛmɛw daminɛni ye.
Zenerali fatura Sɛki Jara den, SEDEYAWO kɔfɛjɔkow ɲɛmɔgɔ, a ka fatuli tiɲɛnna awiyɔn kasaara dɔ la Nizɛriya jamana kɔnɔ, tun b’a la k’a yɛrɛ kɛ degelikaramɔgɔ, tɛmɛ tɛ min na, ani IBEKA ka fatulen ɲininikɛla, san 2013 ani san 2018 perezidansigikalataw la.
Tiɲɛ don, IYƐRIDE ka kelenyatɔn bɛ ye, o tuma, i ko cɛsiriko, jɔda bɛɛ la, perezidansigikalata nata ɲɛ, Bubu Sise ka kan ka min sɔrɔ fɔlɔ la, wa siga t’a la, o bɛna min sɔrɔ, siga t’a la!
Musa Ture - Gawo Marabolo gɔfɛrɛnɛri y’a latigɛ k’a jira k’a fɔ ko a b’a la ka bagan minɛ, k’a ɲɛsin lakanabaliya ma, min bɛ jamana dugukolo kan.
Sɔrɔ baarakɛbaga Abudulayi Kone ka fagali kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen kɔfɛ, min fagala a denbaya Abudulayi Oputain ka denbaya kɔrɔ k’a danfara a fɛ, Kolonɛli Sidiki Samake taara fanga saba fɛ.
A fɔlɔ ye dugukolo sigili kan, min bɛ na sen kan, k’a daminɛ nin don ntɛnɛndon na ani min bɛna to senna tile tan ni duuru ɲɔgɔnna kɔnɔ, min bɛ se ka lakodɔn, o waati kɔnɔ foroba cakɛdaw ani mɔgɔw ka kannabilaw bɛna kɛ fɛɛrɛ kelen min bɛ sɔgɔma nɛgɛkanɲɛ 21 ni sɔgɔma nɛgɛkanɲɛ 5 cɛ.
Dɔ de tɛ dɔwɛrɛw ye, kojugubakɛlabaw y’a hakili la a ye marabolo wolonwila kɔnɔ.
Walasa ka dɛsɛ ka gɛlɛya sɔrɔ, marabolo mara ɲɛmɔgɔyaso y’a latigɛ fana k’a kɛ sababu ye ka sɔrɔli kɛ yɔrɔw ni walew la, minnu kɛra ka maramafɛnw yɛlɛma ka kɛ denminsɛnw ka ntolatanw ye forobabaaraw senfɛ.
Walasa ka taabolo lasɔrɔ, latigɛlisɛbɛn min ye 0057 ye, feburuyekalo tile 12 san 2021, bɛ ɲɛnamayali ɲɛnajɛw ɲɛnamayali kɛ sariyasɔsɔ la ni tulonkɔniw ye, minnu daminɛna a kɔnɔ, k’a daminɛ marifaw fɛ, minnu bɛ ɲɔgɔn fɛ, n’olu bɛɛ lajɛlen don ɲɔgɔn na.
Mɔgɔ minnu sɔsɔli bɛ nin kɔnɔnasariya kɛcogoya la, n’u ma ɲangili ɲangiliw ɲɛsinnen, minnu ɲɛsigilen don a koɲɛ na, b’u bila minɛni na ani polisiw ka maramafɛn minɛni kokɛtaw la, k’a bɛn a la, sira minnu na arsenali kofɔlen bɛ bolodiɲɔgɔnma kɛ ka bolimafɛn dɔ la, min tɛ se ka bɔ a la.
O tɛ bɛɛ ye.
Gawo gɔfɛrɛnɛri ka ɲɛmɔgɔya kologɛlɛw bɛ fana kɛ mobili tɔgɔlenw kan.
K’a bɔ fɛɛrɛw la minnu bɛ maramafɛn ani lakanakɛbagaw bolo walima u ka jamanaw cɛ bolodiɲɔgɔnw, a kɔnnen don bolifɛnw bɛɛ la minnu ma tɔgɔ sɛbɛn ka ta ka taa duguba kɔnɔ walima ka dugubakɔnɔmɔgɔw, dugubakɔnɔmɔgɔw, dɔwɛrɛw cɛla.
A bɛ ye kɛnɛ kan ko mɔgɔ kologɛlɛnnenw ani mɔgɔ dusu minnu bɛ i n’a fɔ sigida baarasariya kuraw tɛna se k’u bisigi k’olu bɛɛ kɛnɛ kan dugukolo kɔnɔn min kɔlɔsilen don foroba fanga sigibaga fɛ.
O bɛɛ sɔrɔ, u bɛ na sɔrɔ ka lakanabaliya danfara sigi minnu na Jamana bɛ yen ani minnu na a tɛ yen.
A KAYITA - O ye jamanakuntigi ye, kumakanw, minnu tun bɛ ka siraba kabini waati jan, labanna k’u kɛ tiɲɛ ye.
Mali ka Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ, Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Bubu Sise, y’a ka walisiw jɔ Faraɲɔgɔnkan, perezidanfanga ani bɛnkanfanga kama (IYƐRIDE), alamahinɛna Sumayila Sise, la.
A sigilen don, sibiridon zuwɛnkalo tile 26 san 2021, Jene IYƐRIDE bolofara ( Moti Mara ) ka sɔrɔkow sekeretɛri la.
Cɛbɔ kɔrɔ sen don Mali perezidansigikalata la, Mamadu Igɔri Jara sen don Faraɲɔgɔnkan, perezidanfanga ani bɛnkanfanga kama ( IYƐRIDE ) la, Mali Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ, Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Bubu Sise, sɔrɔ ani nafolokow minisiri kɔrɔ, de ka waliw bila pariti belebele jɛlen na.
A tara k’a kɛ Jene IYƐRIDE bolofara ( Moti Marabolo ) sɔrɔkow sekeretɛri ye.
A donni tiɲɛtigiyara, sibiridon zuwɛnkalo tile 26 san 2021, Jene pariti bolofara lajɛrɛ kama.
A kunwalen na, pariti ɲɛmɔgɔyaso ye cidenkulu dɔ bila ka baaraw lakɔlɔsi.
O ye jamanako ye, Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Bubu Sise tara ka kɛ Jene IYƐRIDE bolofara sɔrɔkow sekeretɛri ye.
A bolofara ka lajɛba baaraw ɲɛmɔgɔya tun bɛ IYƐRIDE jamana biro perezidanw, Madani Tarawere, Bɛfon Sise ani Sekeretɛri zenerali dankan Gahuru Dukure fɛ.
o ye sɛbɛnni ye an tun bɛ se ka kalan Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ, Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Bubu Sise, ka facebook sɛbɛn kan.
A talen an ka furakɛla fɛ, sibiridon zuwɛnkalo tile 26 san 2021, k’a hakiliw sɔrɔ nin sendonni kan, IYƐRIDE Sekeretɛri zenerali, Dawuda Ture, y’a da tulow kan ko pariti dayɛlɛlen don sendonni bɛɛ ma.
IYƐRIDE ye pariti dayɛlɛn ye kabini a sigili.
An ka sɛbɛnw dayɛlɛla don sendonniw la.
Tɔnni bɛɛ welelen don.
O ye pariti ye, min dayɛlɛla Malidenw bɛɛ ani hali Afirikikaw ye, minnu bɛ Mali la.
K’a da pariti cɛbɔ sugandili kan 2022 perezidansigikalata kama, IYƐRIDE Sekeretɛri zenerali, Dawuda Ture, y’a dajira ko nin ko in bɛna jalatigɛ sisan tuma min na.
Waati nata, an wele bɛ cɛbɔya la, n’a y’a sɔrɔ tɔndenw bɛ se ka cɛbɔya sɔrɔ, fɛɛrɛw bɛ yen ka cɛbɔ sugandili kɛ.
A y’a kuncɛ ten.
Agibu Sogodogo « Ne ka ɲɛna tun bɛ ka kɛ ne ka kin cɛmancɛ kaso la, nka ni ntolatan ye, ne bɛ ne ka jamana kɔnɔ nafa bɛɛ la » Bariselɔni ntolatankɛnɛ kɔrɔ tɔgɔlamɔgɔ ka fɔ la, fɛn ɲumanba diɲɛ kɔnɔ, o ye ka ɲɛmisɛn di mɔgɔw ma.
« Waati dɔ bɔ fɛ, n y’a faamu ko tɔw kɛli ye fɛn jɔda bɛɛ ye diɲɛ kɔnɔ.
I n’a fɔ n balimakɛ Bubakari Sidiki Sangare, BEYƐSIYƐSI perezidan, ye fɛn min kɛ ni ntolan ɲɔgɔndan dɔ labɛnni ye denmisɛnw kama.
Nin hɛrɛ min ye denmisɛnw ka ye, nin ɲɔgɔndan fɛ, sɔngɔ tɛ yen, wa o de kosɔn, n b’a ɲini aw fɛ ka to ka denmisɛnw ka lajɛ Mali ka hɛrɛ kama.
Nin kɛlɛ kama, n labɛnnen don k’i bilasira », a y’o ɲɛfɔ.
A kumatɔla a ka baarasira kan, Douala den y’a dantigɛ k’ale bɔra denmisɛnw dɔ la, hakilina dɛsɛlen don kosɛbɛ.
« Ne ye kin dɔgɔtɔrɔ den ye, n ka diya tun kɛlen don n ka kin cɛmancɛ kaso la, nka ni ntolatan ye, ne bɛ n ka jamana mago bɛɛ la.
Denmisɛnw, minnu ye BEYƐSIYƐSI jɔnjɔn finali tan, tun nisɔndiyalen bɛ ka n ye, nka u ma faamuya fɛn min, san 27 bɔlen, ne tun bɛ u nɔ na.
Ne tun fatulen don kasɔrɔ n tun tɛ fɛn wɛrɛ fɛn wɛrɛ fɛn wɛrɛ fɛn wɛrɛ fɛn wɛrɛ fɛn wɛrɛ fɛn wɛrɛ fɛn wɛrɛ fɛn wɛrɛ.
Ne ye nin sababu sɔrɔ ka taa n kɛlɛ ni talen wɛrɛw ye ani fana n y’a hakilina sɔrɔ ka baara fɛ.
O de kosɔn, ne bɛ fɔ ne yɛrɛ la tuma dɔw, ko ɲɛni ka sebaaya, o ye baara ye », a y’o fɔ ka kɛnɛ kan, yann’a k’a fara a kan ko a kɛlɛla hali n’a ma gɛlɛya.
« Jɔda la belebele bɛɛ la, o ye k’i dɔn ka wuli.
Ne jigina siɲɛ caman ani n bɛ miiri don min na n k’a fɔ ne ka fa ye ko n bɛna baarasigi bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɛbila Real Madiridi kɔnɔ ani k’u ye bɛnkansɛbɛn ɲini ne ma.
Ne fa y’a fɔ ne ye, ne tɛna kɛ fanga sɔrɔ abada.

N bɛ fɛ ka tariku fitini dɔ fɔ aw ma.
Mɔgɔ min b’a ka wari to a kɔnɔ kasɔrɔ a ma foyi kɛ, o wari tɛ ɲɛ.
Mɔgɔ min bɛ wari bila bankibɔ la, hali n’a y’a sɔrɔ 20% hakɛ don, a bɛ sɔrɔ dɔɔɔni.
O de kɛra ne yɔrɔ min na n bɔra Real Madiridi la, yɔrɔ min na n tun tɛ ka ntola kɛ ka taa Mɔriki, yɔrɔ min na n y’a daminɛ ka ntola kɛ.
O n kɛra sababu ye n ka se ka ntola tan dɔgɔkunlaban kelen-kelen, o min y’a to n ka se ka kɛ fɛn ye min ye bi n ye », a ko ten.
Ani ka laɲini denmisɛnw fɛ u ka dusu sɔrɔ ka latigɛ ɲumanw ta diɲɛ kɔnɔ.

Mali jamana basikɛtiboli musow ka tɔn basikɛtikɛlamusow, minnu ka ca ni san 18 ye, y’a sɛmɛntiya k’u ye diyagoya kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲiniw kɛ u ka degelikaramɔgɔba fɛ, nka Mali basikɛtiboli federason, hali n’a y’a sɔrɔ a ladɔnniyala, ma fɛn kɛ, Yumani Watisi Uruwayiti y’o dantigɛ bi.
Amadu Banba, min si bɛ san 51 la, ye jamana musow ka basikɛtiboli tɔn degelikaramɔgɔba ye, minnu ka ca san 18 bɔ, kabini san 2016, a na kɛ ka basikɛtikɛlamuso saba bin walima k’u ka baarasiraw tiɲɛn, n’u y’u ban ka musoko kɛli kɛ u ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, k’a fɔ ɲumanbaaraw tɔndenw ka fɔ la, minnu ɲininkala Yumani Watisi Uruwayiti Wotisi fɛ.
O kɔfɛ, Yumani Watisi Wotisi ye bataki sɛbɛn Diɲɛ basikɛtiboli federason ( FIBA ) la, nin farikoloɲɛnajɛ ɲɛmɔgɔyaso diɲɛ kɔnɔ, ka diyagoya kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini bisigikumaw pereperelatigɛ Mali la, FIBA ye fɛɛrɛ fɔlɔ jɔda bɛ min kɔnɔ, ka dulon, sɛgɛsɛgɛli jaabiw makɔnɔ, degelikaramɔgɔw ani jɔyɔrɔtigiw, minnu na kɛ ka nin damatɛmɛ kɛ walima minnu na kɛ kɛ o ye.
FIBA perezidan, Hamani angi, min ye Mali jamana ye, y’i senbɔ nin baara la waatila a sɛgɛsɛgɛli kuntaala kɔnɔ.
Yumani Uruwayiti Wotisi ye fɔkabɛn kɛ ni mɔgɔ saba ye minnu tɛ yen an’u ka denbayaw mɔgɔw ye, minnu ye banba ka damatɛmɛ kɛlenw kofɔ Mali basikɛtiboli federason ye.
Kasɔrɔ federason kɛlen ma ko kɛ ka jaabi kɛ ninnu sɔsɔliw la, nka a y’i gɛlɛya ka Banba ka damatɛmɛ kɔnɔ, n’a ye lahidu ta faso kulu sigili la mɔgɔ minnu tɛ yen, k’a da u ka mankun kɔfɛ.
Binkanniw kofɔlenw cɛla, dɔw kɛra diɲɛ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw senfɛ, musow ka diɲɛ kupu, minnu tɛ san 19 bɔ FIBA la, san 2019 ani Afiriki san 18 bɔli ŋanayaɲini san 2020 la.
San 2021 musow ka basikɛti kupu, minnu ka ca ni FIBA tɛ san 19 ye, bɛna kɛ Hɔngiri k’a ta Utikalo tile 7 ka taa a tile 15 la, wa Mali ye kulu 16 dɔlakelen ye, minnu sen bɛ a ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw na.
Mali la, musolakafɛnw n’u ka denbayaw ye kulusijalako kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲiniw kofɔ Banba ye kabini san 2016, a ka san fɔlɔ la, k’a kɛ degelikaramɔgɔ jɔnjɔn ye.
Ajara, jamana musow ka tɔn basikɛtikɛlamuso kɔrɔ dɔ, min si tɛ san 18 bɔ, n’a tɔgɔ, i n’a fɔ kasaralen tɔw ta, falenna u ka lakana kama, ka musoya kafoɲɔgɔnya kɛ ani ka binkanni kɛ Banba fɛ, a fa ka fɔ la, a ye kow laseli min ma.
A y’a dantigɛ k’a ka magali tun daminɛ tuma min na Aza, min si bɛ san 17 la, tun b’a ɲini k’a jɔyɔrɔ sɔrɔ tɔn kɔnɔ : Banba y’a wele a ma ni k’a fɔ a tun bɛ fɛ ka musoko kɛ a ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ ani ko a ka kan ka musoko kɛ a ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ yaasa ka jɔyɔrɔ sɔrɔ tɔn kɔnɔ. Aza banna.
FIBA ka jamanaw cɛ ɲɔgɔndan dɔ senfɛ, nin kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini nana ni diyagoya kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini ye : A [ Banba ] nana Hoteliso kɔnɔ ( n ka denmuso la ) sɔgɔma nɛgɛ ɲɛ 2 waati la.
A y’a tɛgɛ ta, a y’a to a farikolo fan dɔw la.
A y’a tɛgɛw bila a ka kulotɔn kɔnɔ. Ajara bolila ka bɔ so kɔnɔ.
O binkanni kɔfɛ, Banba ye Azara ntolatan waati dɔgɔya kosɛbɛ tɔn kɔnɔ.
Ntolatantɔn basikɛtikɛlamuso fila wɛrɛw ye nin koɲɛdɔnnaw ɲɛfɔ.
Mariyama (seudonimu) y’a lase Yumani Watisi Wotisi ma ko tuma min na a si bɛ san 15 la, Banba y’a ɲini ka musoko kɛ ale ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, a ka hoteliso kɔnɔ, tɔn ka taama dɔ senfɛ FIBA diɲɛ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kama, ani k’a senbɔ tɔn na, a ka ban kɔfɛ.
Mariyama y’a sɛmɛntiya fana ko Banba tun bɛ kasobonba denmisɛnw bagabaga, n’u tun b’a kɛcogoya lagosi.
Denmusonin sabanan dɔ, Umaru (seudonimu), y’a sɛmɛntiya ko tuma min na a tun bɛ san 17 la, Banba y’a ɲini k’a sɔrɔ a muso la ani ka musoko kɛ a ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
Tuma min n y’a ban, a ma to n ka ntola tan.
A ye n bila ntolatanw kɔnɔ. Ntolatanna musow y’a sɛmɛntiya Yumani Uruwayiti Wotisi ye k’a fɔ ko kulusijala tun bɛ Banba la ni jamana musow ka ntolatanna wɛrɛw ye, minnu tɛ san 18 bɔ, ni ka kulusijalafɛnw kumafalen kɛli ye k’a ɲɛsin ntolatan waati ma, wari ani farikoloɲɛnajɛ labɛnw ma.
Mali la, diyagoya waleyaw ni mɔgɔw ye minnu si bɛ san 15 la ka taa san 21 la, olu ye sariyasɔsɔ ye min kɛbaga ye denbaya ye min ka fanga bɛ mɔgɔ la walima n’a ka kalan walima n’a ka lakɔli bɛ baara la, walima n’a ka baaratigi ye.
A ka kɔlɔsili baara hukumu kɔnɔ ani ka bɛn a ka donni sariyaw ma FIBA la, Mali basikɛtiboli federason de ka kan ka ntolatannaw ani basikɛtikɛlamusow lakana damatɛmɛw la ani ka degelikaramɔgɔw kɛli jɔyɔrɔtigiyaw la ni ɲangiliw ye ani bilali.
Denmisenw ani balikubaliw, minnu bɛ FIBA farati la, hakɛw lakana ntuloma Sɛbɛn duuru ka fɔ la, diyagoya kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini ani diyagoya kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini kama ntolatannaw ani basikɛtikɛlaw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, k’a fara magaliw kan minnu kɛlen don balikubaliw kan u degelikaramɔgɔw fɛ.
Sɔrɔli kɛ diyagoya kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini ani kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini bɛ se ka nɔw sɔrɔ waati jan na mɔgɔ minnu bɛ to u farikolo ani hakili kɛnɛ kan, i n’a fɔ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya, depression ani trauma kɔfɛ gɛrɛzɛgɛya taabolo.
Fa, min y’a denmuso, Ajara, ka koɲɛ cogoya ɲɛfɔ, y’a dantigɛ k’o, ntolatanna ɲumanba, tun ye basikɛti bila Banba ka minɛn kɔfɛ.
A bɛ lajɔ ka caya wa foyi kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen tɛ nin waati la.
A kɛr’a la. Funankɛniw bɛ siran k’u ka jɔyɔrɔ tora ntolatantɔn kɔnɔ walima k’u gɛrɛ nɔw la, ola, ko cogoya gɛlɛya kosɛbɛ.
Ahimari Mayiga, Afiriki ni Mali farikoloɲɛnajɛ denmisɛnw ka Lakana sigibaga, ntolatannaw ani basikɛtikɛlamusow ka lakana tɔn dɔ y’o dantigɛ.
Ka caya, Mali basikɛtiboli federason jɔyɔrɔ tun ka kan ka ye ka basikɛtikɛlamusow lakana, nk’a mɔgɔ si tɛ hami nin denmisɛn ntolatannaw fɛ cogoya la minnu tɛ se ka kɛ. Federason ka dɛsɛli a ka jɔyɔrɔtigiya la ka sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛ walima ka magali bisigikumaw juguya la ka kɛ banba ka nali ɲɛ.
Mariyama y’a dantigɛ k’a fɔ ko Banba ye musow ka basikɛtiboli tɔn degelikaramɔgɔ sabanan ye.
Farikoloɲɛnajɛ ɲangata ye gɛlɛya ye min bɛ jamana kɔnɔ, Mali kɔnɔ ani farikoloɲɛnajɛ kan.
2018 jamana ɲɛmɔgɔsɛgɛli ɲɛmɔgɔyasɛbɛn ka sɛgɛsɛgɛli dɔ y’a to a jate ko Mali musow ani npogotigiw, minnu si bɛ san 15 la ka taa san 49 la, bɛ ɲangataw sɔrɔ nin cogo la.
Ni Zezolɛnpikiw ye Japan jamana kɔnɔ ani FIBA san 19 tɛmɛnenw ka Diɲɛ basikɛti kupu ye, minnu bɛ ka sɔrɔ joona, FIBA ani SEYEW ka kan ka kokɛta dɔw ta joona walasa ka degelikaramɔgɔw bɛɛ, minnu bɛ ka damatɛmɛ kɛ, ani basikɛtiboli ɲɛmɔgɔw bɛɛ, minnu ma se k’u ka ci la ka Mali basikɛtikɛlamusow lakana.

An ye nin janfa sɔrɔ ka sin ale ma, tile damadɔ kɔ, teri dɔ fɛ Ameriki dugukolo kan.
Anw tun y’a dɔn ko Maliden bɛ se ka kɛ jɔnjɔn ye a kanukɛɲɔgɔn na, k’a sababu kɛ dɔrɔnko ye walima n’a diyagoya ye ka bɔ a la.
Nka, an tun bɛ ban k’a jira k’a fɔ ko Hamani angi jatigɛbagaw bɛna sɔn ka san sɔrɔ fo yɔrɔ jan na ka cɛ dɔ fara ɲɔgɔn kan basikɛtiboli ɲɛnabɔli la ani hali farikoloɲɛnajɛ kunkan, a ka ca ka tɛmɛ o kan.
O n’a ta bɛɛ, an tun ka kan k’an sigi n’a bɛɛ kɔfɛ, Hayidara Ayisata Sise n’a bɛ fɔ a ma Sato (Cemancɛ fanga depite kɔrɔ n’a ka SEYƐNITE jamana kolatigɛjɛkulu mɔgɔ kɔrɔ ), o minɛnni kɛra mɛkalo tɛmɛnen Maliden dɔw fɛ, minnu sigilen don Farafina woroduguyanfan na, yaasa a kana sigi ka kɛ Farafina depite perezidanti ye.
Muso jɔnjɔn, Afiriki tilebinyanfan ani cɛmancɛfan bɛɛ n’a kɛra Magɛrɛbu ye min farikolo bila bolo la, nege kɛr’a la, nege kɛr’a la, nege kɛr’a la a ka fasodenɲɔgɔnw fɛ k’a da a kan dɔw tun bɛ fɛ k’a yɛrɛ fɔ k’a yɛrɛ fɔ k’a yɛrɛ fɔ k’a fɔ k’a yɛrɛ fɔ k’a yɛrɛ fɔ k’a yɛrɛ fɔ k’a yɛrɛ fɔ k’a yɛrɛ fɔ ni nin ɲɔgɔnna koɲumanya ye.
Tuma min i ye fitini ye, mɔgɔ bɛ tɔw ka nafa juguya la.
A ɲɛfɔlen k’a da a kan tempelibagatɔ, Mali ka kan ka jɛn ni min ye. Ni Mali kɛra basikɛti tempɛyɔrɔ ye, janko musow ta, Hamani angi y’a latigɛbaga ye.
A talen a ka koɲɛw ɲɛnabɔli taɲɛ fɛ ani a kokɛta yiriwali yecogo min bɛ a la, k’a to a dugumada fɛ,
A y’a ( basikɛti ) to a ka bɔ a ka farifaga la ani k’a kɛ bonya ka da a kan Afiriki ani diɲɛ kɔnɔ.
Wulikajɔ galabu, a sera ka min lasɔrɔ Afiriki basikɛti la, k’a kɛ FIFBA / Afiriki perezidan, o kɔfɛ FIBA perezidan ye.
Basikɛti Liga Afirika walima Afiriki basikɛti Ligi ( ƐNIBEYA dawulama kɛcogoya Afitiki ) tako fɔlɔ, k’a ta mɛkalo tile 16 la ka se a tile 30 la Kigali, Ruwanda kɔnɔ, o b’a seereya.
K’a bɔ a la, ko ale de ka perezidanya kɔnɔ Mali y’a ka bangu jɔnjɔn fɔlɔ ta ( jama farikoloɲɛnajɛw la ) kulɔbukunda (Joliba musow, san 1995 ) ani jamana jamajɛtɔnw ( Samatasɛgɛ musomanw, san 2007, Dakaro, Senegali kɔnɔ ).
Ni o ye bonya sɔrɔ nin ɲɛmɔgɔ in na ani a ɲɛmɔgɔ, min ye bonya ani bonya koɲɛdɔn, Afiriki fan bɛɛ fɛ ani diɲɛ kɔnɔ, a yɛrɛ ka jamana kɔnɔ nin tɛmɛsira kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya bɛ min na, ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
Nka, den bɛɛ nisɔn kɛ min ye, Hamani sera tuma bɛɛ ka jɔnjɔnw tiɲɛ, an ma dabila ka minnu kɛ a ye, kabini a y’a yɛrɛ bɔ a ka marakɛcogo danfara fɛ.
Wa, siga t’a la, u b’u yɛlɛma dibi kɔnɔ ( u ma dusu sɔrɔ ka baara kɛ ni kɔnɔn bɔli ye ), kabini Hamani angi y’a latigɛ ka bila waatini kɔnɔ karidon tɛmɛnen ( zuwɛnkalo tile 13 san 2021) walasa FIBA k’a ka sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛ a yɛrɛ kan nin diyagoya kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini bisigikumaw kan basikɛtikɛlamusow kan ( denmisɛnninw na a kow bisigilenw waati la ) Mali kɔnɔ.
Ne sen ma don abada ani ne ma jalakiliw komɛn abada, minnu cogoyaw fɔlen don aw ka bataki kɔnɔ, a y’o sɛbɛn Niyɔriki Tayimu ma.
O bɔlen kɔ yen, Niyɔrɔki donkibaru faseri tɛ foyi si jira ko perezidan angi ye basikɛtikɛlamusow diyagoya kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini Mali la.
Nka, i n’a fɔ a y’a jira an na, a ka hakilila an’a ka jogoɲumanya farikoloɲɛnajɛ la tun bɛ fɛ a ka bila sɛgɛsɛgɛlikɛlaw ka bila la, a ka waatilabaara kɛlen kɔ. Mɔgɔ minnu bɛɛ ka baara kɛ dusukunjɛlenya kɔnɔ ni Wɛki angi ye walima n’u y’a kɛrɛfɛ, olu dun nɔnabila ni ka nin janfa kalanni ye.
Ani k’o kɛ, k’a da a kan ɲɛmɔgɔ tɛ min bɛ jɛn n’a ye dan ka sɔrɔ ntolatannaw ani musomanw farikolo ani hakili la, a ye minnu ka nafaw lakana tuma bɛɛ.
Jɔn de bɛ se an na laban na?
Munna Malidenw kɛra nin gɛlɛya la ka taa u yɛrɛ ka nafaw la diɲɛ ɲɛfɛ?, an ka cɛmisɛn, Kasimu Tarawore, y’a yɛrɛ ɲininka a ka Facebook tile kɔnɔ.
Ani ka hakilijigin kɛ ko nin koɲɛ wulila ka bɔ fan bɛɛ la sini Bamakɔ.
U b’a miiri ka Hamani angi nɔgɔya, nka k’a kɔdon o ma, Mali de nɔgɔyalen don halibi.
Farafina dɔ min bɛ FIBA kunna, k’a fara Maliden dɔ kan, o ka kan ka kɛ dusukunjɛ ye anw fɛ.
Nka o bɛɛ la, dɔw ma se ka min kun bɔ abada wa u ye mankutu caman kɛ walasa k’a bɔ.
Wa hali farati kɛ ka jamana tɔgɔ tiɲɛni ma kɛ sababu ye k’u bɛ bila u ka dɛsɛ la.
O de tɛ mɔgɔ ɲuman ye bi, k’a da a kan mɔgɔ tɛ se ka ɲɛcogo ɲuman, fasodenya ɲuman, panafirikani ɲuman ladiyali.
ani ka Hamani angi fɛ, fo ka se hakɛ la.
Wa i n’a fɔ miiri lakodɔnnen dɔ y’a fɔ cogo min, kiritigɛla dɔ bɛ yen min tɔgɔ ko waati wa a bɛ mɔgɔw bila a jɔyɔrɔ la!
Alfali A seginnen Konowari cɛmancɛ ani tilebinyanfan kɔnɔ, perezidan kɔrɔ Loran Bagibo y’a ka kiri kofɔ, ntɛnɛndon, diɲɛ kojugu Kiribulonba fɛ.
« Ne tɛ kojugukɛla ye.» Nin y’a siɲɛ fɔlɔ ye kabini a seginnen Konowari, perezidan kɔrɔ Loran Bagibo ye kuma fɔ, ntɛnɛndon zuwɛnkalo tile 28, a ka kiri an’a labili la Diɲɛ kojugukɛrɛba (SEPEYI) fɛ, k’a sɛmɛntiya k’a tun bilala ka taa Lahayi bawo « cɛ gɛlɛya dɔ tun ka kan ka bɔ ɲɔgɔn na ».
« SEPEYI, o tun tɛ sɛbɛ la, cɛ min bɛ mɔgɔ kofɔ, ani ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn min bɛ mɔgɔ kofɔ, o la, olu y’a bila yen », Loran Bagibo y’o dantigɛ Mama, a ka bangamara la, Konowari tilebinyanfan jamana cɛmancɛ la.
Nka, a y’a fara a kan ka bɔ laadaɲɛmɔgɔw, a ka paritiɲɛmɔgɔw an’a ka kunnafonidilaw ɲɛkɔrɔ, « n man nimisa, bawo n n tun seginna ni kojugukɛcogo ye, aw bɛɛ de bɛ na malo sɔrɔ yan ».
Loran Bagibo labila pewu, marisikalo laban, SEYƐPI fɛ, yɔrɔ min na a jalakira kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la ni kojugukɛw ye ka sin diɲɛ ma, o kɛra sababu ye k’a segin Kodiwari.
« Jɛmanw fana, minnu t’an dɔn, minnu bɛ an ka kɛlɛ ncininw kɔfɛ yan, y’a dɔn ko ne ( tun tɛ ) tun tɛ kojugukɛ ye.
Ne bɛɛ kɛ, ɲɛ, nka ne tɛ kojugukɛla ye », Loran Bagibo y’o sɛmɛntiya dɛmɛninw kɔrɔ.
A tun b’a fɔ ni laadalaɲɛmɔgɔw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ ɲɔgɔn cɛ ɲɔgɔn cɛ ɲɔgɔn cɛ ɲɔgɔn cɛ ɲɔgɔn cɛ ɲɔgɔn cɛ ɲɔgɔn cɛ, minnu donna a la ni « bɛnɲini » ci ye.
« Bɛnɲini dafalen » « A yeli de tun bɛ kɛnɛ kan an tun sigilen bɛ ka bɛnɲini kama.
Fo a ka kan k’i sinsin a ka jama kan yaasa ka Konowari fasojama wele bɛɛ ka bɛnɲini kama ɲuman », Jozefu Goli Obu, Mama ka « dugukolow kuntigi » y’o dantigɛ AYƐFIPE ye, sigida ɲɛmɔgɔba dɔ, min lamɛnnen don mɔgɔba dɔw fɛ.
O laadalaɲɛmɔgɔw ka kan fana ka don ɲɛnajɛ la min na k’a « purifayɛ » cogo min, i n’a fɔ a ka jamana laadala b’a fɛ cogo min nɔnabila mɔgɔ ye ani min bilala kaso la.
« Taradon, n bɛna a lasɔrɔ, n bɛna a ɲini a fɛ k’a to bɛnɲini baara la, a ka kuma fɔlɔw ka taa jamana ma bɛnɲini siratigɛ la », « dugukolow kuntigi » y’o sɛmɛntiya, a kɛtɔla k’a sɛmɛntiya k’a ka saratiwaati kɛ a mɔgɔw fɛ nin ɲɛnajɛ kama.
« Jama belebele kɔnɔ, tuma min na du mɔgɔ dɔ bɔra gɛlɛya dɔ la, mɔgɔw b’a lasɔrɔ.
O de kɔrɔ ye k’a yɛlɛma a ka da kɛnɛ kan sɔgɔmada jona fɛ, yanni sankɔrɔtalen ɲɛ, ni bɔli ye kɛnɛ kan k’a bɛ tali kɛ ni Kpobarawi ani Titawi laadaw ye », san saba ɲɛmɔgɔ y’o ɲɛfɔ.
Mama forobakɛnɛ kan, dugu sigibagaw y’a makɔnɔni makɔnɔ, k’a to perezidandan kɔrɔ ka kuma filɛ u la, ni k’a tan ni k’a kɛ.
« Bagibo tara walasa ka lafiya lasɔrɔ jamana kɔnɔ », Brigite Kudu, min bɔra Zebizeku dugunin mɔgɔw fɛ, y’o fɔ.
« Ne nisɔndiyara, nin don in ye kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye.
Perezidan Bagibo kannabilalen don.
Mɔgɔ b’a kan k’a mɛn, a k’a fɔ kuma kelen durɔn », Beyatisi Jedeje, min bɔra Kpakeku, y’o fɔ a bolo, « bɛn ani bɛnɲini » taamasiyɛnnen dɔ de b’a bolo.
Mɔgɔ ba caman ye sebagaya bɔli kɛ a ye, karidon, Mama, tile tan a seginnen kɔ Abijan.
Seginni, min ma kɛ gɛlɛya si ye, k’a kɔdon a nali ma, zuwɛnkalo tile 17 Abijan, n’a taamasiyɛnna ni caman cɛjɔyɔrɔw ye, lakanakɛbagaw ani a kanuɲɔgɔnw cɛ, minnu tun bɛ fɛ k’a lasɔrɔ pankulu kɔrɔ.
Loran Bagibo, min tun bɛ fanga la kabini 2000 fanga la, tun minɛna awirili 2011 Abijan, o kɔfɛ kalo wolonfila bila ka taga SEPEYI la, yaasa k’a kiri ka taa ɲangataw la, san 2010 perezidansigikalata laban kɔfɛ.
A banni ka jɔ a ka dɛsɛli la, Alasani Watara ɲɛkɔrɔ, tun ye kalata kɔkan gɛlɛya kɛ, min ye su 3 000 kɛ.
A kura ɔkutɔburukalo san 2020 saratiwaati sabanan kama, Alasani Watara ye ɲɛfɛjɔ di Loran Bagibo ka seginni la tile damadɔ a ka labili kɔfɛ.
Ni AƐFUPE ye Jamana Labɛnni kura minisiri min bɛ fangabulonw cɛkow ɲɛnabɔli bɛ min bolo, Karamɔgɔba Ibarahima Ikasa Mayiga, ka badenyataama hukumu kɔnɔ Jamana fangabulonw ye, kabini a ka sigili la, a taara, ntɛnɛndon zuwɛnkalo tile 28 san 2021, Jamana cɛmancɛlafanga biro la, min ɲɛmɔgɔya bɛ Sanogo Aminata Male fɛ.
Nin taama, min ye Sanogo n’a baarakɛɲɔgɔnw yeli jira, kɛra taamasiyɛn baaraɲɔgɔnya ye fan fila ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, min nana ni Mali Jamana labɛn kura ye.
An y’a sugandi, fɔlɔsili kɛ, ka na Jamana cɛmancɛlafanga ka biro la.
minisiri Ikasaka ko ten, k’a da a kan cakɛbulon faralen don, jamana ni fasodenw cɛ kuma fɔ.
Jɔnni ye nin cakɛbulon kɔrɔ, a ko ten, walasa ka jamana cogoya tiɲɛ di, Jamana fasodenw bɛ min miiri la, Jamana k’a yɛlɛma, k’a labɛn kura.
Bi.
Jamanakuntigi yɛrɛbakun, Karamɔgɔba Ibarahima Ikasa Mayiga ka kɔkɔrɔdon na, an ye fɛɛrɛ sɔrɔ ka Jamana jɔ.
K’a da a kan, koɲɛdɔnni, koɲɛdɔnni de bɛ se ka ko cogoyaw faamuya ani ka ɲɛnabɔcogow kofɔ.
Ani o, Minisiri tɛmɛna kuma fɛ, an y’a to u ka dai ɲuman na.
An ye Jamana fɛn kɔlɔsili lataamacogo lakɔlɔsi.
fɛɛrɛw sɛgɛsɛgɛliw, Jamana ni a jɛɲɔgɔnw cɛ, hadamadenyako, politikiw, ani fasodenw durɔn.
A dɛsɛliw dɔgɔyara.
O waati surunnin kɔnɔ, minisiri Ibarahima Ikasa Mayiga y’a jɔ a la, an tun nana ni badenyataama ye, nka nin taama yɛlɛmana ka kɛ baaraɲɔgɔnya ye, walasa k’an ka Jamana miiri kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, kabini sariyasunba fɛ ka taa fasodenya fɛ, fasodenya kɛcogoya la, ani cogoya la ka fasodenya labɛn kokura waati kɔnɔ, walasa a ka to jamana cɛmancɛ la, a daminɛ an’a laban na.
O de ye an ka taama kɛcogo ye.
A kɛra lakɔli yɛrɛ-yɛrɛ ye an fɛ.
An bɛ lamɛnni na kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la Jamana baarakɛla dɔ fɛ min ye kirisow ɲɛnabɔ, kabini dugumada fɛ ka taa sanfɛ, jamana kirisow, i n’a fɔ maraboloyɔrɔw kɔnɔ, n bɛ kuma SEDEYAWO kan sini, nka fana min tɛmɛna Jamana ka sanfɛyɔrɔ yɛlɛmaba fan bɛɛ fɛ, walasa ka filɛ, ka faamuya, ka sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛ.
O de la an ye deli kɛ bi.
Nin tɛ dɔwɛrɛ ye dɔgɔyali ye.
An bɛna segin ka na sɔɔni yaasa ka ɲɛnabɔcogow kalan ka ɲɛsin forow danfaralenw ma, jamana ɲɔgɔnfaamuya lajɛba min tun bɛ Jamana cɛmancɛbaga ɲɛnajɛ kɛyɔrɔ la, i n’a fɔ jamana kumaɲɔgɔnya bɛɛ sen bɛ min bolo Jamana cɛmancɛbaga la yɔrɔ min na.
Kumaɲɔgɔnya donw cɛmancɛlafanga kan, sigibaga tɔw ani don cɛmancɛlafanga kan, ɲɔgɔn kan, yuruguyurugu, kalan, kiri, adw. O ye dajiraw ye, nka fo an ka kan ka taa ɲuman sugandiliw fanfɛ ani ka Mali kura dilan.
O de la an ye min sɔrɔ yan.
An ye k’a ye k’o ye ko bɛ se ka kɛ.
Sisan, cogoya dɔɔnin kɔnɔ, k’o bɛɛ faaba kɛ, ka ɲɛnabɔcogow sɔrɔ, minnu labɛnnen don ka waleya cɛmancɛlafanga tɔgɔ kama ani olu kɔfɛ, ni ɲɛmɔgɔ kura sigilenw ye, minnu bɛna kɛ k’u cɛsiri ka ɲɛnabɔcogow ye, minnu sɔnna Malidenw bɛɛ fɛ.
O de fɔra anw ye ɲɛnabɔcogo ye Mali kama.
Wa an hakililatigɛla anw kɔrɔfɔw la.
N bɛ Barikada kɛ Jamana Cɛmancɛ n’a ka baarakɛkulu la, u ka labɛnni na.
An bɛna taa Malidenw bɛɛ ɲɛ, yaasa mɔgɔ bɛɛ ka faamu k’a fɔ ko mago kelen, faraɲɔgɔnkan kelen bɛ yen Mali dafɛ, ka taa ɲɛnabɔcogow ɲɛfɛ, minnu ye kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye.
Hadama B. Fofana Aminata Sidibe, Jamana Sigidalamɔgɔw ka pankurujamana Cakɛda (Anac) ka mara kolatigɛjɛkulu perezidan ye, ye o jɛkulu ka laadalatɔnsigi 29nan ɲɛmɔgɔya kɛ.
Nin tun ye alamisadon zuwɛnkalo tile 23 san 2021, A cakɛda ka lajɛso kɔnɔ.
A tun bɛ kɛ ka sɛbɛnw ani waleyali yɔrɔw jira ka kɛ sɛbɛn kɔnɔn yani a ka baaraw daminɛ ka kɛ sɛbɛn kura la.
O cogo de la, mara kolatigɛjɛkulu perezidanti, Aminata Sidibe, a ka kumafɔ senfɛ, ye hakilijigin kɛ ko nin waatilabaara bɛ kɛ waati min na an ka jamana bɛ fangabulonko, lakana ani kɛnɛyako gɛlɛya kɔnɔ, min n’a nɔw ye sɔrɔ baaraw dɔgɔya ye.
Ka da a la a ko in na.
Nin ɲɔgɔnye baaraw ka kan ka kɛ, janko, baara kofɔlenw fɛsɛli an’u sɔnni na, baara kofɔlenw san 2020 baaraw laselisɛbɛn an’a ɲɛnabɔli laselisɛbɛn, baara bolodalenw san 2021 baara kama waleyali yɔrɔ fɛ, ani fana Cakɛda ka labɛncogo labɛncogo yɛlɛmani baarabolodali an’a labɛncogo labɛncogo fɛsɛfɛsɛli.
A ka kuma fɔlenw na, Anaki ka baarakɛsan 2020 latigɛlisɛbɛn lakodɔnnen ye sɔrɔw ani kuluw la, k’a da Sefa wari hakɛ dɔrɔmɛ 4 33 419 824 hakɛ kan.
Wari sɔrɔlenw na, binkanniw kɛra ka se sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 4 584 320 666 ma, k’a bɛn 98,94% ma, k’a da fɔliw kɔrɔ.
Wari hakɛw bɛ jate ka kɛ Sefa wari 4 404 884 862 ye, n’o ye taacogo ye 96,09% ye, k’a da kibaliw kan.
A ka baarakɛnafolo falenni n’a ta bɛɛ, k’a sababu kɛ koronawirisi fiɲɛbanaba ye, min ye dɛsɛ sɔrɔ 60%, Anaki ka baarakɛlenw, mɔgɔw b’a jate.
Perezidan Modibo Keyita-Sɛna ( AYIPƐNKI – ƐSI ) ka sɛbɛn lakurayali,
Lakana ani lakana ɲɛmɔgɔw kologɛlɛyali Mali pankuruw yɔrɔw kan, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnneya la Bamakɔ Senfu, min ye sɛbɛnfɛnbɔli kɛlɛkɛlɛli yɔrɔw sɛbɛn.

Tumutu ani Gawo pankuruw lakurayali, minnu y’a daminɛ ka sonyaliw sɔrɔ, n’a kɛra Kayi pankurujigi kan ; kalan dɔ kɛra Kayi ani Sikaso pankuruw fiyɛlɛli kama.
ɲininisɛbɛnw daminɛna Kidali, Mɛnaka ani Tawodeniti pankuruw yɔrɔni nafolobɔ kama.
Baara bolodalenw siratigɛ la, a bɛ hakilina kuraw kofɔ.
An bɛ ka ɲinini baarabolodali kɛ walasa ka jamana pankulu sigi. Kuma laban na, an bɛna tɛmɛ ani ka pankulu pankulu sirili kan, min daminɛna san 2020 wa min bɛna tɛmɛna kɛ, bawo sɛbɛntiya hakililaw dɔ de don.
A y’o mɛtigiya.
A bɔlen bɛ A cakɛda ka baaraw kofɔlenw na, minnu tun sɔrɔdasi kosɛbɛ kɛnɛyako gɛlɛya fɛ, k’a daminɛ kokura, ka taa ɲɔgɔn fɛ, k’a da a kan pankuru yuruguyurugu taacogo kan, awiyɔn kuluw Aipk-ƐSI ye dɔbɔn 28,8% kɔnɔ san 2020 kɔnɔ, k’a da san 2019 kɔnɔ.
Taamakɛta yuruguyurugufeere fana jigina ka bɔ 57,3% ɲɔgɔnna san 2020 kɔnɔ, k’a da san 2019 kan.
O bɛ sɔrɔ dulonni fɛ, k’a daminɛ marisikalo tile 19 san 2020 la ka taa zuluyekalo tile 25 san 2020, taamadenw ka jagokɛyɔrɔw sonyaliw ka taa Mali la, Kowidi - dizinɛfu ( 19 ) fiɲɛbanaba kɛlɛ hukumu kɔnɔ.
Adama TARAWORE - Kidali dugu, Mali kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya kɔnɔ, kɛra forobabaaraw jɔnjɔn ye kabini dɔgɔkun damadɔ.
Jamana minisiri caman ka taama kɔfɛ, Alize Bɛnkansɛbɛn kɔlɔsilikɛjɛkulu ka dakun de tun ye ka sigi dugu kɔnɔ, o min tun kɔnnen don gɔfɛrɛnaman mɔgɔw fɛ ɲini ka san 7 bɔ.
An yɔrɔ jan don waati la min na Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ Musa Mara tun bɛ ka taama kunfalen kɛ dugu kɔnɔ, san 2014.
Kabini nin don na, kow yɛlɛmana ka taa bɛɛ la kuluw maramafɛntigiw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ minnu tun bɛ Kidali dugu ɲɛmɔgɔya ani Cɛmancɛ Jamana cɛ.
San caman kɔnɔ, yɛrɛbakunw ka kannabilalen ɲɛmɔgɔw ka dusukasi ka sin Mali ma, tiɲɛna.
O yɛrɛ sigibagaw yɛrɛ sɔrɔlen bɛ k’u sigi yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya la, wa diɲɛ mɔgɔkɔrɔdonbagaw, min ye burudamɛ ko ye, b’a dɔn k’a fɔ ko sahelikungoyɔrɔ masiridenw yɛrɛ-yɛrɛ ye jihadikɛlaw ye, foyi si tɛ minnu bolo, ka bɔ dugukolo tileni na, min bɛ ɲɔgɔn na.
Sanw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ la, jogoɲumanya, min tun bɛ Yɔgɔw ni Imagadi cɛ barika dafɛ, y’a dɔgɔya kosɛbɛ.
Gati t’a jigi ye ka dugu lasɔrɔ fanga fɛ, ka tɛmɛ Ɛli Haji Gamu kan an’a yɛrɛw yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya bɛ k’u yɛrɛ lasɔrɔ dugu kɔnɔ.
Teriyantolatankɛw kɛliw kɛra dɔɔɔni ye, w’a musow ani denmisɛnw ka yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya, minnu ɲɛmɔgɔya bɛ kuluw maramafɛntigiw fɛ, bɛ ɲini ka tunun.
O bɛɛ n’a ta, Kidali bɛ to i n’a fɔ muso fatuli, a hakili b’a ka cɛsiri an’a farikoloɲɛnajɛw la.
K’a kɛ kɔsa min, a y’a mɔgɔ kofɔlenw bila ka tɛmɛ kumalasesɛbɛn fɛ, min bɛ sɔrɔdasi zoni fila sigili dantigɛ Guruma kɔnɔ Azawadi tɔnw ka Koladilanjɛkulu (SEMA) fɛ.
N’o ma kɛ wale ye min bɛ kɛnɛ kan, o ye kanu dantigɛli ye, SEMA jɔyɔrɔtigiw ka fɔ la, minnu k’u bɛ waleya kɛ dusukunnako ye jamaw ye, minnu sɔrɔlen don ɲankataw la.
Nka SEMA ka damatɛmɛni ŋaniya tɛ fan si la Malidenw fɛ, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la kɔgɔduguya jamajɛkulu dɔw.
Kaɲaka marabolo sigibagaw fanba bolo, kuma tɛ kɛ ko kulu marifatigi dɔ, min bɛ don ani k’a ɲɛ belebele Kidali, bɛ na ka bugɔlɔso gɛlɛya Guruma kɔnɔ, lakanabaliya bɛ min na kaban.
Ka bɔ Ifogiw ka dugu la walasa k’u yɛrɛ sigi yɔrɔ wɛrɛw la, o ye sɔrɔdasi fɛɛrɛ ye, min tɛ mɔgɔw fɛ fana gɔfɛrɛnaman ye, o min ka kokɛcogo kɔrɔtalen y’a to a faamuya ko SEMA y’a ka wale kɛ kelen ye sɛbɛn in kɔnɔ.
Ko bɛɛ kɛlen, Ifogayi sigifɛnw y’u cɛsiri kalo laban ninnu kɔnɔ, n’o tɛ kabini san 2020, yɔrɔ min na siɲɛ fɔlɔ tɛmɛnenw Turegɛzi sɔnna Alize Bɛnkansɛbɛn bɛn ani bɛnɲini kama Mali la yɛlɛmali taabolo ma.
Jamana kumaɲɔgɔnya, bɛɛ sen bɛ min na Bamakɔ, san 2019 desanburukalo la, Kidali cidenkuluw y’u ka Mali tɔgɔ, min tɔgɔ kelen ani mɔgɔ tilalen tɛ, sɛmɛntiya pewu.
Nin kɔrɔfɔ kɛbagaw dɔlakelen, Mosa Agi Atahari, ye Denmisɛnw ani Farikoloɲɛnajɛw minisiri ye sisan.
Kidali dugu bɔlen mɔgɔ caman wɛrɛw bɛ gɔfɛrɛnaman kɔnɔ, i n’a fɔ Alamudu Agi Iliyɛni, Malidenw minisiri sigilen kɔkan.
Nin yɔrɔfɔw gɔfɛrɛnɛri kɔrɔ, min bɛ ATT perezidan kɔnɔ, tɛ mɔgɔ tɔgɔ dɔnnen ye Kidali burudamɛ burudamɛ kɔnɔ.
Ni minisiriw ani jamana cidenkuluw seginna ka Kidali sira ta, siga t’a la ko gɔfɛrɛnaman ka nin daw dayɛlɛnni kosɔn zoni denmisɛnw ye, min tolen don Jamana bolo.
Umaru KONATE Tuma min na diɲɛ tɔ bɛ ka taa ɲɛmajɔ la, Mali
A y’i tɛmɛ ka taa ɲɛ, ni Kameruni tɛ dɔ ye.
Kabini san 1991, foyi si tɛ sigi nin jamana ɲuman kɔnɔ, yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya faw y’u denw di.
An b’a kɛ, an b’a dɛsɛ kokura.
A filɛ kɛcogoya fɛ, politiki cogoya bɛ taa cogo min na jamana kɔnɔ kabini san tan ni saba bɔ.
Ni politiki mɔgɔw bɛ ɲɛ nɔ bɛ nin politiki hakilila kɔnɔn, fasojama, a bɛ sɛgɛn, k’a gɛlɛya ani ka balo gɛlɛya kɔnɔ, min ɲɔgɔn ma deli ka kɛ.
Juguman na, wulikajɔ seginna ka na.
Bamakɔ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, mɔgɔw b’a miiri ko cɛw ka yɛlɛmani kɛli de bɛ na se ka kɛ Jamana ɲɛmɔgɔya la.
U ( Bamakɔkaw ) t’a dɔn ko taabolo de bɛ kofɔ wa cɛw tɛ.
O de kosɔn, u bɛ sira la halibi, ka X walima Y ka taali la, tuma min na u tɛ fɛ k’a kunna, kasɔrɔ u ma kɔrɔta hakililatigɛ.
O de kɛra san 2020 ni silamɛyadiɲɛmɔgɔ dɔw ka bɔliw kɔlɔsili tɛ minnu kan ani ƐMISƐNKI – ƐRƐFIPE.
U ye mankutu kɛ gɛlɛya kɔnɔ ka taa Jamana ɲɛmɔgɔya la walasa ka lɛbaga caman sama ka bɔ siraw kɔnɔ dɔgɔkun caman kɔnɔ, ka perezidan Ibarahima Bubakari Keyita ka baarabila la, min tara demokarasi kɔnɔ, n’a ta bɛɛ.
U ka kɛlɛ kɔnɔ, u ma se ka hakililatigɛ di Malidenw ma, ka ɲɛsin jamana nata ma, IBEKA kɔfɛ. Nin tiɲɛnisigiya kɔnɔ, min bɛ danbetigiya ko la, Kati ɲɛmɔgɔ denmisɛn dɔw donna tanni la, utikalo tile 18, san 2020. Sɔrɔdasiyataama daminɛ politikikɛnɛ kan, min bɛ na ni dusukasi ni dusukasi ye Ɛmusɛnki Ɛrɛfupe jɔyɔrɔtigiw fɛ, minnu bɛ na u ka bolofara la, sɔrɔdasiyata jɛkulu fɛ, min bɔra ka Jamana Kolatigɛjɛkulu sigi, fasodenw ka hɛ
U ka fɔ la, fanga tun seginna u ka hakɛ la.
Nin y’a jira k’a fɔ ko damatɛmɛ tɛ faga Mali la, nka a yɛrɛ b’a la k’i gɛlɛya.
Demokaratiw, minnu bɛ fɛ ka fanga ta sira kɔnɔ.
U ma se k’a dɔn, sɔrɔdasiyata denmisɛnw ma se k’u jɔyɔrɔ fa ka ɲɛsin fasojama ma min y’a sɛgɛn ka sigi ka ɲɛ.
