agali kɔnɔn!
Gɔfɛrɛnaman dɔ labɛnni kɔfɛ, fɛn bɛ daminɛ ka daminɛ.
Jamana cɛmancɛlafanga kolatigɛjɛkulu ( SEYƐNITE ) bilala sen kan k’a kɛ cogoya kelenw kɔnɔ, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la Mali sigidajama tilali kosɔn, min bɛ mɔgɔw ka jɛɲɔgɔnya ani sendonni gɛlɛya kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, minnu sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛra olu fɛ, yen fɛ.
Tiɲɛnisɛya ani danaya dɛsɛ bɛ sigi Jamana kunna.
Cɛmancɛlafanga jɛkulu ani sɔrɔdasi kama tɛ ka ɲɛsin kelen yɔrɔ ma tuguni.
Kɔlɔsili ye mɛkalo tile 24 san 2021.
Segin ka na a daminɛ ma.
Cɛmancɛlafanga perezidan, Mubahi Njadu, n’a ka minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ, Mukutari Wani, bilala ka bila perezidandankan fɛ, kalo kɔnɔntɔn kɔnɔ, cɛmancɛlafanga laban na, o la, o ye fasodenw ka jigi bɔ a la.
Tuma bɛɛ sɛgɛnnen don yaasa ka jigiya segin.
Sɔrɔdasikɛ jɛkulu kuntigi y’a latigɛ ka yɛrɛbakun ka kow ta bolo la.
O kɛli kama, baarakɛɲɔgɔnw bɛ ka caya ni Mali cakɛda mɔgɔw bɛɛ ye.
Nin daminɛ kura kama, a ko ɲuman kɛra ƐMI SƐNKI ƐRƐFIPE kan, min bɛ a ka fɛɛrɛ jɛkulu perezidan jira k’a kɛ Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ jɔyɔrɔ ye.
Nin taabolo ɲuman bɛ nin tɔn baarakɛbagaw bolo, minnu bɛ sebagaya wele kaban, bɛ ɲininkaliw kun ye, minnu jɔda ka bon, filɛlikɛla caman fɛ, u ladɔnniyalen.
A tun y’a kɔlɔlɔsili ye sɔrɔdasi fɛn na, Sogɛli Mayiga bɛna kɛ baarakɛcogoya dɔrɔnni ye walasa ka yɛrɛbakun ka nafaw kɔfɛ walima k’a yɛrɛ kɛ jɔyɔrɔ ye walasa k’a ka politiki hakilila kɔfɛ? Sogɛli Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ, nin ye kɛlɛ ɲuman ye fasoɲɛmɔgɔw ka tɔn kama.
ƐMUPEYƐRI.
Kabini san 1991, o pariti b’a ɲini ka sira dɔgɔya politikikɛcogoya la.
A kɛtɔla Sogɛli sɔnna a ma k’a kɛ Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔya kɔnɔ, Kolonɛli Asimi Goyita y’a ɲinɛ ko sɔrɔdasiw ka yɛlɛnni politiki kɛnɛ kan o bɛ kɛ politikimɔgɔw dɛsɛ ye, Sogɛli bɛ min kɔnɔ kabini san bisaba?
Kasɔrɔ a ma pereperelatigɛ kɛ, gɔfɛrɛnaman nata bɛna kɛ, fanba la, ƐMUSƐNKI ɲɛmɔgɔw ye.
Sogɛli la, an b’a jira k’a fɔ ko pariti ncinin dɔ walima wɛrɛkofɔ jɛkulu marakɛcogo ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ tɛ kelen ye ka bɔ Jamana ta la bawo tiɲɛw an’a kɔrɔfɔw tɛ kelen ye.
Minnu y’u teliya k’a fɔ ko Sogɛli ye cɛ ye cogoya cɛ ye, u ka kan ka yɔrɔ bɔ.
Cɛ kiri bɛ kɛ baara fɛ ani a tɛ kɔrɔfɔ fɔ.
Ɛmusɛnki Ɛrɛfupe fɛɛrɛ jɛkulu perezidan kɛlɛla yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya kama, mɔgɔ b’a faamuya nɔgɔyara ko nin tɛ kɛ ka Mali mago ɲɛ, nka k’a ŋɛnɛ yɛlɛma kɛ fɛn ye.
Sogɛli bɛna ɲɔgɔn sɔrɔ fɛn bɛɛ la a tun bɛ fɛ ka min kɛlɛ ƐMISƐNKI – ƐRƐFIPE bɔliw senfɛ wa cɛ ka gɛlɛya kosɛbɛ a ka fɛn min tɛ fɛ.
Kɔkɔrɔdonbaga caman minnu fɔra nin fɛ, o fɛ, olu tɛ dɔwɛrɛ ye ka baara lanɔgɔya cɛmancɛlafanga ɲɛmɔgɔ kuraw ye bawo, an bɛ dɛmɛ kɛ mɔgɔ la ni walew ye minnu kɛra wa fɔli tɛ kumakanw fɛ walima siratigɛw fɛ.
Malidenw fanba tɛ dumuni siɲɛ saba don.
Baarakɛdenw ka sɛgɛn bɛ yɛlɛ don ni don.
Dɔgɔtɔrɔw don ni mɔgɔ jigiwaralenw ye.
yɔrɔ minnu cɛsirilen bɛɛ ɲininikɛla la,
jamana bɛɛ bɛ maramafɛntigi kuluw ka kɔlɔsili kɔnɔ, w’a banbaganciya bɛ ka ban Bamakɔ.
Malidenw tɛ yɔrɔnin kelen durɔn.
O tuma, waati tɛ kɔrɔfɔkabɛn kologɛlɛyalenw walima politikicɛsirikow filiw ye bilen.
I n’a fɔ cɛmancɛlafanga perezidan kura y’a fɔ cogo min, faden kelen min bɛ ɲɔgɔn na, o ye waati ye.
O la, walasa k’a seereya Maliden miliyon 20 ma, k’a bɛ se ka Mali kura sigi, Sogɛli ka kan fɔlɔ ka bɔlɔlɔw la, minnu bɛ kɛ sariyasɔsɔ la feerekɛlaw fɛ, ka dɔ bɔ ɲininikɛla hakɛ dɔgɔya an ka siraw kɔnɔ, ka kɛnɛkɛnɛw lakana ani laban na ka jɔnjɔnw bila ɲuman ka kɛlɛ ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, n’a bɛ fɔli ye yuruguyurugu, n’a bɛ fɔli la, n’a bɛ fɔli la ani nafoloko ɲangili.
Politiki walima fɔkabɛn ani misali ɲuman marakɛcogo, a ye lahidu ta Malidenw ye.
Jɔnni ka kan ka bɔ mɔgɔ ye walima ni min ye?
Ni bɔli ni misali ye a ka kan ka kɛ, Sogɛli b’a dɔn ka ɲɛsin mɔgɔ ma ko ale tɛ a ka kan ka kɛ a labɛn.
A bɛ mɔgɔ dɔw de la ni minnu ka kan ka bɔ a ɲɔgɔn na, wa a ka misali tɛ a bɛɛ la ɲuman ye, n’an bɛ kalan a kɔfɛ sɛbɛnw kɔnɔ.
Kasobonba « Kasobonba » bɛ ye Jamana ɲɛmɔgɔya la kaban cɛmancɛlafanga kofɔ.
Kolonɛli Asimi Goyita, yɛlɛma kɛlen a la, y’a jira, a ka kɔrɔfɔ kɔnɔ, k’a jira k’a fɔ ko a bɛna sigi jamana Kumaɲɔgɔnya bɛɛ sen bɛ min na, cɛmancɛlafanga waleyali kama kalo kɔnɔntɔn kɔnɔ, minnu tolen don.
Min ye Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ ye jamana sigili kuraw labɛnni bila ɲɛ fɛ walasa k’a ka cɛmancɛlafanga lataama.
K’a ye da a kan, Sogɛli y’i yɛlɛma ka taa mɛɛnni kan, min t’a tɔgɔ fɔ.
Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ kura ka walew bɛ nin bisigikuma sɔrɔ.
N’a kɔfɛ k’i cɛsiri fɛn bakuruba la, min ye fangabulonkow yɛlɛmaniw labɛnni ye, walasa ka kalafili kannabilalenw labɛn ni jɛlenw labɛn, a bɛ waati kɛ kosɛbɛ taamaw la, minnu tɛ fɛn ye ka latigɛli kɛli ɲuman fɛ.
Nin taamaw ani kumaɲɔgɔnyaw, an ye olu ye ka ye kaban nin jamana kɔnɔ.
A farali kuma fɔlen, Sogɛli dun bɛ tali kɛ ni cɛmancɛlafanga bɛnkansɛbɛn ye, n’a ka gɔfɛrɛnaman ye mɔgɔ mugan ni wolonfila ( 28 ) bɛ min na.
Min ye bɛɛ sen donni ye baara kɛnɛ kan mɔgɔ kura ka kɔrɔfɔw bɛɛ la, a yɔrɔ ka jan sɔrɔ a sɔrɔ.
Gɔfɛrɛnaman kura labɛnnen don kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la ni ƐMI 5nan mɔgɔw ye, sɔrɔdasiw, kulu marifatigiw ani mɔgɔbaw, minnu wajibiyalen don diinɛ ɲɛmɔgɔ dɔw fɛ.
Politiki mɔgɔw ani jɛrɛjɛkuluw bolofara, jɔda bɛ min na, bɔra nin cogo la.
O ko cogoya tɛ fɛn ye ka fisa jamana sigiliw kɛli la minnu bɛ Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kun na.
Kow hakɛ la, minnu bɛ ɲininkaliw kɛ jamana nata kan nin marakɛcogo kɔnɔ, n’a taamasiyɛnna kaban ni tiɲɛni ye.
Donan.
Lebedem.
Fo mɔgɔ ka miiri la ko Alize Bɛnkansɛbɛn kalanni kura bɛna kɛ a fan dɔlakelen kama ani ka fan tɔw bila.
Bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɔbilala fan saba bɛɛ ka laɲiniw ye, u bɛ fɛ k’u bila Bɛnkansɛbɛn kɔnɔ.
Bɛnkansɛbɛn ma kan ka dayɛlɛ kokura.
O ye fiɲɛbanaba ye, min ka kan ka bali.
ye SEMA mɔgɔw, minnu tun bɛ Bamakɔ, kunnafonilajɛ dɔ senfɛ kunnafonidilaw ka soba la, karidon tɛmɛnen.
U tun ye cidenkulu ɲɛmɔgɔ, Atayi Agi Mohamɛdi, Med Alimuludu Ulidi Ramadan, kumalasela, Sidi Agi Bayi ani Tila Agi Zayini, bɛɛ SEMA ka cidenkulu mɔgɔw ye, minnu tun bɛ Bamakɔ la, ka Bɛnkansɛbɛn bilali sen kan kunnafonidilaw ɲɛkɔrɔ, Alize baarataabolo Bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɔbilali san 6 kama.
Min ye Alize Bɛnkansɛbɛn kalanni kura ko ye, SEMA mɔgɔw, minnu tun bɛ lajɛ na, bɛɛ bɛnna ni nin ko ye fiɲɛbanaba ye, min man kan ka dayɛlɛ abada.
U ka kumalasela Alimuludu Ulidi Ramadan ka fɔ la, fan bɛɛ bolonɔbilali fan bɛɛ ka laɲiniw ye, u bɛ fɛ ka minnu kɛ.
Bɛn bɛnkansɛbɛn kalanni kura bɛ na kɛ sababu ye anw fana ka fɛn bɛɛ lana an ma se k’o don Alize.
a y’o dantigɛ.
Bɛnkansɛbɛn fan si ma wasa sɔrɔ.
Diɲɛmaa de y’an jagoya ka Bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɛbila.
An tun t’a fɛ ka bolonɔbila.
Tila Agi Zewini y’o fɔ.
Cidenkulu mɔgɔw bolo, Bɛnkansɛbɛn bɛ fanbaw don ba la kaban, Jamana ka sagotigiya, jamana kelenya, jamana dugukolo tileniya ani jamana ka perezidanfanga cogoya bɛ minnu na.
Ni fan dɔw b’a jate ko nin koɲɛw dɔlakelen sɔsɔla, a fan bɛ se ka Bɛnkansɛbɛn kɔlɔsilikɛjɛkulu ( SEYƐSIYA ) bila a falenni kama.
Ataye y’o ɲɛfɔ walasa k’a kunw ani taabolo jira, minnu bɛna se ka Bɛnkansɛbɛn ka falen.
Nin kɔnɔkow tɛ, falenni wɛrɛ si tɛ.
Nin kalanni kura bɛ se ka Bɛnkansɛbɛn dayɛlɛ ni cɛfɔli wɛrɛw ye, minnu tɛna labɛn.
O bɛ na kɛ Bɛnkansɛbɛn tɛ waleyali ye.
ye Lajɛ kumakɛlaw ɲɛfɛ yani a k’a hakililatigɛ ko nin waleya tɛna kɛ kɛ dusukasiw tali kura ye kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la Mali ni kuluw maramafɛntigiw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
Politiki wulikajɔ bɛɛ, kɔlɔsili bɛɛ, min bɛ na ni min ma deli ka kɛ, o tuma, kɔlɔsili bɛ segin na.
Diɲɛ bɛɛ taabolo de don.
O kandi ma kɛ, mɔgɔ tɛ se ka jigifa ko gɛlɛya tɛna kɛ.
Atayi Agi Mohamɛdi, cidenkuluɲɛmɔgɔ bɛ siran.
K’a bɔ o la, SEMA hakililatigɛlen bɛ to senna cɛmancɛlafanga fɛ.
Cɛmancɛlafanga gɔfɛrɛnaman ka tɛmɛ Cɛmancɛlafanga Perezidan fɛ, a ma banakoya jira an na, k’a da Bɛnkansɛbɛn lawaleyali kan.
A ma bɔ an na fɛn dɔ la, min bɛ mɔgɔ da a la ko ŋaniya t’a la k’a kɛ.
Kolonɛli Asimi Goyita y’a jira k’a fɔ k’a ka kɔrɔfɔw kɔkɔrɔmadon ni Cɛmancɛlafanga Perezidan ka fɔli ye k’Alize Bɛnkansɛbɛn waliyali kɛcogoya ye.
SEMA k’a b’a fɔ k’a labɛnnen don ka taa Bɛnkansɛbɛn lakana fo ka taa SEYƐNITE ɲɛkɔrɔ.
SEMA bɛ se bi ka kunnafonidi lajɛba labɛn Bamakɔ ani k’u ka hakilila di u ka kannabila ani lakana kɔnɔ.
O b’a jira k’a fɔ ko tababu bɔra wa danaya b’a daminɛ ka sigi.
Cidenkulu Atayi Agi Mohamɛdi y’o lakodɔn.
Kureyisi Sise.
BƐNKI BƐNKI DE ALIZƐRI San wɔɔrɔ bolonɔbilali kɔfɛ, a lawaliyali gɛlɛyaw Bolonɔbilala mɛkalo tile 15 san 2015 o kɔfɛ lakodɔnnen zuwɛnkalo tile 20, Bɛn ani bɛnɲini Bɛnkansɛbɛn Mali la, min bɔra Alize taabolo la san wɔɔrɔ, a lawaliyali kɔfɛ ye lagamuli caman kun ye.
Mali kɛlɛbolo ka jagoya dɛsɛlen kɔ ka Kidali dugu minɛ, murutili fanfɛ wa o min kɛra fiasko ye.
O waati famaw ye kumafalenw daminɛ Alizeri ni SEMA ( SEMA ) banbaganci kɔrɔw ye diɲɛmɔgɔw ka ɲɛmajɔ kɔnɔ ani kalo kɔrɔntɔn kɔfɛ, min y’a to fan fila ka fu siri kɛnɛ kan.
Mali ɲɛmɔgɔw ka laɲini na, Bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɔbilala jamanakunda Bamakɔ, mɛkalo tile 15 san 2015 ani san kelen zuwɛn tile 20 kama, mɔgɔ minnu tun nege bɛ.
San wɔɔrɔ tɛmɛnnen kɔ, Bɛn bɛnkansɛbɛn min bɔra Alize baarataabolo la, o bɛ to ka caman bɔ ɲɛnɛ ani ɲɔgɔn cɛ, olu kelenw fɛ, minnu y’u ka bolonɔbila kɛ.
Wa n’an ka kan ka san wɔɔrɔ bakurubajate kɛ, n’a bɔra tile wɔɔrɔ min lakɔlɔsi koɲuman ni marifatigi kuluw bolonɔbilala ani Mali kɛlɛbolo ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, a waleyali bɛ to kunbalan ye waati bɛɛ SEYƐSIYA wɛrɛw n’a ta bɛ waati min na an ka sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛ, o kun ninnu kunw bɛ kɛ kɛ baarakɛbagaw ( kɛlɛbolo kulu ani Jamana ), minnu bɛ kɛ fankelenfɛjuguya la, fan kelen fɛ ani fan wɛrɛ fɛ, nin gafe mankanni fɛ, jama fɛ.
O de b’a to mɔgɔ lakodɔnnenw ka tɛmɛ bɛnkansɛbɛn dafɛ.
O sababu la bi, Bɛnkansɛbɛn bɛ kirin, yɛlɛma jɔnjɔn si tun ma se ka sen kan kasɔrɔ faralikɛbaga kɔrɔw, minnu ma maramafɛn, y’u kologɛlɛya k’u ka sɔrɔdasi kɛ Mali kɔrɔnfɛla kan bi, ni k’u tɛgɛ fanga di jatigɛwalekuluw ma, minnu bɛ ka taa Sahɛli kɔnɔ.
O bɔlen kɔ yen, o de ye Nizɛri perezidan kɔrɔ, Mahamadu Isufi, bila k’a fɔ ko siga ma bɔ, Bɛnkansɛbɛn bilali sen kan bɛ marabolo bɔ u dabolo kan ani ko.
Kidali ye bagabagali ye Nizɛri kɔnɔna lakana kama.
Sidi Barahimu Ulidi Sidati ka dɛmɛni, min ye Alizeri bɛnkansɛbɛn falenni bolonɔbilala Azawadi jɛkuluw ka kolatilenjɛkulu (SEMA) tɔgɔ la, ye dusukunnako sigi a baarakɛɲɔgɔnw kɔnɔ, minnu cɛsirilen don bɛn ani basigi ɲinini kama Mali la.
Ni Abudulayi Umaru Jɔpu ka nali ye Kɔkankow ani Jamanaw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ bolodiɲɔgɔnma cakɛdaba la, an’a min ye nin bɛnkansɛbɛn kɛbaga ye, an jigi b’a kan ko a bɛ na gɛlɛya dɔ kɛ a waleyali kama.
Usumani Mahamani - Kɛlɛbolo labɛnnen kɛlɛbolo fɔlɔw labɛnni, hadamadenya sigibajuw baaradaw seginni, DEDEYƐRI, yiriwali baarabolodaliw kɛra, dɔwɛrɛw cɛla, ko fɔlenw kɛra, nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn senfɛ, min ɲɔgɔn ma deli ka kɛ. Bɛnkansɛbɛn, bɛn ani bɛnɲini kama, min bɔra Alize taabolo la ani diɲɛmɔgɔw ye ɲɛsigi sɔrɔ kunu, ni ɲɔgɔnye ye, Kɔlɔsilikɛjɛkulu ( SEYƐSIYA ) ka ɲɔgɔnye
Kabini bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɔbilala san 2015 baarakɛbagaw cɛ, fɔlɔ
A ɲinini fɔlɔ tun ye kɛ sɛtanburukalo san 2019.
Ani fana gɔfɛrɛnaman kama, ani diɲɛ mɔgɔw maramafɛntigi jɛkuluw ani diɲɛ mɔgɔw kama, taama Kidali, o tuma, tun ka gɛlɛya do, ka nin tɛmɛni don waati kura la, bɛn taabolo la.
Gɔfɛrɛnaman mɔgɔ wɔɔrɔ ye taama kɛ.
Kolonɛli - mazɔri Isimayeli Wage ( Jamana Bɛnɲini ), Mamadu Mohamɛdi Kulibali ( Jamana ka kofɔlen ), Mohamɛdi Saliya Ture ( Baara ni degelibaara ), Kolonɛli Modibo Kone ( Sigidalamɔgɔw ka Lakana ani Lakana ), Bintu Funɛ Samake ( Musow ni Den ka Lataa ɲɛ ) ani Mahamudu Ulidi Mohamɛdi ( Sɛnɛ, Jagoko ani Pesko ).
.
faseri kɔfɛ L’Essɔri san 2021 kalosaba fɔlɔ kɔnɔ, Fekola daman ye sanu ɔnsi 125 088 bɔ, k’a bɛn 7% ( ɔnsi 8 088 ) ma ka tɛmɛ ɲɛsigilen kan. BEDEGLODI Mali dugujukɔrɔfɛnw ka jɔyɔrɔtigiw ye ntɛnɛndon zuwɛnkalo tile 14 tɛmɛnen labɛn u ka daga la, min sigilen don Nizɛri Cite la, u ka san kunnafonidilajɛ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen, min ye suguya 3nan ye.
Sababu jɔyɔrɔtigiw bolo ka sigidajama ka baarakɛlen bakurubajate kɛ, gɛlɛyaw an’a ko nataw.
U ye kunnafonidilaw ka laneli ɲɛfɔ gɛlɛya kan min sirilen bɛ Minankoto yɔrɔ fɛnbɔ yamaruyasɛbɛn dili kura mankan na Keɲeba.
A lajɛba tun bɛ ka kɛ ni Bedegɔlidi ɛmɔgɔba, Bili Litili, ye, lamini a masurunnamɔgɔ caman fɛ.
A ka lamɛnni na, ɛmɔgɔba y’a dantigɛ ko san 2020 kɔnɔ, BedeGɔlidi – Mali cakɛda ye dɛmɛ kɛ Mali sɔrɔ la, k’a bɛn sefawari miliyari 34 ɲɔgɔnna ma, saraw ani hadamadenya nafamafɛnw na, baarakɛlaw ye.
San 2016 – 2020 waati kɔnɔ, Bili Litili, a ka dugujukɔrɔfɛnw cakɛda ye Sefa wari miliyari 162 ɲɔgɔnna sarali Mali gɔfɛrɛnaman ye.
Sigida mɔgɔw ka yiriwalinafolobɔ kɔrɔw, DEZE ka fɔ la, bɛ sefawari miliyari 2,1 ɲɔgɔnna na, ani sefawari miliyari 82 ɲɔgɔnna minɛnen bɛ fɛnw sanni na Mali la.
Fekola daman, fɛnsɔrɔw ani ko nataw. Bedegɔlidi – Mali ɲɛmɔgɔba fɔlɔ y’a dajira ko san 2020 kɔnɔ, Fekola daman ye sanu ɔnsi 622.000 bɔ, a bɛ ɲini ka sanu tɔni 18 bɔ.
San 2021 kalosaba fɔlɔ kɔnɔ, Fekola daman ye sanu ɔnsi 125 088 bɔ, k’a bɛn 7% ( ɔnsi 8 088 ) ma, ka tɛmɛ ɲɛsigilen kan, a y’a ɲɛfɔ, ka kɔn a dantigɛ k’a fɔ ko san 2021 kɔnɔ, Fekola daman tun ka kan ka sanu ɔnsi 530 000 ni 560 000 cɛ ( tɔni 16 ɲɔgɔnna ), ni fɛnsɔrɔw b’a ta Lamerikɛn dolariwari 405 ni 445 cɛ ( Sefawari 245.000 ɲɔgɔnna ) ɔnsi kelen.
Diɲɛ kurudon sɔngɔ ( PEYƐRIZE ) bɛ kɛ Lamerikɛn dolariwari 745 ni 785 cɛ ( Sefa wari miliyɔn 432.000 bɛ ɲɔgɔn na ) ɔnsi kelen.
Baara sigida. San 2020 laban na, Bedegɔlidi tun bɛ Malidenw 2.053 baara la ani mɔgɔ minnu bɛ ta ka bɔ jamana kɔnɔ 130.
O kɔrɔ k’a fɔ ko an ka baarakɛta dɔrɔmɛ 90nan ye Mali ye, a y’o dantigɛ, ani k’a fara a kan ko An bɛ to ka sigida baarakɛta dɔw jɔyɔrɔta, n’a kɛli ye ka baarakɛta maganw bila sigida ani jamana hakɛw la.
Hadamadenya jɔyɔrɔtigiyaw ani sigidajama ka yiriwali. O siratigɛ la, lajɛba y’a da kɛnɛ kan ko 2021 baarabolodali kuraw jirala ani tara Keɲeba sigidajama ka yiriwali ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu fɛ.
Bakuruba fɔ la, a bɛn’a pereperelatigɛ, ni baarabolodali tan jirala ani k’a lakodɔnni ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu fɛ, Fagu, Medinandi, Tintiba, Malaya, Bilaliba, Kolɔnba ani Sokundo dugukolow ani dugukolow nafama na, ni Fekola ani Bɛtekili ye.
Bulilitili ka fɔ la, a ka baarabolodaliw musakaw mumɛ jate bɛ Sefa wari miliyɔn 300 ye.
Fekola tɔgɔlajanba Fekola tɔgɔlajanba Fekola tɔgɔlajanba Fekola tɔgɔlajanba Fekola tɔgɔlajanba Fekola tɔgɔlajanba Fekola tɔgɔlajanba Fekola tɔgɔlajanba Fekolo tɔgɔlajanba dɔ kɔnɔ.
Mali gɔfɛrɛnaman ye Fekola S.A. ka daman jɛɲɔgɔnjugu kɛnɛ ye. nin cakɛda ka nafolow 80% min bɛ baara la Keɲeba sɛrikili kɔnɔ, olu bolo BEDEGɔlidi bolo ani 20% Mali Jamana bolo.
kunnafonidilaw ka ɲininkaliw ye minɛn kɛ, janko, Minankoto fɛnbɔ yamaruyasɛbɛn bɔli cogoya kan, k’a da BEDEGɔlidi ka wari miliyɔn 500 wari kan, i n’a fɔ vinibɔ.
A ka jaabi kɔnɔ, DEZE Bili Litili ye nin jalakiliw mankutu ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
A ka kumafɔw la, k’a kɔdon fɛn min bɛ don kunnafonidilaw la, BedeGɔlidi Mali ma foyi san Minankoto yamaruyasɛbɛn bɔli kama.
AM Ture - K’a kɔdon kunnafoni dɔw ma, san 2021 mɛkalo tile 7 minisirisariya n° 2021 waleyali, min bɛ tali kɛ peyazi ani sirabakanboli yɔrɔw sigili kan ani k’u ka yɛrɛtigiya sɔngɔw sigi, bɛ kɛ cogo ɲuman ye.
Wa bisigikumaw, minnu bɛ sɛbɛn namaralenw kofɔ, tɛ dɔwɛrɛ ye.
Jɔdaba fɔlɔ don, ka minisirisariya kofɔ, yaasa ka gɛlɛya sɔrɔ koɲuman.
Nin minisirisariya min bɛ minisiriw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, a ka sariyasen 2 kɔnɔ, b’a dantigɛ ko jɔyɔrɔw, minnu sigilen don, bɛ bila cɛmancɛlafanga la, k’a ɲɔgɔn fɛ, sariyaw, minnu bɛ senna, labato.
Sariyasen 3 b’a fɔ ko peyazi baarakɛyɔrɔ dɔ farali ni mobili kelen ye, o bɛ peyazi wari sarali kɔnɔ, min sɔngɔw sigilen don nin cogo la.
Bolimafɛn saba kama, sɔngɔ bɛ dɔrɔmɛ 400 ɲɛ sɛgɛsɛgɛ la ani tɛmɛni kɔnɔ.
Kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw bolo (250 ɲɛsin ani tɛmɛni kɔnɔ).
takisiw (F250 sɛgɛsɛgɛli ani tɛmɛsɛgɛli kɔnɔ).
forobafɛnw minibusi minnu ka ca ni mɔgɔ 25 ye (Sefa wari 250 sɛgɛn ani tɛmɛsɛgɛla kɔnɔ).
Donfiniw minnu bɛ sojɔminɛnw taama baaraw la (300 dɔrɔn ani tɛmɛni kɔnɔ).
businw ani businw, minnu ka mɔgɔw ka ca ni mɔgɔ 25 ye ( Sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 300, ani tɛmɛni kɔnɔ ).
dɔwɛrɛw ani dɔwɛrɛw donitalaw (300 ɲɛsin ani tɛmɛni kɔnɔ).
Jɔda b’a la fana k’a dantigɛ ni taamasiyɛn ye ko bɛɛjɔyɔrɔ hakɛ bɛ se ka lakodɔn san kelen, sirakan labɛnni magoɲɛw jateminɛ kɔfɛ, k’a da sɔngɔta taaɲɛ kan.
Wa jama minnu sigilen bɛ peyazi jɔyɔrɔw la bɛ sɔrɔ bɛnkasɛbɛn karitɛmɛ sɔrɔ, min dili kɛcogoyaw an’a wari hakɛ sigilen don minisiri ka sira bɛ min bolo.
O bɔlen kɔ yen, nin minisiriso cɛ minisirisariya sariyasen 4 b’a fɔ ko peyazi ni pesazi baarakɛyɔrɔ, min ma cɛsiri la, bɛ sirakanboli ɲɛmɔgɔ fɛ fo k’a sɔrɔ baarakɛden dɔ ka baara la.
Peyazi wari sɔrɔ minnu bɛ bɔ nin minisirisariya sariyasen 2 waleyali la bɛna tilali kɛ cogoyaw kɔnɔ, minnu sigilen don yamaruyasɛbɛn doniw gafe fɛ.
Ani fana, a ka sariyasen 7 ka fɔ la, ɲɛmɔgɔw, minnu bɛ baara la nin minisirisariya waleyali la, ye :
Jamana sirakanw ɲɛmɔgɔ, jamana dugukolo, kɛnɛ ani bajikantaamaw ɲɛmɔgɔ, Sirakanw ɛmɔgɔba ɲɛmɔgɔba, Zandarama ɲɛmɔgɔba, Polisi ɲɛmɔgɔba, Sigidalamɔgɔw ka Lakana ɲɛmɔgɔba, Zandarama Kɛlɛbolo ɲɛmɔgɔ, Marakɛcogo ɲɛmɔgɔ, Marakɛcogo ɲɛmɔgɔ, Marakɛcogo ɲɛmɔgɔ, Marakɛcogo ɲɛmɔgɔ.
Fɛn bɛɛ bɛ ka ɲi!
Min ye a waleyali ko ye kɛnɛ kan, a bɛ kɛ k’a kɛ koɲuman ye, sirakanboli ɛmɔgɔba, Lala Koyite, ka taama laban dɔ senfɛ, ka kɔlɔsili kɛra ka fɔ la.
k’a kɛ hadamadenya jɛɲɔgɔnw ka fara ɲɔgɔn kan.
O sababu la, Sirabakan ɲɛmɔgɔyama ɲɛmɔgɔba, Lala Koyite, y’a ɲini ka sɔsɔli bɛɛ jira k’a fɔ ko bileta don baarakɛminɛlenw ani mankutu kɛlenw labaarali kan.
Ale ka fɔ la, kɛcogo bilalenw bɛ donfɛn bɛɛ kɔnɔ, minnu ka kan.
Min ye sɛbɛn kɛlenw ye, olu bɛ kɛ waatini kɔnɔ jɔyɔrɔ kuraw la minnu sigira walima minnu sigilen don goni kɔnɔ walasa ka magoɲɛw ɲɛnabɔ.
Nin sɛbɛn ninnu bɛ kɛ baarakɛla tɔgɔtigiya, peyazi jɔyɔrɔ sigili, Sirabakan Fanga ɛmɔgɔyaso ka dogo kan yaasa k’a tiɲɛtigiya jigifa.
Mmu Lala Koyite y’a hakililatigɛ ko sɛbɛn namaralenw tɛ yen, k’a kɔdon kunnafoniw ma, minnu bɛ sirakanna, wa ko sɛbɛn namaralenw bɛna senbɔ sirakɛbɔ la, ni sɛbɛn namaralenw kɛli bɛna sɔrɔ kabini.
Ola, ko bɛɛ bɛɛ ɲɛ ka ɲi sisan waati la!
Burama Keyita - A kɔrɔ ye Bamakɔ dugu yɔrɔw yɛlɛmani kɛjɔyɔrɔ kelen, min bɛ na segin ka na, labɛnni ye.
Nin kelenyatɔn, min bɛna sigi Sanankɔroba komini kɔnɔ, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la Sinmina, bɛna Bamakɔ belebele don sigidajamaw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ hukumu kɔnɔ.
Bamakɔ Disiriki mɛri, Adama Sangare, ani SAYƐRI Kɔnɔkulu Jaje ɲɛmɔgɔ n’a bɛ fɔ a ma Amadu Sankare, dugujukɔrɔfɛnw, kuranko ani jiko minisiri, Lamini Seyidu Tarawore, ka ɲɛsinnen kɔnɔ, ye bolonɔbila kɛ, alamisadon zuwɛnkalo tile 17, tɛmɛnen, Radisson Kolatigɛli la, bolodiɲɔgɔnma sɛbɛn, min bɛ tali kɛ baarabolodali la ani minɛni na, jɛkulu kɛlɛli baarabolodali kan, min bɛ tali kɛ min na,
Mɔgɔba caman tun bɛ yen, E2S Energy Sɔrɔli Sɔrɔtigi, SAYƐRI Kulu tɔnden sigidajama dɔ, baarabolodali latigɛbaga, Fode Ibarahima Magiraga ani Sanankɔrɔba mɛri bɛ minnu cɛla.
Nin jɛɲɔgɔnya kura, min bolonɔbilala Disiriki Miriya ani Kuranko ɲɛnabɔli SEYƐSI E2ƐSI kɔnɔ, kɔnɔ, bɛ kɛ Bamakɔ dugu yɔrɔjɔyɔrɔ yɛlɛmani yɔrɔ sigili ye.
Nin baarabolodali, min b’a ɲini ka jɛkulu, min bɛ yen, ka se kologɛlɛya, siga t’a la, o bɛ ŋaniya jira famaw ɲɛmɔgɔw fɛ, ka dɔ fara ɲɔgɔn kan, ka dɔ fara ɲɔgɔn kan, jama ka hɛrɛ kama.
O kosɔn, SEYƐSIYE mɛri, Adama Bɛrethe, ye wele bila cakɛdaw jɔyɔrɔtigiw ma, minnu ka baaraw kɛli bɛ minnu bolo, ka magan si bali, yaasa laɲiniw, minnu ɲininen don ka tɛmɛ nin bolonɔbila fɛ, ka tiɲɛ sɔrɔ.
A ka baarabolodali jira k’a fɔ, E2S ɛmɔgɔ, Fode Ibarahima Magiraga, y’a dantigɛ ko a baarabolodali laɲini ye ka dɛmɛ kɛ Bamakɔ Disiriki fɛnjɔnw ɲɛnabɔli gɛlɛya ɲɛnabɔ ani k’a hakililatigɛ ko fɛnjɔnw ye fɛn faraɲɔgɔn kan min bɛ a ka dɛmɛni na galabu feere la Mali kɔnɔ.
Nin kelenyatɔn, min bɛna bila Sanankɔroba komini kɔnɔ, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la Sinmina, bɛna Bamakɔ belebele don jɛrɛjɛkuluw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ hukumu kɔnɔ.
Ale ka fɔ la, nin kelenyatɔn bɛna tɛrɛ / ZI bɔ ɲɔgɔnna 1500 ɲɔgɔnna yaasa ka MW 40 bɔ.
A ka waleyali musakaw b’a jate ka kɛ SEFAWARI miliyari 130 ye, a bɛna baaraw, jɛlenw ani jɛlenw na, 6000 sɔrɔ.
SAYƐRI Kɔnɔkulu ɲɛmɔgɔba, Jaje n’a bɛ fɔ a ma Amadu Sankare, y’a pereperelatigɛ ko Sanankɔroba ka sugandili ka nin kelen don, o tun tɛ kun ye.
Bawo, a ka fɔ la, a ka surun nɛgɛsira fɛ Gine – Sikaso – Bamako ani o min bɛ fɔ a ma Bukili Kɛɲɛkaya.
dɔ bɔli min bɛ sɔrɔ EYƐDƐMU ka bɔlɔlɔ sanfɛ, o bɛna nɔgɔya ka tɛmɛ bɛɛ kan.
Yaan’a k’a dantigɛ ko lamini lakana bɛ kɛ mɔgɔ durɔn de ye, nin baaraboloda waleyali la, ka tɛmɛ bɔliw ɲɛnabɔli fɛ ani fɛɛrɛ minnu bɛ don nin kama.
A labanna ka wele bila bɛɛ ka wulikajɔ la, baarabolodali ɲɛni ɲuman kama, jamana ka nafa bakuruba kama.
Nin yɔrɔbaarakɛyɔrɔ labɛnni bɛna dɛmɛ kɛ kosɛbɛ Bamakɔ dugu lasaniya la.
Kuma kelen na, ka Bamakɔ kɛ dugu yɛrɛbakun ye.Disiriki mɛri, Adama Sangare, ka fɔ la, hakilinaw tɛ ban o siratigɛ la, nka Jamana ŋaniya an’a bilasirali de bɛ dɛsɛ tuma bɛɛ.
Yaan’a k’a nisɔndiya sɛbɛnfura in bolodiɲɔgɔnma sɛbɛnfura la a ka meri ani E2ƐSI cɛ, walasa ka walankatalenw yɛlɛmani baarakɛyɔrɔ sigi ni fɛn ye.
A laban na, a y’a ɲini bɛɛ ka bilasirali kɛ, baaraboloda ɲɛni kama.
AMTure - Nin y’a siɲɛ fɔlɔ ye, SEYƐSIYA ɲɔgɔnye bɛ kɛ Kidali, sifilɛli caman kɔfɛ.
A kɛra Alizeri kɔkankow minisiri, SE Sabiri Bukadumu, ka ɲɛmɔgɔya kɔnɔ, bɛnɲini minisiri, Kolonɛli Isimayɛli Wage ani Gɔfɛrɛnaman mɔgɔ wɛrɛw, Pilatifɔrɔmu ani SEMA marifatigi kuluw tɔgɔlamɔgɔw ɲɛna.
Minisima tɔgɔlamɔgɔ a ɲɔgɔnye la ye foli kɛ ni ɲɔgɔnsamasama ani ɲɔgɔnsamasama ye Mali fan fɛ ani diɲɛ fɔkabɛn fan fɛ.
S.E.M. Zan Iwi - Drian, Faransi Jamana ka Erɔpu ani Jamana kɔkankow minisiri ani Afiriki Faraɲɔgɔnkanjɛkulu Bɛn ani Lakana Komisɛri, S.E.E.M. Salifu Sɛrigi, y’a ɲini k’a sen don baaraw la viziyokɔnferansi, Mahamati Salehi Annatifu, Diɲɛtɔnba Sekeretɛri zenerali Tɔgɔlamɔgɔ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen, y’a fɔ a ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kɔfɛ ko « a bɛ san duuru kɔnɔ n bɛ SEYƐSIYA la, wa nin y’a siɲɛ fɔlɔ
O b’a jira k’a fɔ ko diɲɛmɔgɔ bɛɛ bɛ dɛmɛ kɛ Mali la ani a labɛnnen don ka Mali bilasira nin dakun kura wa danaya de bɛ sinsin, politiki ŋaniya yɛrɛ-yɛrɛ de bɛ kɛ min ye ».
Min ye Kolonɛli - mazɔri Isimayeli Wage ta ye, Jamana Bɛnɲini minisiri, a y’a da tulow kan ko « danaya hakilina, ɲɔgɔn faamuyali ka bɔ a fɔlɔ la, ka ko dɔw bɛɛ faamuya.
Ola, jɔda b’a la k’a jate ko a latigɛra ko Mali fan bɛ to ka danaya kokɛtaw kologɛlɛya ni wale kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw ye, ka ɲɛtaa lakana koɲɛw kan ani ka Sirabakanbɛn dilan, min sigira bɛɛ ka ɲɛsin mɔgɔw ma, yaasa an ka se ka ɲɛsin o kan tiɲɛ na, ni ka gɛlɛyaw don ba la, bɛɛ ka ɲɛsin mɔgɔw ma cogo min ».
Mohamɛdi Lamini Ulidi Sidadat bolo, SEMA waleyali perezidan, « an ye baara kɛ Malidenw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
A labɛnni kɛra ni Kidali marabolo gɔfɛrɛnɛri ye, wa Malidenw de ye nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛ labɛn, an Malidenw de tun bɛ lakana ».
« SEYƐSIYA taara yɔrɔ o y’a siɲɛ fɔlɔ, nin waatilabaara Kidali marabolo kɔnɔ, siga t’a la, ye bɛn, bɛnɲini taamasiyɛn Mali denw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
Nin waatilabaara bɛ bɛn kɛbagaw bɛɛ ka ŋɛnɛya seereya di Mali kɔnɔ », Habala AƐSI Hamizata, pilatifɔrɔmu ka kumalasela y’o ɲɛfɔ.
« Ka Mali bandari ye ka don Kidali dugu kan kokura, o ye dusukunnako ye, o ye dusukunnako ye anw fɛ.
Malidenw bɛɛ jɛlen don ni wale in ye ka taa yɛrɛminɛni kura fanfɛ Mali la », Kolonɛli Modibo Kone, Lakana ani Sigidalamɔgɔw ka Lakana minisiri,
SEYƐSIYA wulilen ka waatilabaara ka kan k’a ɲɛsin DEDEYƐRI taabolo ma, fangabulonkow yɛlɛmaniw sennateliya, dɔwɛrɛw cɛla.
An ka hakilijigin kɛ ko, Jamana bɛ sigibagaw fanba b’a ɲini ka Bɛnkansɛbɛn bɛn kama kalan kura ye.
Berehima JALO - Jamana ntolatan mɔgɔbaw bɛna a ka teriyantolatan sabanan ani laban ntolatan kɛ, k’a sababu kɛ FIFA donw ye ( zuwɛn 2021 ) ka sin Tinizi ma.
A ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn bɛ na kɛ tarata zuwɛnkalo tile 15 Aradi Hamadi Agrebi tɔgɔla ntolancifɛɛrɛ la.
O ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn dira Misiraw ka jalatigɛli trio dɔ ma.
Jalatigɛla cɛmancɛ, Ibarahima Nuredine, bɛna dɛmɛ kɛ a fasodenɲɔgɔnw, Ahmɛdi Tafufi ani Hani Abedɛli Fata fɛ.
Jalatigɛla nɔnabila bɛna kɛ Tinizi Yusiri Buali ye.
Dɛsɛli kɔfɛ Alizeri ( 0 – 1 ), zuwɛnkalo tile 6, teriyantolatan ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn fɔlɔ senfɛ, ntolatan nulɛli ƐRIDE Kɔngo kan (1 – 1 ), jumadon tɛmɛnen, Tinizi, Mali Samatasɛgɛw bɛna ɲini k’u yɛrɛ yɛrɛ lasɔrɔ ɲɛsin Tinizi musolakaw ma.
Sugandili wɛrɛ tɛ Mohamɛdi Maguba cɛw bolo ni sebaaya tɛ.
Nin ntolatan senfɛ, Tinizi sen bɛ na kɛ ntolatanna ɲɛmɔgɔ caman bolo, i n’a fɔ Yusɛfu Makani, Ferjan Sasi, Dylan Brɔnni walima Wahibi Kazi.
Wɛrɛdon tɛmɛnen, Samatasɛgɛw ye ntolatan foyi kɛ ka sin ƐRIDE Kɔngo Leopariw ma (1-1).
A daminɛna kɔfɛjɔ dɔ kɔfɛjɔw bolo minnu tun tɛ yen, n’a ta bɛɛ, ƐFISE Nantes kɛbaga, Kalifa Kulibali, ye daminɛni jaabi dayɛlɛ Samatasɛgɛw ( miniti 4nan ).
A labɛnnen kologɛlɛyala, jamana mɔgɔbaw ye ntolan dɔrɔn, nk’a ma se ka wari hakɛ fila sɔrɔ.
Tako filanan waati kɔnɔ, Kasɔnbuya, kolatigɛla Kɔnsɔrɔ la, de tun bɛ sojɔminɛnw kisi Dunbiya ( miniti 55nan ).
Fan laban na Lewopariw tun bɛ ka wuli ka taa ɲɔgɔn na, ni laban na u ye mugu ci Akolo fɛ, o min tiɲɛnna Munkɔrɔ fɛ.
Nka,Raja Casablanka kɛbaga, Bɛni Malango, tun labanna ka ntolatan nulɛbɔ, n’a kɛtɔ ye ka Kutu Sami ( miniti 86nan ) bugɔ a ɲɛ kan.
Usumani KAMARA - A nisɔndiyalenw ani minnu bɛ hami nin cɛmancɛlafanga waati ɲɛni ɲuman na, min ye Mali fasojama ka laɲiniba ye, Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ, Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Sogɛli Kokala Mayiga, ye taamaw suguya caman kɛ, kabini waati dɔ la, a ka perezidanw fɛ.
O la, arabadon zuwɛnkalo tile 23 san 2021, a kɛra Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Bubu Sise ka goti ye.
Mali bolo, foyi si tɛ foyi ye!
Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Sogɛli K. Mayiga ka taama, minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ, gɔfɛrɛnaman kuntigi, ka bɔ Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Bubu Sise fɛ, minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ, ye o taamasiyɛn ɲuman ye.
O la, arabadon zuwɛnkalo tile 23 san 2021, Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Sogɛli K. Mayiga, a ka badenyataamaw hukumu kɔnɔ, janko PEYƐMU kɔrɔw fɛ, bisimila Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Bubu Sise fɛ, k’a kuma tɛ dɔwɛrɛ ye ni Mali tɛ.
Cɛ, min si bɛ san 28 la, n’a sɔrɔla k’a ye nin gɛmisɛn di Jamana kuntigi ma, jama ka lajɛrɛ senfɛ, o minɛnna.
Fo ka taa kiriso cakɛdaw dɔnnen, Damiyɛn Tarɛli fana ɲangira ni baara walima degelibaara wajibiyali ye ani marifabila kɛli san duuru kɔnɔ.

Faransi Blu ka fɔ la, nin na kɛ ka kɛ dague kelen, kalama kelen ani maramafɛn senbɔli ye.
Maramafɛn nafamafɛnw tun sɔrɔla kaban mɔgɔ sigibaga jɔnjɔn, Damiyɛni T. fɛ, min ye Jamana perezidan gɛlɛya, jama ka badenyata dɔ senfɛ taratadon o tɛmɛnen kɔ Tɛnni-Lɛrɛmitazi la.
Aritɛri S. bɛna wele bila kiriso la, san 2022 tilancɛ filanan laban kama, ka jaabili kɛ sariyasɔsɔw la, minnu sirilen don maramafɛnw kan, minnu sɔrɔla sariyasɔsɔ kɔnɔ, Jamana lafasasariyatigi Alɛki Peririn y’o pereperelatigɛ.
Sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛlen fɔlɔw ka fɔ la, Damiyɛni T. ye mɔgɔw bɛɛ ka tariku kɔnɔmɔgɔ ye, min bɛ masurunnamɔgɔyasira kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen tɛmɛ bɔlɔlɔ barokɛyɔrɔw kan, nka mɔgɔ b’a fɔ ko ale tɛ politikikow ani ɲangata tɛ a ka bɛɛjɛkulu kɔnɔ.
A sigira Sɛn-Waliɛri ( Doromi ) la, a ka sigiyɔrɔ ye, tɔn fila, Erɔpu tarikulakɛlɛkɛbagaw kɔnɔ.
Kɛlɛw kɛli minnu tilenna ɲinɛ na, ni baarakɛlaw 1500 de bɛ Faransi kɔnɔ.

Nin ɲɔgɔnye ye Afiriki ni Erɔpu jamana lasigiden caman ka donni ye.
inini fila kɔfɛ san 2019 ani san 2020, nin siɲɛ kɛra a ɲuman ye.
Alamisadon, feburuyekalo tile 11, san 2021,
Alize bɛnkansɛbɛn kɔfɛ, a y’a ka ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kunfɔlɔ kɛ Kidali, bilasirali fila kɔfɛ ani cɛfɔli caman kɛlen kɔ fan bolonɔbilali fanw cɛ, fan kelen fɛ ani fan wɛrɛ fɛ, ɲɛmɔgɔ kuraw, minnu y’u ka ŋaniya jira ɲuman na, nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kɛli kama.
SEYƐSIYA ɲɔgɔnye, min taara Bamakɔ kɔnɔ, ye farafina ni Erɔpu jamanaw caman ka lasigidenw kɛnɛ kan, minnu cɛla Tilebinya fanga tɔgɔlamɔgɔw, i n’a fɔ Faransi ani Ameriki, ani fana ONI tɔgɔlamɔgɔ Mali la, nka nin SEYƐSIYA ɲɔgɔnye sanfɛla 5nan kofɔlen ye Faransi jamana kɔkankow minisiri ka sen donni ye, min ye baara kɛ viziyokɔnferansi fɛ ani min ye SEYƐSIYA ɲɔgɔnye mankutura Kidali ni taamasiyɛbɛn ye.
Farafina Kelenyatɔn Bɛn ani Lakana Komisɛri fana tun bɛ yen.
Nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn senfɛ, ɲininkali koɲɛw bɛɛ tun bɛ kumafalenw tabali kan, k’a bɛn Kidali sariya ma, min tolen don halibi koɲɛ kɛnɛkɛnɛ ye, DEDEYƐRI ( Maramafɛnbila, Senbɔli kɛlɛ la, Bolo donni kura ) ka gɛlɛya.
Bɛnɲini minisiri, Kolonɛli Isimayeli Wage ye da kɛnɛ kan ko bi, ka tɛmɛ 400 kan kɔgɔduguyanfan marabolow kɔrɔkɛlɛdenw bɛ degeliyala la ka don Mali Kɛlɛbolo sen don, n’olu bɛ fɔ a ma ko maramafɛntigiw, minnu labɛnna kokura.
A kuma fɔra fana hadamadenya sigibaju baaradaw seginni kan Kidali o siratigɛ la Minisima y’a latigɛ ka tɛgɛ bila dogoyɔrɔ la walasa ka nin baarabolodali wari miliyɔn kelen na.
A ko, min ye nin SEYƐSIYA ɲɔgɔnye sanfɛyɔrɔ in taamasiyɛn Kidali, o ye jamana kolow yɛlɛnni ye dugu kan kabini kalo damadɔ.
An ka hakilijigin kɛ ko Mali darapo wulila ka taa Kidali dugu kan IBEKA ka fanga kɔnɔ Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ Bubu Sise ka taama tuma na.
Usumani M. Tarawore - Mali gɔfɛrɛnaman ye jɛɲɔgɔn kun ye Bedegɔlidi bolo, a ka ɲɛmɔgɔ ka fɔ la Mali la, Wili Bili Litili, ka fɔ la.
Bedegɔlidi Mali ɲɛmɔgɔ, Wiliya Bili Litili, n’a ka baarakɛjama ye kunnafonidilajɛ labɛn, zuwɛnkalo tile 14, dugujukɔrɔfɛnw cakɛda daga la, walasa ka san 2020 bakurubajate kɛ, ka gɛlɛyaw kofɔ, yanni a ka ko nataw fɔ.
Bili Litili ka fɔ la, sɔrɔko sebagaya ɲɛni san 2020 na, nafa sera tɔnden waribɔlaw ma ani fan caman mɔgɔ wɛrɛ minnu sen b’a la Mali la, a y’o dantigɛ.
Bedegɔlidi ye sefawari miliyari 34 ɲɔgɔnna saraw ani baarakɛlaw ka hadamadenya nafalafɛnw la, miliyari 162 gɔfɛrɛnaman ye, sigidajamaw ka yiriwalinafolobɔ miliyari 2,1 ɲɔgɔn ani fɛnw minɛnenw ye 82 ɲɔgɔnna Mali la.
San 2020 kɔnɔ, Fekola daman ye sanu ɔnsi 622 000 bɔ.
San 2021 kalosaba fɔlɔ kɔnɔ, Fekola daman tɛmɛna a ka sebagayaw waleyaliw ɲumanw fɛ, ni sanu ɔnsi 125 088 bɔli ye, k’a bɛn 7% ( 0888) ma, ka tɛmɛ ɲɛsigilen kan.

Mamadu TOGOLA / maliweb.net - Kɔlɔsili, min kɛra Kɛlɛsikɛbɛnikɛlaba ( BEWEZE ) fɛ, Buguni dugubakɔnɔkomini mɛiriyɔrɔ la ( KUBU ) la, zanwiye tile 1 san 2017 waati kɔnɔ ka taa bila desanburukalo tile 31 san 2019.
Komini baarakɛkulu ka tɔn gabakɛyɔrɔ ye, san fila ɲɛnabɔli kɔnɔ, bugɔli ye min ka ca ni Sefa wari miliyon 208 ye (Sefa wari miliyon 208 33 717 ) la, k’a kɛ Komini ka kɛsu kɔnɔ.

Wa n’o ma kɛ, an k’an senbɔ an ka mɛri bɛɛ mɔgɔba la, min ye Buguni dugubakɔnɔmɔgɔw ka meri gɛlɛya kɔnɔ.

Ka da an kumakɛɲɔgɔnw na, a bɛ na gɛlɛya sɔrɔ.
Wa bi, ko gɛlɛn ka gɛlɛn.
Kow tiɲɛniw la. K’a ta zanwiye 2017 la ka taa desanburukalo 2019 la, an kumakɛɲɔgɔnw b’a ɲɛfɔ, Mɛri Buguni, Mamuru Kulibali n’a ka tɔn ka farikoloɲɛnajɛ fɛn kɛlen kɔrɔ kɛra baarakɛnasariyatigi ye, min y’a yɛrɛ yɛlɛma ni gabakɛda ye.
A gafew sigibaju kan, baarakɛla dɔ b’a ɲɛfɔ Mayiri ka kɔnɔna kɔlɔsilikɛdaga labɛnni tiɲɛni.
A bɛ fara a kan, fɛnw minnu bɔra DAWO feere la ( A ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw weleyali baarakɛla ) k’a se bakuruba la sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 950 000 hakɛ la ani kalankɛtaaraw saraw, minnu tɛ yen Buguni Komini kɔnɔ, k’a se bakuruba la sefawari miliyon 126,7 hakɛ la (126 712 156 hakɛ la ).
Fɛn wɛrɛw, minnu sɔrɔla Buguni Miriya ɲɛnabɔli kɔnɔ, fɛn kɛnɛkɛnɛkɛnɛw yɛlɛmali kɛcogoya dɔrɔn, k’a bɔ an ka sefawari miliyon 53 ma (Sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 53 ani sefawari minnu sɔrɔlen t’a la ka sefawari miliyon 10 (Sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 10 ani sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 24 ).
Wa ɲɛfɛn min bɛ tile bɔ an ka kunnafonisunw ka fɔ la, o ye ko Buguni mɛri, Mamuru Kulibali, bɛ nafalafɛnw sɔrɔ a yɛrɛ la, ni sefawari miliyon 3,8 ( Sefawari 3 875 000 ) bakuruba ye.
Bloki kɔnɔ, Buguni Miriya baarakɛlaw y’a da kɛnɛ kan ko tiɲɛniw, minnu sɔrɔla komini tɔn mara kɔnɔ, ye sariya ani baarasariya sɔrɔ.
O bɛ fara a kan, nafolokow kɛcogoya juguw nafolokow ɲɛnabɔli la.
Wa an kumakɛɲɔgɔnw tɛmɛna k’a jira k’a fɔ ko Miriya ka marakɛcogo baarakɛbagaw danfaralenw t’u jɔyɔrɔw an’u jɔyɔrɔtigiyaw hakililatigɛ pewu, fɛn min bɛ fɛn ɲininenw lasɔrɔli ma.
O la, dɛsɛ, minnu lakɔlɔsi fasodenya ɲɛnabɔli hukumu kɔnɔ, bɛ Buguni gɔfɛrɛnaman bali ka se ka kɛ ni baaraw ye fasodenw ye.
Min ye so ani dugukolo ɲɛnabɔli ko ye, an ka kunnafonisunw b’a da kɛnɛ kan ko Buguni Miriya ma baaraw kɛ, minnu ka kan, walasa ka laɲiniw sɔrɔ, minnu bɛ di a ma, kɛcogoya kɔnɔ, fasodenw kunnafoni ni jogoɲumanya tuma min na, dugukolow bolonkɔnɔni tuma.
Lakanatigilamɔgɔw layiriwali baarakɛcogo dɛsɛli bɛ KUBE ka baarakɛjama labaarali bali.
Wa bi, fɛnko-fɛnko-fɛnko-fɛnko, i n’a fɔ a bɛ yen Buguni Miriya la, tɛ kɛnɛ kan, k’a kun kɛ gafe jɔnjɔnw tɛni ye, walasa k’a hakililatigɛ fɛn kɔlɔsili an’u lakana.
Ka da an kumakɛɲɔgɔnw ka dantigɛlenw na, Buguni Komini ka kolatigɛjɛkulu ye fɛn ɲumanw di Mɛri Mamuru Kulibali ma, sigida biro mɔgɔw, sigidajama baarakɛlaw, baarakɛta baarakɛjɛkuluw mɔgɔw ani dɛmɛniw ma, fɛn ɲuman dɔw ma, minnu cɛsirilen don Jamana fɛɛrɛ la.
Wa an ka kunnafonisunw ka hakililatigɛ.
Buguni meri fɛ, Sɛgɛsɛgɛlikɛla y’a lakɔlɔsi ko Komini ka kolatigɛjɛkulu ye nafamafɛnw dɔ di minnu na, nafolokow dɛmɛni kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw ani nafamafɛnw dɔw bɛ minnu na.
O nafamafɛnw sɔrɔbagaw ye,
Mɛri, sigida biro mɔgɔw, sigida ciyakɛda baarakɛlaw ani baarakɛta fɛɛrɛtigiw mɔgɔw.
Yanni a ka pereperelatigɛ.
San 2010 zuwɛnkalo tile 28 Cakɛda ɛmɔgɔyasɛbɛn n° 005 / SEYƐSEBE kɔfɛ, Mɛri Mamuru Kulibali ye san 2017 mɛkalo tile 29 baara ɛmɔgɔyasɛbɛn n° 06 / KUBU ta, min bɛ tali kɛ Musakatigi ani Biletɛri ma walasa ka Mɛri ka dɛmɛ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen kelen waleya.
O la, saratiwaati kɛra sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 25 000 na kalo kelen, Mɛri tɔgɔ la, min kɔnɔ sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 24 000 ye nafoloko dɛmɛ kɛ ani sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 24 000, walasa ka Mɛri ka galabu ani talifoni musakaw ta ba la.
A dun tɛ nin nafamafɛnw ɲɛsigilen don baarasariya fɛ, min bɛ senna.
A wari hakɛ bakuruba, min sara Mɛri la, a kalanni waati kɔnɔ, bɛ sɔrɔ sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 3 170 000 na.
Fan wɛrɛ fɛ, an ka kunnafonisunw b’a fara a kan ko Buguni Miriya ka sɔrɔbɔw musakatigi ma segin ka na fɛnw minnu bɔra a feere la, ka bɔ forobasɛbɛn na ( DAWO ) la.
K’an ka sefawari miliyon 1,8 mumɛ kɔnɔ (1 850 000), sɛgɛsɛgɛli baarakɛjɛkulu ma seginni seereyaw sɔrɔ fo ka sefawari miliyon 900 000 hakɛ la.
DAWO feerew, minnu ma segin ka na, mumɛ hakɛ ye Sefa wari miliyɔn 950 000 ye.
Wa o tɛ bɛɛ ye.
Fo ka se ka kɛ.
Buguni yɛrɛmarakafo « Mɛri Mamuru Kulibali » kelen tɛ ɲangiliw waleya suguw kan, minnu waleyali bɛ tile kɔnɔ.
O cogo la, sugufiyɛbagaw n°046 / KUBEYƐNKI – DEYƐSIPE SIK 2018 minnu bɛ tali kɛ sojɔso saba ( 3 ) labɛnni baaraw ye.
Biro ni kunnafonidisɛbɛn dilalen dɔ fɛ, jɛkulu fila ( 2 ), latɛrin saba, Jalanikɔrɔ lakɔliw la, Hɛrɛmakɔnɔ Kɔgɔdugu Bɛnkansɛbɛn kɔnɔ, Buguni dugubakɔnɔna komini kɔnɔ.
ani n°047/ KUB DEYƐRIPE – DEYƐSIPE SIK 2018 min bɛ tali kɛ Duguninina, Hɛrɛmakɔnɔko Sɛnɛri ani Masablakura SEYƐSIKƐMUW kalanso kologɛlɛyɔrɔ baaraw la Buguni dugubakɔnɔna komini kɔnɔ, ye bɛnkansɛbɛn waatiw tɛmɛn, kasɔrɔ Mɛtiri Mamuru ma mɛnni ɲangiliw waleya.
Nin ɲangaliw, minnu ma waleya, bɛ fara sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 8 162 130 (miliyon mugan ni naani ani ba kɛmɛ ni naani ani kɛmɛ naani ani kɛmɛ naani ani kɛmɛ naani ani kɛmɛ naani ani kɛmɛ naani ani kɛmɛ naani ani kɛmɛ naani ani kɛmɛ naani ) kan.
O waati kɔnɔ, an ka kunnafonisunw y’a dajira ko sɛgɛsɛgɛli baarakɛkulu ye hakilinaw fɛsɛgɛli, minnu bɛ tali kɛ fɛsɛfɛsɛgɛli ani saraw yɛlɛmali, Buguni dugubakɔnɔna kɔnɔ, mara kɔntiw, wari sɛbɛnw kunnafonidisɛbɛnw ani juru bɛnkansɛbɛnw na.
Kumaw bɔlenw na, a bɛ ye k’a fɔ ko nafolokow baarakɛjɛkulu perezidan ye sɔrɔ minɛ, k’a kɛ a yɔrɔ an’a jɔyɔrɔ ye, Dugujukɔrɔ kɔrɔ yamaruyasɛbɛnw sɔrɔ.
O cogo de la, a ka sɛgɛsɛgɛli waati kɔnɔ, sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 5 130 000 hakɛ kan, min sɔrɔla bɔlɔlɔw la, nafolokow ɲɛnabɔli baarakɛjɛkulu Peresidan ye sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 650 000 wɛrɛ bila sɔrɔw marabolo la, o kɔfɛ a ye sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 1 130 000 hakɛ lase, sɛgɛsɛgɛli baarakɛkulu tɛmɛlen kɔfɛ.
Kiriyɔrɔw hakɛ bakuruba, minnu ma wari bila nafolokow ɲɛnabɔli baarakɛjɛkulu Peresidan fɛ, tɛmɛna miliyon 4 ( SEFAWARI 4 020 000 ) ye.
Grotɛkow dɔw. A gabakɛ, min bɛ senna Buguni Miriya la, tɛmɛna a hakilina kan.
O la, an kumakɛɲɔgɔnw b’a ɲɛfɔ ko Buguni Dantigɛli Akademi ɛmɔgɔ ye, cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya cogoya.
O cogo la, sɛgɛsɛgɛli baarakɛkulu y’a lakɔlɔsi ko, saraw kɛcogow kan, minnu sɔrɔla Kalanso Akademi fɛ, Buguni Mɛri, Mamuru Kulibali, ye Jamana Tɔnw kalankuluw kalankɛbagaw ka saraw sarali ɲɛnabɔ, minnu y’u yɛlɛma ka bɔ a ka Komini kɔnɔ, kasɔrɔ sariyasunbaaraw doni tɛmɛna.
A wari hakɛ bakuruba, min sara, fɛsɛfɛsɛli waati kɔnɔ, b’a la ka tɛmɛ an ka sefawari miliyon 126 kan (SEFAWARI dɔrɔmɛ 162 625).
Wa ni nafoloko kɛcogoya ye, sɛgɛsɛgɛlikɛla baarakɛkulu y’a da tulow kan ko Buguni Miriya ka sɔrɔta sɔrɔbaga tɛ dugukolo yɛlɛmali yamaruyasɛbɛn dɔ labato, min sigilen don fɛsɛfɛsɛliw kɔnɔ, a jateminɛ waati kɔnɔ.
O la, sɛgɛsɛgɛlikɛlaw ka sɛgɛsɛgɛli kunkurunni kɔfɛ, bugunatigɛw, waati kɛnɛkɛnɛkɛnɛw tali kɛsɛfɛsɛgɛli kɔfɛsɛgɛw ani hakilijakabɔw ani wari hakɛw siratigɛli kɔfɛ, minnu bɛ kɛ bugunatigɛlaw la dantigɛlenw na, bɛ ye kɛnɛ kan ko Buguni Miri ka wari hakɛ sɔrɔtigi ye, k’a jira k’a fɔ kɛnɛkɛnɛ yɛlɛma dɔw ye, wari minnu bɛ dɔgɔya la ka se hakɛ min ma.
Dɔbɔliw hakɛ bakurubajate bɛɛ, danfara min kɛra dɔgɔyaba fɛ, min sigira hakililatigɛliw fɛ, an’a wari hakɛw cɛla, minnu bilala Wari hakɛ sɔrɔbaga fɛ, san 2018 ani san 2019 baarasow kɔnɔ, ye sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 24 479 750 ye.
I n’a fɔ o tun tɛ bɔli kɛ, kɛnɛnkɛnɛnnenya yɛlɛmali wɛrɛw kama 2018 ani san 2019 sanu na, sɔrɔta si ma lakodɔn, k’a wari hakɛ mumɛ tɛmɛ miliyon 29 kan ( SEFAWARI dɔrɔmɛ 29 000 ).
Wari hakɛ mumɛ minnu ma wari sɔrɔ bɛɛ hakɛ ye sefawari miliyon 53,9 ye (Sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 53 919 725 ).

Zan Piyɛri Jɛmisɛmi - Faciyɔrɔ Mara ani Desantaralizasyɔn Minisiri, Yetenan-Kolonɛli Abudulayi Mayiga ye, san 2021 tarata don, Bamako Foroba lajɛrɛ yɔrɔ la, baaradenya baaraw dayɛlɛ, kalataw ɲɛnabɔli cakɛda kelen sigili la sen kan, cɛmancɛlafanga kalataw kama.
A bɛ kɛbagaw bɛɛ fara ɲɔgɔn kan ( Mara, Paritipolitikiw, Jɛrɛjɛkulu, Jamana ɛmɔgɔbaw ).
Baara kɛlen tile fila kɔnɔ, k’a kɛ mɔgɔ minnu sen bɛ na kɛ kalafiliw ɲɛnabɔli cakɛda kelen pe min bɛ na bila sen kan cɛmancɛlafanga hukumu kɔnɔ bolodalenw ɲɛnabɔli kama.
Hakilijin na, Minisiri Abudulayi Mayiga y’a da tulow kan ko kalataw ɲɛnabɔli cakɛda kelen sigili tɛ bɔ cɛmancɛlafanga sariyaw na, nk’a bɛ fɔ Jamana Kumaɲɔgɔnya bɛɛ sen bɛ min na.
O kosɔn, yetenan-kolonɛli Abudulayi Mayiga ko ten, Gɔfɛrɛnaman ɛmɔgɔ minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ ye kumafalen dayɛlɛ kokura walasa k’a se ka Cɛmancɛlafanga kalata nataw labɛn ni kalataw ɲɛnabɔli cakɛda kelen ye.
O de kosɔn, minisiri Mayiga y’o fara a kan, a y’a jira k’a fɔ ko n ka baaradaba ka politikitɔnw ani jɛrɛjɛkuluw ka fɛn ɲini a koɲɛ kan.
A baaradanin, a ko ten, bɛ bila nin hukumu kɔnɔ.
Walasa k’a politikijɛkuluw ɲɛfɔ a koɲɛ kan, baara tile fila kɔnɔ, Abudulayi Mayiga y’a da kɛnɛ kan ko jirali naani bɛna kɛ.
A fɔlɔ bɛ tali kɛ yɔrɔw kɛcogoya kan, k’a da kalataw ɲɛnabɔli Cakɛda kelenkelen kan (Zemana Mara ani Desantaralizasyɔn Minisiriso).
A filanan bɛ kɛ taamasiyɛnni na, min bɛ tali kɛ kalataw labɛnni na Mali Cɛmancɛlafanga waati la ( Jamana ɛmɔgɔbaw, minnu bɛ tali kɛ ).
Sabanan bɛ tali kɛ kalataw ɲɛnabɔli ciyakɛyɔrɔw koɲɛdonni na Mali la, kalata nataw labɛnni wajibiyalenw an’a cɛsirikow kan kalataw ɲɛnabɔli Cakɛda kelen pe min bɛ bila sen kan ( Jamana ɛmɔgɔba ).
Kuma laban na, a ɲɔgɔnna bɛ sigi ni kalataw koɲɛnabɔli Cakɛda kelen sigili la, kalata nataw labɛnni kama ani fɛɛrɛw minnu bɛ se ka kɛ, kalata taabolo danaya kologɛlɛyali kama.
O kɔfɛ, minisiri Abudulayi Mayiga y’a fɔ k’a yɛrɛ dalen bɛ k’a fɔ ko kumafalenw kɔfɛ, kalataw ɲɛnabɔli Cakɛda kelen sigili koɲɛ bɛna ɲɛnabɔ ni bɛnkan ye.
A y’a kuncɛ ten, ne tun tɛ se ka dan sigi ni fila ani fila bolodiɲɔgɔn fɛɛrɛkow ani nafolokow bolodiɲɔgɔnma kɛbagaw ye ani Mali teriw bɛɛ, u ka kɔkɔrɔdon ani bilasirali kama an ka jamana lakanani, lafiya ani yiriwali kologɛlɛyali la,
Hadama B. Fofana A seginnen a ka bangamara la Mama, Konowari cɛmancɛ ani tilebin na, perezidan kɔrɔ Loran Bagibo y’a ka kiri kofɔ, ntɛnɛndon, diɲɛ ɲangili kiritigɛlaw fɛ.
« Ne tɛ kojugukɛla ye.» Nin y’a siɲɛ fɔlɔ ye kabini a seginnen Konowari, perezidan kɔrɔ Loran Bagibo ye kuma fɔ, ntɛnɛndon zuwɛnkalo tile 28, a ka kiri an’a labili la Diɲɛ kojugukɛrɛba (SEPEYI) fɛ, k’a sɛmɛntiya k’a tun bilala ka taa Lahayi bawo « cɛ gɛlɛya dɔ tun ka kan ka bɔ ɲɔgɔn na ».
« SEPEYI, o tun tɛ sɛbɛ la, cɛ min bɛ mɔgɔ kofɔ, ani ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn min bɛ mɔgɔ kofɔ, o la, olu y’a bila yen », Loran Bagibo y’o dantigɛ Mama, a ka bangamara la, Konowari tilebinyanfan jamana cɛmancɛ la.
Nka, a y’a fara a kan ka bɔ laadaɲɛmɔgɔw, a ka paritiɲɛmɔgɔw an’a ka kunnafonidilaw ɲɛkɔrɔ, « n man nimisa, bawo n n tun seginna ni kojugukɛcogo ye, aw bɛɛ de bɛ na malo sɔrɔ yan ».
Loran Bagibo labila pewu, marisikalo laban, SEYƐPI fɛ, yɔrɔ min na a jalakira kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la ni kojugukɛw ye ka sin diɲɛ ma, o kɛra sababu ye k’a segin Kodiwari.
« Jɛmanw fana, minnu t’an dɔn, minnu bɛ an ka kɛlɛ ncininw kɔfɛ yan, y’a dɔn ko ne ( tun tɛ ) tun tɛ kojugukɛ ye.
Ne bɛɛ kɛ, ɲɛ, nka ne tɛ kojugukɛla ye », Loran Bagibo y’o sɛmɛntiya dɛmɛninw kɔrɔ.
A tun b’a fɔ ni laadalaɲɛmɔgɔw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ ɲɔgɔn cɛ ɲɔgɔn cɛ ɲɔgɔn cɛ ɲɔgɔn cɛ ɲɔgɔn cɛ ɲɔgɔn cɛ ɲɔgɔn cɛ, minnu donna a la ni « bɛnɲini » ci ye.
« Bɛnɲini dafalen » « A yeli de tun bɛ kɛnɛ kan an tun sigilen bɛ ka bɛnɲini kama.
Fo a ka kan k’i sinsin a ka jama kan yaasa ka Konowari fasojama wele bɛɛ ka bɛnɲini kama ɲuman », Jozefu Goli Obu, Mama ka « dugukolow kuntigi » y’o dantigɛ AYƐFIPE ye, sigida ɲɛmɔgɔba dɔ, min lamɛnnen don mɔgɔba dɔw fɛ.
O laadalaɲɛmɔgɔw ka kan fana ka don ɲɛnajɛ la min na k’a « purifayɛ » cogo min, i n’a fɔ a ka jamana laadala b’a fɛ cogo min nɔnabila mɔgɔ ye ani min bilala kaso la.
« Taradon, n bɛna a lasɔrɔ, n bɛna a ɲini a fɛ k’a to bɛnɲini baara la, a ka kuma fɔlɔw ka taa jamana ma bɛnɲini siratigɛ la », « dugukolow kuntigi » y’o sɛmɛntiya, a kɛtɔla k’a sɛmɛntiya k’a ka saratiwaati kɛ a mɔgɔw fɛ nin ɲɛnajɛ kama.
« Jama belebele kɔnɔ, tuma min na du mɔgɔ dɔ bɔra gɛlɛya dɔ la, mɔgɔw b’a lasɔrɔ.
O de kɔrɔ ye k’a yɛlɛma a ka da kɛnɛ kan sɔgɔmada jona fɛ, yanni sankɔrɔtalen ɲɛ, ni bɔli ye kɛnɛ kan k’a bɛ tali kɛ ni Kpobarawi ani Titawi laadaw ye », san saba ɲɛmɔgɔ y’o ɲɛfɔ.
Mama forobakɛnɛ kan, dugu sigibagaw y’a makɔnɔni makɔnɔ, k’a to perezidandan kɔrɔ ka kuma filɛ u la, ni k’a tan ni k’a kɛ.
« Bagibo tara walasa ka lafiya lasɔrɔ jamana kɔnɔ », Brigite Kudu, min bɔra Zebizeku dugunin mɔgɔw fɛ, y’o fɔ.
« Ne nisɔndiyara, nin don in ye kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye.
Perezidan Bagibo kannabilalen don.
Mɔgɔ b’a kan k’a mɛn, a k’a fɔ kuma kelen durɔn », Beyatisi Jedeje, min bɔra Kpakeku, y’o fɔ a bolo, « bɛn ani bɛnɲini » taamasiyɛnnen dɔ de b’a bolo.
Mɔgɔ ba caman ye sebagaya bɔli kɛ a ye, karidon, Mama, tile tan a seginnen kɔ Abijan.
Seginni, min ma kɛ gɛlɛya si ye, k’a kɔdon a nali ma, zuwɛnkalo tile 17 Abijan, n’a taamasiyɛnna ni caman cɛjɔyɔrɔw ye, lakanakɛbagaw ani a kanuɲɔgɔnw cɛ, minnu tun bɛ fɛ k’a lasɔrɔ pankulu kɔrɔ.
Loran Bagibo, min tun bɛ fanga la kabini 2000 fanga la, tun minɛna awirili 2011 Abijan, o kɔfɛ kalo wolonfila bila ka taga SEPEYI la, yaasa k’a kiri ka taa ɲangataw la, san 2010 perezidansigikalata laban kɔfɛ.
A banni ka jɔ a ka dɛsɛli la, Alasani Watara ɲɛkɔrɔ, tun ye kalata kɔkan gɛlɛya kɛ, min ye su 3 000 kɛ.
A kura ɔkutɔburukalo san 2020 saratiwaati sabanan kama, Alasani Watara ye ɲɛfɛjɔ di Loran Bagibo ka seginni la tile damadɔ a ka labili kɔfɛ.
SUN : FRANCE 24 - Perezidan Habibu Sisoko ka lagosibagaw seginna ka jɔyɔrɔ la jumadon ka tɛmɛ Senegali kunnafonidisɛbɛn dɔ fɛ, « Liberason », min y’a kɔrɔ dɔ kan, min bisigilen don « waritɔ dogolen » la ( Habibu tɛ se k’a yɛrɛ bɔ ɲɛmisɛnni na, tuma bɛɛ, a tun bɛ fɔ k’a yɛrɛ minɛ, siga t’a la ko nin magotɛ kelen tun bɛ a la, mɔgɔw bɛna kuma ale fɔ cogo wɛrɛ la, k’a kɛ cogo wɛrɛ la ko sisan ).
K’a kɛ sɛgɛsɛgɛliw ye, kojugu don jamana nafolokow kunnafoniɲiniw ɲɛnabɔli celulantɔn (Sentifu) ka laselisɛbɛn ( an bɛna min fɔ a waati bɛɛ la ).
Ani fana kɔnɔko kan ani kɔnɔko kan, ko ye filɛli ko ye ka perezidan Habibu Sisoko bɔ.
Munna?
Nka, ɲininka mɔgɔw fɛ, minnu tɛ fɛ ka nin fasodenɲɔgɔn cɛɲi nɔgɔyali ye farikoloɲɛnajɛ kɔnɔ ani olɛnpikisi la kɛnɛkan ye.
An t’a fɛ ka nɔ bila sɛgɛsɛgɛli bisigilen na min dayɛlɛla Dakaro ( Senegali ) la, nka an bɛ se ka da kɛnɛ kan kaban ko nin koɲɛ nana sɛbɛnfura kosɛbɛ k’a da a kan Habibu ka yɛlɛnni bɛ mɔgɔ ncininw jɔrɔtigiya tiɲɛnin kɔnɔ.
O mɔgɔ kelenw, minnu ma jɔnjɔn kɛ, minnu ye ko bɛɛ kɛ walasa k’a bɔ u dabolo kan Mali kɔnɔ, tiɲɛni ani ɲɛfɔli fɛ.
Sababu kologɛlɛyalen ni dalakuma ye, Habibu ma kɛ kɔfɛjɔ ye abada.
Hakililaw walima seereyaw tɛ k’a bɛn a jalakibagaw fɔ, hali n’u labɛnnen don ka bɔ dugukolow bɛɛ la yaasa k’a tɔgɔ bɔ, nka abada a ma sɔn k’a yɛrɛ dɔgɔya u ka fanga la.
A ye waati di k’a ka baara kɛ waati bɛɛ kɔ, k’a da a kan a dalen b’a la ko n’u b’a fɛ k’a da o la, o k’a da a kan yecogo t’u bolo walasa u ka yɛrɛ wuli nin jɔyɔrɔtigiya dakun na.
I n’a fɔ a y’a ka nin tilali kɛ a yɛrɛ, min bɛ hakilijigin kɛ ko « dɔgɔdaba de ye mɔgɔ min bɛ tɔw tiɲɛ.
Juguman tɛ mɔgɔ hɛrɛ sɔrɔ abada ».
Wa o mɔgɔ jɛlenbaw ninnu tɛ fɛn min dɔn, o ye ko Sinosimu perezidan ma ɲini abada k’a garijigɛ jagoya, hali n’a y’a sɔrɔ a ye nin tɛmɛsira kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen in na, min kɛra a dusukunjɛlen ye an’a ka ɲɛmɔgɔyaba ye.
An ka fɛn la, Habibu Sisoko ani Hamani angi ka kanu tɛ k’u yɛrɛ kɛ, nka Mali ni jamana wɛrɛw ka kan k’u wulikajɔ kɛ o kama.
Ani k’o kɛ, k’a da a kan nin farikoloɲɛnajɛ ɲɛmɔgɔba fila ye jamana lasigidenw ye, nka fana k’a da a kan an ka kun bɛɛ bɛ k’a miiri ko janfa ninnu bɛ ɲɛsin u ma kojugu.
I n’a fɔ ni jamana walima fanga dɔw ŋaniya ciyakɛyɔrɔ tun bɛ kɛ k’an ka jamana bɔli u dabolo kan fɛn wɛrɛ la min, fo yan, ye kunnafonidiminɛn ɲuman hakililatigɛ a ye, o tuma, i ko i ko ɲuman.
Anw ka jamanaw cɛkow ka kan ka bataki dɔ labɛn sɛbɛ la, k’a da a kan farikoloɲɛnajɛ jamanaw cɛkow nafaw tɛ dɔnnen ye mɔgɔ si la bi.
Jamanaw cɛkow bɛ ɲɛsin farikoloɲɛnajɛ cɛsirikow ma. O cogo la, kabini olɛnpikisima bangeli la ka taa san 19nan laban na, Kupɛrin Piyɛri ka hakilina kɔnɔ, politiki ani diɲɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛ jɔyɔrɔ ma dabila ka taa se.
O cogo de la, Nɛlisɔni Mandela ( zuluyekalo tile 8 san 1918 – desanburukalo tile 5 san 2013 ) y’a kɔkɔrɔdon Irigibi Diɲɛ Kupudimɔgɔ kan walasa k’a ka faraɲɔgɔnkan jɛɲɔgɔn politiki la, ka tilali kɛ a fankelenfɛjɔw fɛ, walasa k’a ka jamana « Farikoloɲɛnajɛ » kologɛlɛya.
« Farikoloɲɛnajɛ kɛra kibaruya ani dantigɛli fɛɛrɛ ye, o kɔrɔ ye fangafɛɛrɛ ye.
Farikoloɲɛnajɛlaw b’u yɛrɛ sɛmɛntiya, i n’a fɔ u ka jamana lasigidenw, tuma dɔw, minnu dɔnnen don ka tɛmɛ mɔgɔba wɛrɛ kan, ani fana dɔnnen don hali k’a kɛ u ka jamana ye.
Mɔgɔ bɛ miiri Usiyɛni Bɔliti la Jamaiki walima Novaki Jokowici la Sɛribi kama », diɲɛmɔgɔw ka karamɔgɔ dɔ y’o fɔ an ye kɔsa la.
O la, mɔgɔ b’a faamuya kosɛbɛ, munna, fanbaw bɛɛ bɛ kɛlɛli la bi, walasa ka « farikoloɲɛnajɛ jalatigɛli » fɛɛrɛw di u ma.
Ani k’o kɛ k’a da a kan « farikoloɲɛnajɛ ye diɲɛ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw kun ye, jamana minnu bɛ ɲɔgɔn kan y’u jɔyɔrɔ ta ».
A bɛ fɛ ka kɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛ jamana belebele ye, i n’a fɔ an ka ɲɛmɔgɔw y’a fɔ cogo min, a b’a bisigi k’a ka politiki, jamana ni jamana wɛrɛw, dɔnko ani kan na.
ani sɔrɔko fana.
Tariku fitini kama, i k’a dɔn ko farikoloɲɛnajɛ sɔrɔ bɛ jɔ, ni Erɔwari miliyari 600 ye, n’a bɛ ɲini ka 2% bɔ diɲɛ kɔnɔnfɛn kɔnɔn ( PEYIBE ) la.
Mali sen bɛ gɛlɛya caman na kabini a bɛ san bi fila bɔ, a ka nafa bɛɛ bɛɛ la k’a farikoloɲɛnajɛ jate kɛ lasigidenw ka fɛɛrɛ ye min bɛ se ka dɔ fara a ka jamanaw cɛ ɲanamaya kan an’a ka jamanaw cɛ ɲanamaya kan.
O b’a bisigi ko an ka kan ka Mali tɔgɔlamɔgɔ politiki kura yiriwali diɲɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛ cakɛdaw la, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la latigɛli jɔyɔrɔw la.
Juguman na, bi fɛn bɛɛ kɛra walasa an ka tɔgɔlamɔgɔw ka bɔ sigida dɔw la farati b’a la k’an ka dɔw ka da datuguli kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la.
Ani k’o kɛ kasɔrɔ an ka jamanaw cɛkow ka ko labɛn, i n’a fɔ a ka kan.
N’an y’a ŋaniya tiɲɛ na, ka kɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛ jamana belebele ye don dɔ la, an tɛ se ka to k’an kɔdon an fasodenɲɔgɔnw ma, minnu y’u kɛlɛ k’u ka Afiriki ani diɲɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛkɛyɔrɔw ka ɲɛmɔgɔya jɔnjɔn fara ɲɔgɔn kan, n’a kɛtɔla k’a fɔ u ka bonya an’u ka hɔrɔya ka tiɲɛ ni Maliden wɛrɛw ka jɛɲɔgɔnjɔn ye, ni dɔ farali kɛli tiɲɛli ye.
Mɔgɔ minnu bɛ nin cɛ dɔn ɲɛmɔgɔya bɛ min bolo ɲɛmɔgɔya kelen ani mɔgɔ belebele bɛ min na, ka Habibu Sisoko jalaki ni nafolokow ɲɛfɔli ye, o ye yɛlɛko ɲuman ye, k’a da a kan a bɛ ɲini ka farikoloɲɛnajɛ lasɔrɔ, fɔlɔ judo, o kɔfɛ olɛnpikisi, walasa ka farikoloɲɛnajɛlaw bilasira, minnu bɛ fan bɛɛ fɛ, u ka laɲiniw kɛ.
Nka, i ko a m’a dabila k’o kɛ kokura nin masurunnakɔrɔw ye, a y’a to Ala ma tuma bɛɛ, waati la.
O de tɛ kɔfɛjɔyɔrɔ juguman ye mɔgɔ min bɛ danaya sɛbɛn min na a ka jalaki tɛ.
O cogo la, m’a fɔ ko, « an bɛ se ka ko bɛɛ fɔ, ka ko bɛɛ kɛ.
Nka fɛn kelen ye tiɲɛ ye.
Waati ye tiɲɛ danbetigi bɛɛ la ɲuman ye ».
Alfali ( Kunnafonisun zuwɛnkalo tile 21 san 2021) K’a kun bɔ « U kɛra mun ye? » kunnafonidicakɛcogo kelen bɛ di ŋana bɛɛ ma.
Kabini a dilan, a y’i sɛbɛn nin hakilina na walasa ka bɔ cɛw ni musow ɲinɛ la, minnu ye kɛnɛ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen taamasiyɛn.
Nka an de ka de kɔrɔ ye ka ɲɔgɔn sɔrɔ u ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, dɔw bɛ baarasira ɲuman ni caman bɛ min na.
O de ye an ka dɔgɔkun ŋana, Usumani Jara, SEWOBE ntolatanna kɔrɔ, Bamakɔ disiriki Ligi ntolatan mɔgɔ kɔrɔ, Femafuti perezidan kɔrɔ, Afiriki Ntolatan Faraɲɔgɔnkankulu ntolatan kuluw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ labɛnni ɲɛmɔgɔya kɔrɔ mɔgɔ kɔrɔ, Femafuti perezidan danbetigi, douani ɲɛmɔgɔba kɔrɔ.
Kumasurun na.
A ka donjatesɛbɛnw bɛ di fo ka se hakɛ la fo ka a ka faseri kɛnɛ kan min ka kan k’i jagoya an na ni farati ye k’an ka kalanbaga tilenw nɔgɔya.
A bɔlen kɔ Femafuti ka ɲɛmɔgɔya la san 19922, a sɔnna tɔgɔ tɔgɔ la, ka bɔ farikoloɲɛnajɛ kɔnɔ ani farikoloɲɛnajɛ kɛli bɛɛ la.
An sera ka Femafuti perezidan kɔrɔ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn, Bubakari Jalo, a bɛ fɔ min ma kɛ SEWOBE kɔlɔsibaga kɔrɔ ye, n’a bɛ fɔ a ma ko SEPIPE Mayɛri.
Ba Usumani y’an bisimila a ka gafe la, bangebɔ ka so dɔlakelen na Bamakɔkura.
Usumani Jara lakodɔnnen don ntolatan kɔnɔ, k’a da a kan a y’a to mɔgɔ caman ka don an ka jamana kɔnɔ, Afiriki ani diɲɛ kɔnɔ.
Bi a bɛ mɔgɔw ni ɲanamaya fɛn min dɔn, a ka kan ni ntolatan ye.
K’a to a ka farikoloɲɛnajɛ baaraw ɲɛmɔgɔya kɔnɔ, a ka baara baaraw n’a ta bɛɛ foroba cakɛdaw kɔnɔ, o y’a to ntolatan bɛ se ka kɛ ni tileni ye, foyi si tɛ se ka tiɲɛ.
O n’a ta bɛɛ, Usumani Jara ka nege belebelew bɔra miirinataabaliyaw fɛ, ɲangata bɛ min na ani kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la farikoloɲɛnajɛ bɛ se ka min sɔrɔ.
Ale ka fɔ la, kuluw ani kuluw hakilila bɛ daminɛ, ka farikoloɲɛnajɛ kɛ a ka waati hadamadenyasira kɛnɛko ye, min tɛ dɔn ka tɛmɛ bɛɛ kan, i ko ntolatanna.
A kumaɲɔgɔnya Usumani Jara ye kɛ misali ye walasa k’a se k’a ɲɛcogoyaw lakodɔn.
Jamana cɛ ni taabolow ye min bɛ ban k’a ka jatew ɲɛnabɔ ni Tariku ye, hakililila belebele min ka jɔyɔrɔtigiya kosɛbɛ.
Usumani Jara sigila sɛtanburukalo tile 29 san 1946 Bamakɔ, k’a kɛ dogoyɔrɔbaw, minnu ɲɔgɔn ma ɲɔgɔn kan, n’a b’a ka hakɛw lakodɔnnen san 2008 desanburukalo tile 31 san, baarasira caman laban na, an bɛna fɔ min kan duguma.
Faaba dugu cɛmancɛ la, ntolatan, jagoya la, tun ye a ka farikoloɲanajɛ fɛn ye.
A taara Bamakɔ – Kura olɛnpikikaw farikoloɲɛnajɛ la, k’a o kɔfɛ ka Bamakɔ Olɛnpikiko Kulɔbu ( SEWOBE ) sɛgɛrɛ san 1962 – 1963 ntolanci tuma.
A tora san tan ni ntolatantɔn jalatigi ye.
O waati kelen na Usumani Jara ni Bamakɔkura ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu, Asiki Mohamɛdi, ka ntolan kuluw ye.
PEYƐNA, Pari dogoyɔrɔw ka farikoloɲɛnajɛ Kelenyatɔn,
Newɛliyikaw ka Tɔn ani Moti Sanga Kulɔbu ka Tɔn,
San 1973 kɔnɔ, a y’a ka ntolatan sɛgɛnnafiyɛnbɔ ta, k’a da a kan a ka mara waati baara tun t’a to a ka waati yɛrɛ-yɛrɛ sɔrɔ ka degelikaramɔgɔya kɛ.
K’a bɔ Moti la, a bilala Bamakɔ san 1976 la, wa waati min sugandira SEWOBE ɲɛmɔgɔw fɛ, u ka ko bɛɛ bila sen kan walasa k’a bila faaba Ligi la.
O cogo de la Usumani Jara ye sɛbɛnikɛlaba dankan jɔyɔrɔ min bɛ sɛrɛkɛlaba la.
Ceba Kulibali, Adama Tarawore, Bakari Dɔsolo Tarawore, Jibirili Mayiga.
1978 feburukalo tile 28 kow ye Femafuti ka kɛli n’a ka baaraw bila ɲɛfɛ.
Farikoloɲɛnajɛw baaradaba, min ɲɛmɔgɔya tun bɛ Mɛtiri Aaliyɔni Bulɔndin Beye bolo, ye Bamakɔ Ligi waatilabaarakɛjɛkulu dɔ sigi sen kan, yɔrɔ min na Usumani Jara bɛ wariko zenerali jɔyɔrɔ la ani Femafuti jamana waatilabaarakɛjɛkulu dɔ, min kɔnɔ a bɛ kɛ fɛɛrɛtigiya baarakɛjɛkulu an’a ka denmisɛnw perezidan ye.
San min bɛ da o kan, nin ntolatan cakɛdaw kɛcogoya bɛ kɛ Ligi kunna, ani federason biro perezidanya dankan, Kolonɛli Sɛki Jara kɔfɛ.
Tuma min o laban weleyala ka taa jɔyɔrɔ wɛrɛw la san 1986, Usumani Jara ye Mali ntolatan ɲɛnabɔli daga ta san naani kɔnɔ ( san 1988 – 1992 ).
ininkali caman tun bɛ an jɔyɔrɔw don yaasa k’a ka ciw koɲɛnabɔ.
Pondason. Nk’a ma sɔn ka nin dafiri dayɛlɛ, yaasa an k’i dogo a la, n’a kɛtɔlen bɛɛ k’an lasɔn k’an dɔn ɲininkali dɔw dɔn.
A ka taama kelen Federason na, min, an ka kunnafoniw ka fɔ la, tun bɛ ɲini ka kɛ kɔntigiya sariya ye, fana ma kɛ sababu ye ka dantigɛli dɔw kɛ.
Ni farikoloɲɛnajɛw minisiriw danfaralenw ye, Usumani Jara sen don kalanw la, ntolatan baaraw ɲɛnabɔli kɛcogoya kuntaala la Mali kɔnɔ, farikoloɲɛnajɛ kan yɛlɛmali farikoloɲɛnajɛ kan, farikoloɲɛnajɛ baaraw nafoloko gɛlɛyaw n’a ta bɛɛ, farikoloɲɛnajɛ baaraw nafolobɔli kama Jamana baarataabolo fɛ, farikoloɲɛnajɛ yɛlɛmali farikoloɲɛnajɛ fɛ, walasa a waleyali ka se ka kɛ ni hakilimaya ye.
Farikoloɲɛnajɛw baaradaba ani Federason cɛ kokɛtaw tun ye?
Jamana kuluw ka jɔnjɔnw tun bɛ ɲɛnabɔ cogo di?
Federason tun bɛ kumakan jumɛn kɛ walasa ka ntolatannaw jateminɛ ni wari hakɛ caman ye?
« Federason bɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛw minisiriso la.
Min ye ntolatan ɲɛnabɔli jɔyɔrɔtigiya sɔrɔ, o tɛna se ka sira sɔrɔ a fan fila ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
Jɛɲɔgɔnya tun don simanfɛjɔyɔrɔ la, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, a cɛɲɔgɔnya tun ka caya.
Jamanakuntigi tun gɛlɛya la ka jɔnjɔnw san.
Foyi labɛnnen tun tɛ, ɲɛmɔgɔw fana tun bɛ k’u ka baaraw kɛ.
Kumakan kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen foyi si tun tɛ ntolatannaw bolo, Federason tun bɛ di a ka fɛɛrɛw labato, k’a to baarakɛsari dɔ ka bila minisiriso la ».
A bolonɔbilala Jamana kalanso la san 1953, a ye bakurubajate bɔ san 1967 walasa ka segin Jamana Mara Sɔrɔ ( EYƐNA ) la.
A ye baara bila ɔkutɔburukalo tile 15 san 1971, k’a kɛ dogoyɔrɔw filɛlikɛla ye.
O la, a ka mara baarasira gɛlɛn ani nafa daminɛna ni degelikaramɔgɔ fɔlɔ ye Faransi Jatebulonw Kalanyɔrɔ la san 1973.
Yanni a ka sonyali kɛ nin kalan kama, a tun bɛ brigadaɲɛmɔgɔya jɔyɔrɔ la Falade.
A seginnen na, a bɛ fɔ ka kɛ Moti marabolo dogoyɔrɔw ɲɛmɔgɔ ye, k’a kɔfɛ ka wulikajɔw lanɔgɔ.
Bamakɔ-Sɛnu biro ɲɛmɔgɔ, duw sɛgɛsɛgɛliw biro ɲɛmɔgɔ, sɔrɔko fɛnw biro ɲɛmɔgɔ, sariya ani baarabɛnkan biro ɲɛmɔgɔ, lakana sɔrɔlenw biro ɲɛmɔgɔ, kɔkankɛli biro ɲɛmɔgɔ, duw cakɛdaw ka sɛgɛsɛgɛli biro ɲɛmɔgɔ, duw ɲɛmɔgɔba dankan ani ɲɛmɔgɔba, san 1991.
San 1991 marisikalo tile 26 jɛkuluw kɔfɛ, Usumani Jara bilala ka kɛ fɛɛrɛtigi kɔnsɛbɛnnen ye sɔrɔ, nafolokow ani jago minisiriso la, san kelen o kɔfɛ a bɛ jɔyɔrɔ kelenw kɛ sɔrɔ ani boloda minisiriso la.
San 1994, a sigira k’a kɛ sɔrɔko kɔlɔsilikɛjɛkulu kɔnɔsilikɛjɛkulu n’a labɛnni mɔgɔ ye.
O fɛɛrɛ baara kɛlen kɔfɛ, a bɛ segin ka na douanw ɲɛmɔgɔba la, k’a kɛ ɲɛmɔgɔ ka ladilikɛla ye, fo ka taa a ka san 2008 sɛgɛnnafiyɛnbɔ la.
Hakilijakabɔlen Usumani Jara ye kalo damadɔ basigi kɛ, walasa k’a ka kalanw biro sigi, min ka baara ye degelikalan ani baarakɛɲɔgɔnya koɲɛnabɔliw jɔli ye.
Federason perezidan kɔrɔ ye furu kɛ ani den duuru fa don, ni denmisɛn caman ye.
Diɲɛnatigɛ la, a bɛ ntolatan fɛ, mɔgɔw ni ɲɔgɔ cɛ.
Kumasurun na, an hakili b’a la ko Femafuti perezidan kɔrɔ, Usumani Jara, tɔgɔ bɛ ye Mali ntolatan sanfɛjɔyɔrɔw la ni kupu fɔlɔ ye marabolo kɔnɔ min taara Samatasɛgɛw fɛ san 1989, Kani denmisɛn finali min tilenna Samatasɛgɛw fɛ san 1988, diɲɛ kupu min tanna Arabi Saudita la.
O. Oroze - Telefɔni ( 00223 ) 63 88 24 23.
Bɛnkansɛbɛn kɔlɔsilikɛjɛkulu ( SEYƐSIYA ) y’a ka laadalatɔnsigi 43nan kɛ, zuwɛnkalo tile 29, san 2021, Bamakɔ.
Nin ɲɔgɔnye laɲini tun ye ka sinsin fɛn kan min waleyala bɛnkansɛbɛn bilali la sen kan ani ko ka kan ka sennateliya bɛnkansɛbɛn bilali la sen kan.
Nin waatilabaara ye Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ, Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Sogɛli Kokala Mayiga, SEYƐSIYA perezidan, Bulem Sɛbihi, Alizeri ka lasigiden Mali la, Diɲɛtɔnba Sekeretɛri zenerali tɔgɔlamɔgɔ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen, El-Gasimi Wane, MINISIMA ɛmɔgɔ ( Diɲɛtɔnba ka caman sen bɛ min na basigili kama Mali la ) yeli kɛrɛfɛ.
